--- ARQUIVO: accompaniments.test.ts ---
import { describe, it, expect } from 'vitest';

describe('AccompanimentSelector Logic', () => {
  it('should calculate total extra price correctly', () => {
    const options = [
      { id: 1, group_id: 1, label: 'Arroz Branco', price_extra: 0 },
      { id: 2, group_id: 1, label: 'Arroz Integral', price_extra: 0 },
      { id: 3, group_id: 2, label: 'Brócolis', price_extra: 2.5 },
      { id: 4, group_id: 2, label: 'Cenoura', price_extra: 1.5 },
    ];

    // Test case 1: No extra price
    let selections = { 1: 1, 2: 0 };
    let totalExtra = 0;
    Object.entries(selections).forEach(([groupId, optionId]) => {
      const option = options.find((opt) => opt.id === optionId);
      if (option) totalExtra += option.price_extra;
    });
    expect(totalExtra).toBe(0);

    // Test case 2: With extra price
    selections = { 1: 1, 2: 3 };
    totalExtra = 0;
    Object.entries(selections).forEach(([groupId, optionId]) => {
      const option = options.find((opt) => opt.id === optionId);
      if (option) totalExtra += option.price_extra;
    });
    expect(totalExtra).toBe(2.5);

    // Test case 3: Multiple extra prices
    selections = { 1: 2, 2: 3 };
    totalExtra = 0;
    Object.entries(selections).forEach(([groupId, optionId]) => {
      const option = options.find((opt) => opt.id === optionId);
      if (option) totalExtra += option.price_extra;
    });
    expect(totalExtra).toBe(2.5);
  });

  it('should validate required accompaniments', () => {
    const groups = [
      { id: 1, name: 'Acompanhamento 100g', is_required: true },
      { id: 2, name: 'Acompanhamento 80g', is_required: false },
    ];

    // Test case 1: Missing required accompaniment
    let selections = { 2: 1 };
    let isValid = groups
      .filter((g) => g.is_required)
      .every((group) => selections[group.id]);
    expect(isValid).toBe(false);

    // Test case 2: All required accompaniments selected
    selections = { 1: 1, 2: 0 };
    isValid = groups
      .filter((g) => g.is_required)
      .every((group) => selections[group.id]);
    expect(isValid).toBe(true);
  });

  it('should handle multiple accompaniment selections', () => {
    const options = [
      { id: 1, group_id: 1, label: 'Frango', price_extra: 0 },
      { id: 2, group_id: 1, label: 'Peixe', price_extra: 5 },
      { id: 3, group_id: 2, label: 'Arroz Branco', price_extra: 0 },
      { id: 4, group_id: 2, label: 'Batata Doce', price_extra: 2 },
      { id: 5, group_id: 3, label: 'Sem Molho', price_extra: 0 },
      { id: 6, group_id: 3, label: 'Molho Branco', price_extra: 1.5 },
    ];

    // Test case: Multiple selections with various prices
    const selections = { 1: 2, 2: 4, 3: 6 };
    let totalExtra = 0;
    Object.entries(selections).forEach(([groupId, optionId]) => {
      const option = options.find((opt) => opt.id === optionId);
      if (option) totalExtra += option.price_extra;
    });
    expect(totalExtra).toBe(8.5); // 5 + 2 + 1.5
  });
});


--- ARQUIVO: admin-dishes.ts ---
import { and, asc, count, eq, like } from "drizzle-orm"; 
import { getDb } from "./db.js"; 
import { 
  dishes, 
  categories, 
  dishSizes, 
  sizeAccompanimentGroups, 
  accompanimentGroups, 
  accompanimentOptions 
} from "../drizzle/schema.js"; 

// ===================================================================
// TIPOS E HELPERS
// ===================================================================

export type AdminDish = {
    id: number;
    name: string;
    price: number; 
    categoryId: number; 
    isActive: boolean;
    categoryName?: string | null;
    description?: string | null;
    imageUrl?: string | null;
    slug?: string;
    nutritionalInfo?: string | null; 
    accompanimentGroups?: any[]; 
    sizes?: any[];
};

function mapDishRowToAdmin(row: any): AdminDish {
  return {
    ...row,
    id: Number(row.id),
    price: Number(row.price || 0),
    categoryId: Number(row.categoryId),
    isActive: Boolean(row.isActive),
    categoryName: row.categoryName ?? "Sem Categoria",
    description: row.description ?? null,
    imageUrl: row.imageUrl ?? null,
    nutritionalInfo: row.nutritionalInfo || row.nutritional_info || null,
  };
}

/** * Garante que o preço seja uma string decimal (ex: "10.00") para o MariaDB 
 */
function toPriceString(price: number | string): string {
    const num = typeof price === "string" ? parseFloat(price.replace(',', '.')) : price;
    return isNaN(num) ? "0.00" : num.toFixed(2);
}

function generateSlug(name: string): string {
    const cleanName = name.toLowerCase()
        .normalize("NFD").replace(/[\u0300-\u036f]/g, "") 
        .replace(/[^\w\s-]/g, '') 
        .replace(/\s+/g, '-');    
    return `${cleanName}-${Date.now()}`; 
}

// ===================================================================
// BUSCA E PAGINAÇÃO
// ===================================================================

export async function getPaginatedDishes(params: any) {
    const db = await getDb();
    const page = params.page > 0 ? params.page : 1;
    const perPage = params.limit > 0 ? params.limit : 8; 
    const offset = (page - 1) * perPage;
    
    const conditions = [];
    if (params.search?.trim()) conditions.push(like(dishes.name, `%${params.search.trim()}%`));
    if (params.categoryId) conditions.push(eq(dishes.categoryId, params.categoryId));
    if (typeof params.isActive === "boolean") conditions.push(eq(dishes.isActive, params.isActive));

    const whereExpr = conditions.length ? and(...conditions) : undefined;

    const totalResult = await db.select({ value: count() }).from(dishes).where(whereExpr);
    const totalItems = Number(totalResult[0]?.value ?? 0);

    const rows = await db
        .select({
            id: dishes.id,
            name: dishes.name,
            price: dishes.price, 
            categoryId: dishes.categoryId,
            isActive: dishes.isActive,
            description: dishes.description,
            imageUrl: dishes.imageUrl,
            slug: dishes.slug,
            nutritionalInfo: dishes.nutritionalInfo, 
            categoryName: categories.name,
        })
        .from(dishes)
        .leftJoin(categories, eq(dishes.categoryId, categories.id))
        .where(whereExpr)
        .orderBy(asc(dishes.name))
        .limit(perPage)
        .offset(offset);

    return {
        data: rows.map(mapDishRowToAdmin),
        total: totalItems,
        meta: {
            page,
            perPage,
            totalItems,
            pageCount: Math.ceil(totalItems / perPage) || 1,
        },
    };
}

// ===================================================================
// OPERAÇÕES C.R.U.D.
// ===================================================================

export async function createDish(data: any) {
  const db = await getDb();
  const nutritionalInfo = data.nutritionalInfo || data.nutritional_info;
  const nutritionalInfoString = nutritionalInfo 
    ? (typeof nutritionalInfo === 'string' ? nutritionalInfo : JSON.stringify(nutritionalInfo))
    : null;

  const [result]: any = await db.insert(dishes).values({
    name: data.name,
    slug: generateSlug(data.name),
    description: data.description ?? null,
    price: toPriceString(data.price), 
    categoryId: Number(data.categoryId),
    isActive: data.isActive ?? true,
    imageUrl: data.imageUrl ?? null,
    nutritionalInfo: nutritionalInfoString,
  });
  return { success: true, id: result.insertId };
}

export async function updateDish(id: number, data: any) {
  const db = await getDb();
  const updateData: any = { ...data };
  
  if (data.price !== undefined) updateData.price = toPriceString(data.price);
  
  // Normalização de Nutritional Info
  const nutritionalInfo = data.nutritionalInfo || data.nutritional_info;
  if (nutritionalInfo !== undefined) {
      updateData.nutritionalInfo = typeof nutritionalInfo === 'string' 
        ? nutritionalInfo 
        : JSON.stringify(nutritionalInfo);
  }

  // Proteção: Remove campos que o Drizzle não deve tentar atualizar diretamente
  delete updateData.id;
  delete updateData.nutritional_info;
  delete updateData.categoryName; 

  await db.update(dishes).set(updateData).where(eq(dishes.id, id));
  return { success: true };
}

/**
 * ✅ TOGGLE STATUS (Otimizado)
 * Atualiza apenas o campo necessário para evitar erros de validação Zod no router.
 */
export async function toggleDishStatus(id: number, isActive: boolean) {
  const db = await getDb();
  // Usamos Number(isActive) pois no banco é TINYINT
  await db.update(dishes)
    .set({ isActive: isActive }) 
    .where(eq(dishes.id, id));
  return { success: true };
}

/**
 * ✅ HARD DELETE
 */
export async function deleteDish(id: number) {
  const db = await getDb();
  try {
    await db.delete(dishes).where(eq(dishes.id, id));
    return { success: true };
  } catch (error: any) {
    // Tratamento específico para erro de integridade referencial
    if (error.errno === 1451 || error.code === 'ER_ROW_IS_REFERENCED_2') {
      throw new Error(
        "Este prato possui histórico de vendas e não pode ser excluído. " +
        "Use o Switch para ocultá-lo do cardápio."
      );
    }
    throw error;
  }
}

// ===================================================================
// RELAÇÕES (TAMANHOS E ACOMPANHAMENTOS)
// ===================================================================

export async function getDishById(id: number) {
  const db = await getDb();
  const [dishData] = await db.select({ 
      dish: dishes, 
      categoryName: categories.name 
  }).from(dishes)
    .leftJoin(categories, eq(dishes.categoryId, categories.id))
    .where(eq(dishes.id, id))
    .limit(1);

  if (!dishData) return null;

  const sizes = await db.select()
    .from(dishSizes)
    .where(eq(dishSizes.isActive, true))
    .orderBy(asc(dishSizes.displayOrder));
  
  const sizesWithAccompaniments = await Promise.all(sizes.map(async (size) => {
    const groupLinks = await db.select({ 
        group: accompanimentGroups, 
        isRequired: sizeAccompanimentGroups.isRequired 
    }).from(sizeAccompanimentGroups)
    .innerJoin(accompanimentGroups, eq(sizeAccompanimentGroups.accompanimentGroupId, accompanimentGroups.id))
    .where(eq(sizeAccompanimentGroups.sizeId, size.id));

    const groupsWithOptions = await Promise.all(groupLinks.map(async (link) => {
      const options = await db.select()
        .from(accompanimentOptions)
        .where(eq(accompanimentOptions.groupId, link.group.id))
        .orderBy(asc(accompanimentOptions.displayOrder));

      return { 
          ...link.group, 
          id: Number(link.group.id), 
          isRequired: Boolean(link.isRequired), 
          options: options.map(opt => ({ 
            ...opt, 
            id: Number(opt.id), 
            priceModifier: Number(opt.priceModifier || 0) 
          })) 
      };
    }));
    return { 
      ...size, 
      id: Number(size.id), 
      priceModifier: Number(size.priceModifier || 0), 
      accompanimentGroups: groupsWithOptions 
    };
  }));

  return { 
    ...dishData.dish, 
    id: Number(dishData.dish.id), 
    price: Number(dishData.dish.price || 0), 
    categoryName: dishData.categoryName || "Sem categoria", 
    sizes: sizesWithAccompaniments 
  };
}

export async function getLocalCategories() {
  const db = await getDb();
  return db.select().from(categories).orderBy(asc(categories.name));
}

--- ARQUIVO: admin-loyalty.ts ---
import { eq, desc, like, or, count, and, sql } from "drizzle-orm";
import { getDb } from "./db.js"; 
import { loyaltySettings, users, loyaltyHistory, orders } from "../drizzle/schema/index.js";

// =================================================================
// CRUD DE CONFIGURAÇÕES
// =================================================================

export async function getLoyaltyConfigs() {
    const db = await getDb();
    if (!db) throw new Error("Database not available"); 
    
    let settings = await db.select().from(loyaltySettings).limit(1);
    
    if (settings.length === 0) {
        await db.insert(loyaltySettings).values({
            enabled: true,
            conversionRatePoints: 1,
            conversionRateMoney: "1.00",
            redemptionRatePoints: 100,
            redemptionRateMoney: "1.00",
            maxDiscountAmount: "50.00",
            minCartAmount: "0.00", 
            pointsExpirationDays: 365,
            pointsPerSignup: 100,
            pointsPerReview: 10,
        });
        settings = await db.select().from(loyaltySettings).limit(1);
    }
    
    const config = settings[0];
    return {
        ...config,
        enabled: Boolean(config.enabled),
        conversionRateMoney: Number(config.conversionRateMoney),
        redemptionRateMoney: Number(config.redemptionRateMoney),
        maxDiscountAmount: Number(config.maxDiscountAmount),
        minCartAmount: Number(config.minCartAmount),
    };
}

export async function updateLoyaltyConfigs(data: any) {
    const db = await getDb();
    if (!db) throw new Error("Database not available");

    const updateData: any = {};
    if (data.enabled !== undefined) updateData.enabled = data.enabled;
    if (data.conversionRatePoints !== undefined) updateData.conversionRatePoints = Number(data.conversionRatePoints);
    if (data.conversionRateMoney !== undefined) updateData.conversionRateMoney = data.conversionRateMoney.toString();
    if (data.redemptionRatePoints !== undefined) updateData.redemptionRatePoints = Number(data.redemptionRatePoints);
    if (data.redemptionRateMoney !== undefined) updateData.redemptionRateMoney = data.redemptionRateMoney.toString();
    if (data.maxDiscountAmount !== undefined) updateData.maxDiscountAmount = data.maxDiscountAmount.toString();
    if (data.minCartAmount !== undefined) updateData.minCartAmount = data.minCartAmount.toString();
    if (data.pointsExpirationDays !== undefined) updateData.pointsExpirationDays = Number(data.pointsExpirationDays);
    if (data.pointsPerSignup !== undefined) updateData.pointsPerSignup = Number(data.pointsPerSignup);
    if (data.pointsPerReview !== undefined) updateData.pointsPerReview = Number(data.pointsPerReview);

    await db.update(loyaltySettings)
        .set({ ...updateData, updated_at: new Date() })
        .where(eq(loyaltySettings.id, 1)); 
        
    return { success: true };
}

// =================================================================
// RELATÓRIOS E LISTAGEM
// =================================================================

export async function getCustomersLoyalty(params: {
    page: number;
    limit: number;
    search?: string | null;
}) {
    const db = await getDb();
    if (!db) throw new Error("Database not available");

    const offset = (params.page - 1) * params.limit;
    const conditions = [];

    // Removido filtro de role para exibir todos os usuários cadastrados
    if (params.search && params.search !== "undefined" && params.search.trim() !== "") {
        const term = `%${params.search}%`;
        conditions.push(or(like(users.name, term), like(users.email, term)));
    }

    const whereClause = conditions.length > 0 ? and(...conditions) : undefined;

    try {
        const pointsSubquery = db
            .select({
                userId: loyaltyHistory.userId,
                totalPoints: sql<number>`sum(${loyaltyHistory.pointsChange})`.as('total_points'),
            })
            .from(loyaltyHistory)
            .groupBy(loyaltyHistory.userId)
            .as('sq_points');

        const dataQuery = db
            .select({
                id: users.id,
                name: users.name,
                email: users.email,
                lastActivity: users.lastSignedIn,
                calculatedBalance: sql<number>`COALESCE(${pointsSubquery.totalPoints}, 0)`.as('calculatedBalance'),
                totalSpent: sql<number>`(
                    SELECT COALESCE(SUM(${orders.total}), 0) 
                    FROM ${orders} 
                    WHERE ${orders.userId} = ${users.id} AND ${orders.status} = 'completed'
                )`.as('spent_total'),
            })
            .from(users)
            .leftJoin(pointsSubquery, eq(users.id, pointsSubquery.userId))
            .where(whereClause)
            .orderBy(desc(sql`calculatedBalance`)) 
            .limit(params.limit)
            .offset(offset);

        const countQuery = db
            .select({ value: count() })
            .from(users)
            .where(whereClause);

        const [items, totalResult] = await Promise.all([dataQuery, countQuery]);

        return {
            items: items.map(item => ({
                id: item.id,
                name: item.name,
                email: item.email,
                lastActivity: item.lastActivity,
                points: Number(item.calculatedBalance),
                totalSpent: Number(item.totalSpent || 0),
            })),
            total: Number(totalResult[0]?.value || 0),
            totalPages: Math.ceil(Number(totalResult[0]?.value || 0) / params.limit),
        };
    } catch (err: any) {
        console.error("Erro ao listar fidelidade:", err);
        throw err;
    }
}

// Histórico individual (Extrato)
export async function getCustomerHistory(userId: number) {
    const db = await getDb();
    if (!db) throw new Error("Database not available");

    const history = await db.select()
        .from(loyaltyHistory)
        .where(eq(loyaltyHistory.userId, userId))
        .orderBy(desc(loyaltyHistory.createdAt));

    return history.map(item => ({
        id: item.id,
        userId: item.userId,
        reason: item.reason,
        description: item.description,
        createdAt: item.createdAt,
        points: item.pointsChange, 
        pointsChange: item.pointsChange 
    }));
}

// ✅ FUNÇÃO PARA INSERIR PONTOS MANUALMENTE (CORRIGIDA)
export async function addManualPoints(userId: number, points: number, reason: string) {
    const db = await getDb();
    if (!db) throw new Error("Banco de dados não disponível");

    const type = points > 0 ? 'earned' : 'burned';

    try {
        await db.insert(loyaltyHistory).values({
            userId: userId,
            pointsChange: points,
            type: type as any,
            reason: reason,
            description: reason,
            createdAt: new Date()
        });

        return { success: true };
    } catch (error) {
        console.error("Erro SQL ao inserir pontos:", error);
        throw new Error("Falha ao gravar no banco de dados.");
    }
}

--- ARQUIVO: admin-orders.ts ---
// server/admin-orders.ts
import { getDb } from "./db";
import {
  orders,
  orderItems,
  users,
  customerAddresses,
} from "../drizzle/schema";
import {
  and,
  desc,
  eq,
  gte,
  lte,
  or,
  like,
  count,
} from "drizzle-orm";

export type OrderStatus =
  | "pending"
  | "processing"
  | "shipped"
  | "delivered"
  | "cancelled";

export interface ListParams {
  page: number;
  limit: number;
  status?: OrderStatus | null;
  search?: string | null;
  dateFrom?: string | null;
  dateTo?: string | null;
  userId?: number;
}

// --- 1) LISTA DE PEDIDOS ---
export async function listOrders(params: ListParams) {
  const db = await getDb();
  if (!db) throw new Error("Database not available");

  const page = params.page ?? 1;
  const limit = params.limit ?? 20;
  const offset = (page - 1) * limit;

  const conditions: any[] = [];

  if (params.status) {
    conditions.push(eq(orders.status, params.status));
  }

  if (params.userId) {
    conditions.push(eq(orders.userId, params.userId));
  }

  if (params.search) {
    const term = `%${params.search.trim()}%`;
    conditions.push(
      or(
        like(users.email, term),
        like(users.name, term),
      ),
    );
  }

  if (params.dateFrom) {
    conditions.push(gte(orders.createdAt, new Date(params.dateFrom)));
  }

  if (params.dateTo) {
    const dateToEnd = new Date(params.dateTo);
    dateToEnd.setHours(23, 59, 59, 999);
    conditions.push(lte(orders.createdAt, dateToEnd));
  }

  const where = conditions.length === 0 ? undefined : and(...conditions);

  // Contagem Total
  const totalRes = await db
    .select({ totalCount: count() })
    .from(orders)
    .leftJoin(users, eq(orders.userId, users.id)) // Necessário para filtrar por nome no count
    .where(where);

  const total = Number(totalRes[0]?.totalCount ?? 0);

  // Busca de Dados
  const data = await db
    .select({
      id: orders.id,
      customerName: users.name,
      customerEmail: users.email,
      customerPhone: customerAddresses.phone,
      total: orders.total,
      paymentMethod: orders.paymentMethod,
      status: orders.status,
      createdAt: orders.createdAt,
    })
    .from(orders)
    .leftJoin(users, eq(orders.userId, users.id))
    .leftJoin(
      customerAddresses,
      and(
        eq(customerAddresses.userId, users.id),
        eq(customerAddresses.isDefault, true),
      ),
    )
    .where(where)
    .orderBy(desc(orders.createdAt))
    .limit(limit)
    .offset(offset);

  return {
    data,
    meta: {
      total,
      page,
      limit,
      pageCount: Math.ceil(total / limit),
    },
  };
}

// --- 2) DETALHES DO PEDIDO ---
export async function getOrderDetails(orderId: number) {
  const db = await getDb();
  if (!db) throw new Error("Database not available");

  const [orderRaw] = await db
    .select({
      id: orders.id,
      status: orders.status,
      total: orders.total,
      subtotal: orders.subtotal,
      shippingCost: orders.shippingCost,
      paymentMethod: orders.paymentMethod,
      createdAt: orders.createdAt,
      updated_at: orders.updated_at,
      userId: orders.userId,
      customerName: users.name,
      customerEmail: users.email,
      customerPhone: customerAddresses.phone,
      shippingAddress: orders.shippingAddress,
      shippingAddressNumber: orders.shippingAddressNumber,
      shippingAddressComplement: orders.shippingAddressComplement,
      shippingNeighborhood: orders.shippingNeighborhood,
      shippingCity: orders.shippingCity,
      shippingState: orders.shippingState,
      shippingZipCode: orders.shippingZipCode,
    })
    .from(orders)
    .leftJoin(users, eq(orders.userId, users.id))
    .leftJoin(
      customerAddresses,
      and(
        eq(customerAddresses.userId, users.id),
        eq(customerAddresses.isDefault, true),
      ),
    )
    .where(eq(orders.id, orderId))
    .limit(1);

  if (!orderRaw) throw new Error("Pedido não encontrado");

  const itemsRaw = await db
    .select()
    .from(orderItems)
    .where(eq(orderItems.orderId, orderId));

  // Tenta parsear os acompanhamentos de string para objeto para o frontend
  const items = itemsRaw.map(item => {
    let accs = [];
    try {
      accs = typeof item.accompanimentsSnapshot === 'string' 
        ? JSON.parse(item.accompanimentsSnapshot) 
        : item.accompanimentsSnapshot;
    } catch (e) {
      accs = [];
    }
    return { ...item, accompaniments: accs };
  });

  return { order: orderRaw, items };
}

// --- 3) ALIAS PARA O TRPC ---
// ✅ Importante: resolve o erro 500 pois o trpc chama getOrderById
export const getOrderById = getOrderDetails;

// --- 4) ATUALIZAR STATUS ---
export async function updateOrderStatus(orderId: number, status: string) {
  const db = await getDb();
  await db
    .update(orders)
    .set({
      status: status as OrderStatus,
      updated_at: new Date(),
    })
    .where(eq(orders.id, orderId));

  return { success: true };
}

// --- 5) DELETAR PEDIDO ---
export async function deleteOrder(orderId: number) {
  const db = await getDb();
  if (!db) throw new Error("Database not available");

  // O Drizzle deleta primeiro os itens se houver Cascade, 
  // mas é mais seguro deletar manualmente para evitar erros de Foreign Key
  await db.delete(orderItems).where(eq(orderItems.orderId, orderId));
  
  // Deleta o pedido principal
  return await db.delete(orders).where(eq(orders.id, orderId));
}

// server/admin-packages.ts

import { eq, inArray } from "drizzle-orm";
import { getDb } from "./db";
import { 
  packages, 
  packageOptions, 
  packageOptionDishes, 
  packageOptionGroups,
  accompanimentGroups,
  dishes,
} from "../drizzle/schema";

// -------------------------------------------------------------
// FUNÇÕES DE SERVIÇO DE PACOTES
// -------------------------------------------------------------

export async function getAllPackages() {
  const db = await getDb();
  if (!db) throw new Error("DB Off");
  return db.select().from(packages).orderBy(packages.createdAt);
}

export async function getPackageWithOptions(packageId: number) {
  const db = await getDb();
  if (!db) throw new Error("DB Off");

  const pkg = await db.select().from(packages).where(eq(packages.id, packageId)).limit(1);
  if (!pkg[0]) return null;

  const options = await db.select().from(packageOptions)
    .where(eq(packageOptions.packageId, packageId))
    .orderBy(packageOptions.optionOrder);

  const optionsWithDetails = await Promise.all(options.map(async (opt) => {
    // Pratos vinculados a esta opção específica do pacote
    const optDishes = await db.select({
        id: dishes.id,
        name: dishes.name
    })
    .from(packageOptionDishes)
    .innerJoin(dishes, eq(packageOptionDishes.dishId, dishes.id))
    .where(eq(packageOptionDishes.optionId, opt.id));

    // Grupos de acompanhamentos vinculados a esta opção
    const optGroups = await db.select({
        id: accompanimentGroups.id,
        name: accompanimentGroups.name
    })
    .from(packageOptionGroups)
    .innerJoin(accompanimentGroups, eq(packageOptionGroups.groupId, accompanimentGroups.id))
    .where(eq(packageOptionGroups.optionId, opt.id));

    return {
      ...opt,
      dishes: optDishes,
      accompanimentGroups: optGroups
    };
  }));

  return { ...pkg[0], options: optionsWithDetails };
}

export async function createFullPackage(data: {
  name: string;
  slug: string;
  description?: string;
  imageUrl?: string;
  basePrice: number;
  numberOfOptions: number;
  month?: string;
}) {
  const db = await getDb();
  if (!db) throw new Error("DB Off");

  // ✅ CORREÇÃO: No Drizzle com MySQL/Postgres, usamos .returning() ou o objeto de retorno direto
  const result = await db.insert(packages).values({
    name: data.name,
    slug: data.slug,
    description: data.description,
    imageUrl: data.imageUrl,
    price: data.basePrice.toString(), 
    numberOfOptions: data.numberOfOptions,
    month: data.month,
    isActive: true,
  });
  
  // Se for MySQL, o ID vem em insertId. Se for Postgres, use .returning({id: packages.id})
  const packageId = (result as any)[0]?.insertId || (result as any).insertId || (result as any)[0]?.id;

  return { success: true, packageId };
}

export async function updatePackage(id: number, data: any) {
  const db = await getDb();
  if (!db) throw new Error("DB Off");

  await db.update(packages).set({
    ...data,
    price: data.basePrice ? data.basePrice.toString() : undefined,
    updated_at: new Date(),
  }).where(eq(packages.id, id));
  
  return { success: true };
}

export async function deletePackage(id: number) {
  const db = await getDb();
  if (!db) throw new Error("DB Off");
  return db.delete(packages).where(eq(packages.id, id));
}

// -------------------------------------------------------------

export async function createPackageOption(data: { packageId: number, name: string, optionOrder?: number }) {
  const db = await getDb();
  await db.insert(packageOptions).values({
    packageId: data.packageId,
    name: data.name,
    optionOrder: data.optionOrder || 0
  });
  return { success: true };
}

export async function addDishesToOption(optionId: number, dishIds: number[]) {
  const db = await getDb();
  // 1. Limpa o que já existe para esta opção (Sync)
  await db.delete(packageOptionDishes).where(eq(packageOptionDishes.optionId, optionId));

  // 2. Insere os novos pratos selecionados
  if (dishIds.length > 0) {
    const values = dishIds.map(id => ({
        optionId: optionId,
        dishId: id
    }));
    await db.insert(packageOptionDishes).values(values);
  }
  return { success: true };
}

export async function addGroupsToOption(optionId: number, groupIds: number[]) {
  const db = await getDb();
  // 1. Limpa os grupos antigos
  await db.delete(packageOptionGroups).where(eq(packageOptionGroups.optionId, optionId));

  // 2. Insere os novos
  if (groupIds.length > 0) {
    const values = groupIds.map(id => ({
        optionId: optionId,
        groupId: id
    }));
    await db.insert(packageOptionGroups).values(values);
  }
  return { success: true };
}

/**
 * Esta função é usada se você tiver uma tabela simples de ligação DIRETA 
 * entre pacote e pratos, sem passar pelas "Options".
 */
export async function updatePackageDishes(packageId: number, dishIds: number[]) {
  const db = await getDb();
  // ✅ CORREÇÃO: Certifique-se que o nome da tabela no schema é packageOptionDishes 
  // ou se você tem uma tabela específica chamada package_dishes (importar corretamente)
  await db.delete(packageOptionDishes).where(eq(packageOptionDishes.optionId, packageId)); // Exemplo
  
  if (dishIds.length > 0) {
    const values = dishIds.map(dishId => ({
      optionId: packageId, // Ou packageId dependendo da sua tabela
      dishId
    }));
    await db.insert(packageOptionDishes).values(values);
  }
}

--- ARQUIVO: admin-payment-methods.ts ---
import { eq, desc, asc, and } from "drizzle-orm";
import { getDb } from "./db";
import { 
    paymentMethods, 
    foodCardBrands, 
    orders 
} from "../drizzle/schema"; 
import { z } from "zod";

// Tipos base (assumindo que estes tipos são exportados pelo seu schema, o que corrigimos)
export type PaymentMethod = typeof paymentMethods.$inferSelect;
export type InsertPaymentMethod = typeof paymentMethods.$inferInsert;
export type FoodCardBrand = typeof foodCardBrands.$inferSelect;
export type InsertFoodCardBrand = typeof foodCardBrands.$inferInsert;

// =========================================================================

        .select()
        .from(paymentMethods)

    const methodData = {
        ...data,
        // Converte o valor do minAmount para string (decimal no DB)
        minAmount: data.minAmount.toString(), 
    };

    const [newMethod] = await db.insert(paymentMethods).values(methodData as any);
    
    return newMethod;
}

/**
 * Atualiza um método de pagamento existente.
 */

    const db = await getDb();
    if (!db) throw new Error("Database not available");
    
    const updateData: any = { ...data };

        updateData.minAmount = updateData.minAmount.toString();

    await db.update(paymentMethods).set(updateData).where(eq(paymentMethods.id, id));
    
    return { success: true };
}

    return { success: true };
}

--- ARQUIVO: admin-reports.ts ---
import { eq, desc, like, or, sql, and, gte, lte, count, sum } from "drizzle-orm";
import { getDb } from "./db";
// ✅ CORREÇÃO: Importa orderItems (camelCase) diretamente
import { orders, orderItems, dishes, users, user_profiles } from "../drizzle/schema"; 
import { ENV } from "./_core/env";
import { date, z } from "zod";

// Tipos base para o status de pedidos (deve coincidir com o schema)
type OrderStatus = "pending" | "processing" | "shipped" | "delivered" | "cancelled";

// =========================================================================
// 1. RELATÓRIOS GERAIS DE VENDAS
// =========================================================================

export async function getDashboardSummary(timeframe: "day" | "week" | "month") {
  const db = await getDb();
  if (!db) throw new Error("Database not available");

  let startDate: Date;
  const endDate = new Date();

  switch (timeframe) {
    case "day":
      startDate = new Date(endDate);
      startDate.setDate(endDate.getDate() - 1);
      break;
    case "week":
      startDate = new Date(endDate);
      startDate.setDate(endDate.getDate() - 7);
      break;
    case "month":
      startDate = new Date(endDate);
      startDate.setMonth(endDate.getMonth() - 1);
      break;
    default:
      throw new Error("Timeframe inválido.");
  }

  // Filtro de tempo básico
  const timeFilter = and(
    // ✅ CORREÇÃO DE COLUNA: created_at -> createdAt
    gte(orders.createdAt, startDate), 
    lte(orders.createdAt, endDate)
  );

  // 1. Total de Receita (apenas pedidos concluídos/entregues)
  const [revenueResult] = await db
    .select({
      // ✅ CORREÇÃO DE COLUNA: total_price -> totalPrice
      revenue: sql<string>`SUM(${orders.total})`,
      count: count(orders.id),
    })
    .from(orders)
    .where(
      and(
        timeFilter,
        or(
          eq(orders.status, "delivered"),
          eq(orders.status, "completed")
        )
      )
    );

  // 2. Análise de Vendas por Dia (Gráfico)
  const salesByDay = await db
    .select({
      // ✅ CORREÇÃO DE COLUNA: created_at -> createdAt
      date: sql<string>`DATE(${orders.createdAt})`, 
      sales: sql<string>`SUM(${orders.total})`,
    })
    .from(orders)
    .where(timeFilter)
    // ✅ CORREÇÃO DE COLUNA: created_at -> createdAt
    .groupBy(sql`DATE(${orders.createdAt})`) 
    .orderBy(sql`DATE(${orders.createdAt})`); 

  // 3. Produtos mais Vendidos
  const topProducts = await db
    .select({
      name: dishes.name,
      quantity: sql<number>`SUM(${orderItems.quantity})`,
    })
    .from(orderItems) // ✅ orderItems (camelCase)
    // ✅ CORREÇÃO DE COLUNA: dish_id -> dishId
    .innerJoin(dishes, eq(orderItems.dishId, dishes.id)) 
    .innerJoin(orders, eq(orderItems.orderId, orders.id))
    .where(timeFilter) // Filtra pelo tempo
    .groupBy(dishes.name)
    .orderBy(sql`SUM(${orderItems.quantity}) DESC`)
    .limit(5);

  return {
    totalRevenue: revenueResult.revenue || "0.00",
    totalOrders: revenueResult.count,
    salesByDay,
    topProducts,
  };
}

// =========================================================================
// 2. RELATÓRIOS DE DETALHE
// =========================================================================

export async function getPaymentMethodReport(startDate: Date, endDate: Date) {
  const db = await getDb();
  if (!db) throw new Error("Database not available");

  const timeFilter = and(
    // ✅ CORREÇÃO DE COLUNA: created_at -> createdAt
    gte(orders.createdAt, startDate), 
    lte(orders.createdAt, endDate)
  );

  const results = await db
    .select({
      // ✅ CORREÇÃO DE COLUNA: payment_method -> paymentMethod
      paymentMethod: orders.paymentMethod, 
      totalRevenue: sql<string>`SUM(${orders.total})`,
      totalOrders: count(orders.id),
    })
    .from(orders)
    .where(timeFilter)
    // ✅ CORREÇÃO DE COLUNA: payment_method -> paymentMethod
    .groupBy(orders.paymentMethod) 
    .orderBy(desc(sql`SUM(${orders.total})`));

  return results.map(row => ({
    paymentMethod: row.paymentMethod, // Mapeamento final
    totalRevenue: row.totalRevenue,
    totalOrders: row.totalOrders,
  }));
}

export async function getCustomerAcquisitionReport(startDate: Date, endDate: Date) {
  const db = await getDb();
  if (!db) throw new Error("Database not available");

  const timeFilter = and(
    // ✅ CORREÇÃO DE COLUNA: created_at -> createdAt
    gte(orders.createdAt, startDate), 
    lte(orders.createdAt, endDate)
  );
  
  const [result] = await db
    .select({
      // ✅ CORREÇÃO DE COLUNA: user_id -> userId
      totalCustomers: sql<number>`COUNT(DISTINCT ${orders.userId})`, 
      totalRevenue: sql<string>`SUM(${orders.total})`,
    })
    .from(orders)
    .where(timeFilter);

  return {
    totalCustomers: result.totalCustomers || 0,
    totalRevenue: result.totalRevenue || "0.00",
  };
}

export async function getOrderSummary(orderId: number) {
    const db = await getDb();
    if (!db) throw new Error("Database not available");

    const order = await db
        .select()
        .from(orders)
        .where(eq(orders.id, orderId));

    if (!order.length) return null;

    const items = await db
        .select()
        .from(orderItems) // ✅ orderItems (camelCase)
        .where(eq(orderItems.orderId, orderId));

    return {
        order: order[0],
        items,
    };
}

--- ARQUIVO: admin-settings.ts ---
import { eq } from "drizzle-orm";
import { getDb } from "./db";
import { storeSettings } from "../drizzle/schema";

export async function getStoreSettings() {
  const db = await getDb();
  if (!db) throw new Error("Database not available");
  
  const settings = await db.select().from(storeSettings).limit(1);
  
  if (settings.length === 0) {
    // Cria padrão se não existir (fallback de segurança)
    await db.insert(storeSettings).values({
      generalMinOrderAmount: "0.00",
    });
    return (await db.select().from(storeSettings).limit(1))[0];
  }
  
  return settings[0];
}

export async function updateStoreSettings(data: {
  generalMinOrderAmount?: string;
  minOrderMessage?: string | null;
}) {
  const db = await getDb();
  if (!db) throw new Error("Database not available");

  // Garante que existe registro 1
  const existing = await getStoreSettings();
  
  await db.update(storeSettings).set({
    generalMinOrderAmount: data.generalMinOrderAmount,
    minOrderMessage: data.minOrderMessage,
    updated_at: new Date(),
  }).where(eq(storeSettings.id, existing.id));

  return { success: true };
}

--- ARQUIVO: admin-sizes-accompaniments.ts ---
import { asc, eq, sql, and } from "drizzle-orm"; 
import { getDb } from "./db.js";

import {
  dishSizes,
  accompanimentGroups,
  accompanimentOptions,
  dishes,
  categories,
} from "../drizzle/schema/index.js";

import type { InferSelectModel } from "drizzle-orm";

// ===================================================================
// TIPOS E HELPERS
// ===================================================================
export type DishSizeRow = InferSelectModel<typeof dishSizes>;

function toPriceString(price: number | string | undefined | null): string {
  if (price === undefined || price === null) return "0.00";
  // Trata números com vírgula vindo do administrador
  const num = typeof price === "string" ? parseFloat(price.replace(',', '.')) : price;
  return isNaN(num) ? "0.00" : num.toFixed(2);
}

function generateSlug(name: string): string {
  const cleanName = name.toLowerCase()
    .normalize("NFD").replace(/[\u0300-\u036f]/g, "") // Remove acentos
    .replace(/[^\w\s-]/g, '') 
    .replace(/\s+/g, '-');    
  return `${cleanName}-${Date.now()}`; 
}

// ===================================================================
// 1) DISH SIZES (TAMANHOS)
// ===================================================================

export async function getAllDishSizes() {
  const db = await getDb();
  if (!db) throw new Error("Database not available");
  
  const result = await db.select().from(dishSizes).orderBy(asc(dishSizes.displayOrder));
  
  return result.map(size => ({
    ...size,
    id: Number(size.id),
    priceModifier: Number(size.priceModifier || 0),
    isActive: Boolean(size.isActive)
  }));
}

export async function getSizeById(id: number) {
  const db = await getDb();
  if (!db) throw new Error("Database not available");
  
  const rows = await db.select().from(dishSizes).where(eq(dishSizes.id, id)).limit(1);
  if (!rows[0]) return null;
  
  return {
    ...rows[0],
    id: Number(rows[0].id),
    priceModifier: Number(rows[0].priceModifier || 0),
    isActive: Boolean(rows[0].isActive)
  };
}

export async function createDishSize(data: any) {
  const db = await getDb();
  if (!db) throw new Error("Database not available");

  const [result]: any = await db.insert(dishSizes).values({
    name: data.name,
    weight: data.weight ?? null,
    priceModifier: toPriceString(data.priceModifier),
    noAccompanimentsMessage: data.noAccompanimentsMessage ?? null,
    displayOrder: Number(data.displayOrder ?? 0),
    isActive: data.isActive ?? true,
  });

  return { success: true, id: result.insertId };
}

export async function updateDishSize(id: number, data: any) {
  const db = await getDb();
  if (!db) throw new Error("Database not available");

  const { id: _, ...updateData } = data;

  if (data.priceModifier !== undefined) updateData.priceModifier = toPriceString(data.priceModifier);
  if (data.displayOrder !== undefined) updateData.displayOrder = Number(data.displayOrder);
  
  await db.update(dishSizes).set(updateData).where(eq(dishSizes.id, id));
  return { success: true };
}

export async function deleteDishSize(id: number) {
  const db = await getDb();
  if (!db) throw new Error("Database not available");

  // Remove vínculos primeiro via SQL direto para evitar erros de FK
  await db.execute(sql`DELETE FROM size_accompaniment_groups WHERE size_id = ${id}`);
  await db.delete(dishSizes).where(eq(dishSizes.id, id));
  return { success: true };
}

// ===================================================================
// 4) LÓGICA DE VÍNCULOS (SINCRONIZADA COM ROTEADORES)
// ===================================================================

/**
 * Retorna os vínculos mapeados exatamente como o useAdminSizes.ts espera
 */
export async function getSizeAccompanimentGroupsWithOptions() {
  const db = await getDb();
  if (!db) return [];
  
  // Usamos SQL puro para garantir performance e nomes de colunas corretos no MariaDB
  const [rows]: any = await db.execute(sql`
    SELECT size_id as sizeId, accompaniment_group_id as groupId 
    FROM size_accompaniment_groups
  `);
  
  return Array.isArray(rows) ? rows : [];
}

/**
 * LÓGICA DE VÍNCULO: linkAccompanimentToSize
 * (Substitui o linkGroupToSize anterior)
 */
export const linkAccompanimentToSize = async (data: { sizeId: number; groupId: number }) => {
    const db = await getDb();
    if (!db) throw new Error("Database not available");

    const sId = Number(data.sizeId);
    const gId = Number(data.groupId);

    // 1. DELETE preventivo para evitar duplicidade de PK no banco
    await db.execute(sql`
        DELETE FROM size_accompaniment_groups 
        WHERE size_id = ${sId} AND accompaniment_group_id = ${gId}
    `);

    // 2. INSERT do novo vínculo
    await db.execute(sql`
        INSERT INTO size_accompaniment_groups (size_id, accompaniment_group_id, is_required)
        VALUES (${sId}, ${gId}, 0)
    `);

    return { success: true };
};

/**
 * LÓGICA DE DESVÍNCULO: unlinkAccompanimentFromSize
 * (Substitui o unlinkGroupFromSize anterior)
 */
export const unlinkAccompanimentFromSize = async (sizeId: number, groupId: number) => {
    const db = await getDb();
    if (!db) throw new Error("Database not available");

    return await db.execute(sql`
        DELETE FROM size_accompaniment_groups 
        WHERE size_id = ${Number(sizeId)} AND accompaniment_group_id = ${Number(groupId)}
    `);
};

  const db = await getDb();

  return row ?? null;
}

  const db = await getDb();
  return db.select().from(categories).orderBy(asc(categories.name));
}

--- ARQUIVO: admin-users.ts ---
// server/admin-users.ts

import { and, desc, eq, like, or, sql } from "drizzle-orm";
import { getDb } from "./db";
import { users, user_profiles, orders } from "../drizzle/schema";
import { encrypt, decrypt } from "./encryption";
import { TRPCError } from "@trpc/server";
// se já tiver o import do AuthPassword em outra parte, mantém o seu.
// import { AuthPassword } from "./auth-password"; 

// Helper: faz decrypt aceitando Buffer OU string, com fallback seguro
function safeDecrypt(value: unknown): string | null {
  if (!value) return null;

  try {
    const decrypted = Buffer.isBuffer(value)
      ? decrypt(value) // se sua função já lida com Buffer
      : decrypt(String(value));

    return decrypted || null;
  } catch {
    return null;
  }
}

// ========================================================================\
// 1. LISTAGEM PRINCIPAL (Admin -> Usuários)
// ========================================================================\

export async function getUsersPaginated(params: {
  page: number;
  limit: number;
  search?: string;
}) {
  const db = await getDb();
  if (!db) throw new Error("Database not available");

  const { page, limit, search } = params;
  const offset = (page - 1) * limit;

  const conditions: any[] = [];
  const searchTerm = search?.trim();

  // Busca por nome / email (texto puro)
  if (searchTerm) {
    conditions.push(
      or(
        like(users.name, `%${searchTerm}%`),
        like(users.email, `%${searchTerm}%`)
        // se quiser buscar por documento, daria pra fazer um LIKE em cima do
        // campo criptografado, mas normalmente não compensa.
      )
    );
  }

  const whereClause = conditions.length > 0 ? and(...conditions) : undefined;

  // Query principal de dados
  const dataQuery = db
    .select({
      id: users.id,
      openId: users.openId,
      name: users.name,
      email: users.email,
      role: users.role,
      loginMethod: users.loginMethod,
      createdAt: users.createdAt,
      updated_at: users.updated_at,
      lastSignedIn: users.lastSignedIn,

      // 👇 DUAS FONTES POSSÍVEIS DE DOCUMENTO:
      customerDocumentProfile: user_profiles.customerDocument, // BLOB (migração nova / edição)
      customerDocumentUser: users.customerDocument, // VARCHAR (migração antiga)
    })
    .from(users)
    .leftJoin(user_profiles, eq(users.id, user_profiles.userId))
    .where(whereClause)
    .limit(limit)
    .offset(offset)
    .orderBy(desc(users.createdAt));

  // Query de contagem
  const countQuery = db
    .select({ count: sql<number>`count(*)` })
    .from(users)
    .leftJoin(user_profiles, eq(users.id, user_profiles.userId))
    .where(whereClause);

  const [items, totalResult] = await Promise.all([dataQuery, countQuery]);
  const total = Number(totalResult[0]?.count ?? 0);

  // ✅ CORREÇÃO: Descriptografa documento, priorizando profile -> users
  const usersWithDecrypted = items.map((row) => {
    const encryptedDoc =
      row.customerDocumentProfile ?? row.customerDocumentUser;

    const decryptedDoc = safeDecrypt(encryptedDoc);

    return {
      id: row.id,
      openId: row.openId,
      name: row.name,
      email: row.email,
      role: row.role,
      loginMethod: row.loginMethod,
      createdAt: row.createdAt,
      updated_at: row.updated_at,
      lastSignedIn: row.lastSignedIn,
      customerDocument: decryptedDoc, // é isso que o front usa
    };
  });

  return {
    users: usersWithDecrypted,
    pagination: {
      page,
      limit,
      total,
      totalPages: Math.ceil(total / limit),
    },
  };
}

// ========================================================================\
// 2. DETALHES DO USUÁRIO (Modal de Edição / Visualização)
// ========================================================================\

export async function getUserDetails(userId: number) {
  const db = await getDb();
  if (!db) throw new Error("Database not available");

  // Dados básicos
  const baseUserRows = await db
    .select()
    .from(users)
    .where(eq(users.id, userId))
    .limit(1);

  if (!baseUserRows.length) {
    throw new Error("Usuário não encontrado");
  }

  const baseUser = baseUserRows[0];

  // Perfil
  const [profile] = await db
    .select()
    .from(user_profiles)
    .where(eq(user_profiles.userId, userId))
    .limit(1);

  // Documento pode estar no profile OU direto em users (migração antiga)
  const encryptedProfileDoc = profile?.customerDocument ?? null;
  const encryptedUserDoc = (baseUser as any).customerDocument ?? null;

  const decryptedDocument =
    safeDecrypt(encryptedProfileDoc) ?? safeDecrypt(encryptedUserDoc);

  const decryptedProfile = profile
    ? {
        ...profile,
        // ✅ CORREÇÃO: Decrypt para todos os campos
        phone: profile.phone ? safeDecrypt(profile.phone) : null,
        address: profile.address ? safeDecrypt(profile.address) : null,
        city: profile.city ? safeDecrypt(profile.city) : null,
        state: profile.state ? safeDecrypt(profile.state) : null,
        zipCode: profile.zipCode ? safeDecrypt(profile.zipCode) : null,
        customerDocument: decryptedDocument,
      }
    : {
        // mesmo sem registro em user_profiles, ainda devolvemos algo
        userId,
        phone: null,
        address: null,
        city: null,
        state: null,
        zipCode: null,
        customerDocument: decryptedDocument,
        loyaltyPoints: 0,
        totalSpent: "0.00",
      };

  // Histórico de pedidos (mantido)
  const userOrders = await db
    .select()
    .from(orders)
    .where(eq(orders.userId, userId))
    .orderBy(desc(orders.createdAt));

  return {
    user: baseUser,
    profile: decryptedProfile,
    orders: userOrders,
  };
}

// ========================================================================\
// 3. ATUALIZAÇÃO DO PERFIL (Criptografando na gravação)
// ========================================================================\

export async function updateUserProfile(
  userId: number,
  data: {
    name?: string;
    phone?: string;
    address?: string;
    city?: string;
    state?: string;
    zipCode?: string;
    customerDocument?: string;
  }
) {
  const db = await getDb();
  if (!db) throw new Error("Database not available");

  // 1. Atualiza nome em users
  if (data.name) {
    await db
      .update(users)
      .set({ name: data.name, updated_at: new Date() })
      .where(eq(users.id, userId));
  }

  // 2. Monta dados de perfil com criptografia
  const profileData: any = {
    // Criptografa string para string (VARCHAR/TEXT)
    phone: data.phone ? encrypt(data.phone) : undefined,
    address: data.address ? encrypt(data.address) : undefined,
    city: data.city ? encrypt(data.city) : undefined,
    state: data.state ? encrypt(data.state) : undefined,
    zipCode: data.zipCode ? encrypt(data.zipCode) : undefined,

    // ✅ CRIPTOGRAFIA PARA BLOB: Encripta e CONVERTE PARA BUFFER
    customerDocument: data.customerDocument
      ? Buffer.from(encrypt(data.customerDocument.trim()) || "")
      : undefined,

    updated_at: new Date(),
  };

  // Remove undefined (Drizzle não curte campos undefined)
  Object.keys(profileData).forEach((key) => {
    if (profileData[key] === undefined) {
      delete profileData[key];
    }
  });

  // Verifica se já existe perfil
  const existingProfile = await db
    .select()
    .from(user_profiles)
    .where(eq(user_profiles.userId, userId))
    .limit(1);

  if (existingProfile.length > 0) {
    await db
      .update(user_profiles)
      .set(profileData)
      .where(eq(user_profiles.userId, userId));
  } else {
    // Insere novo perfil (inclui valores default para campos NOT NULL)
    await db.insert(user_profiles).values({
      userId,
      ...profileData,
      loyaltyPoints: 0,
      totalSpent: "0.00",
    });
  }

  return { success: true };
}

export async function updateUserRole(
  userId: number,
  newRole: "admin" | "user"
) {

  if (!db) throw new Error("Database not available");

    .update(users)
    .set({ role: newRole, updated_at: new Date() })
    .where(eq(users.id, userId));
}

}) {

    page: input.page,
    limit: input.perPage,
    search: input.search,
  });
}

// ========================================================================\
// 6. CRIAÇÃO DE USUÁRIO PELO ADMIN
// ========================================================================\

export async function createUserWithProfile(input: {
  name: string;
  email: string;
  password: string;
  role?: "admin" | "user";
  customerDocument?: string | null;
}) {
  const db = await getDb();
  if (!db) throw new Error("Database not available");

  const role = input.role ?? "user";

  // 1) Cria usuário com senha (usa o mesmo helper de senha da auth)
  const hashedPassword = await AuthPassword.hashPassword(input.password);

  const [inserted] = await db
    .insert(users)
    .values({
      email: input.email,
      name: input.name,
      role,
      password: hashedPassword,
      loginMethod: "password",
      createdAt: new Date(),
      updated_at: new Date(),
    })
    .$returningId();

  const userId = (inserted as any).id ?? inserted;

  // 2) Cria perfil com documento criptografado (se informado)
  if (input.customerDocument && input.customerDocument.trim()) {
    const encryptedDoc = Buffer.from(
      encrypt(input.customerDocument.trim()) || ""
    );

    await db.insert(user_profiles).values({
      userId,
      customerDocument: encryptedDoc,
      loyaltyPoints: 0,
      totalSpent: "0.00",
      createdAt: new Date(),
      updated_at: new Date(),
    });
  }

  return { id: userId };
}

type AuthenticatedUser = NonNullable<TrpcContext["user"]>;

function createAdminContext(): TrpcContext {
  const user: AuthenticatedUser = {
    id: 1,
    openId: "admin-user",
    email: "admin@example.com",
    name: "Admin User",
    loginMethod: "manus",
    role: "admin",
    createdAt: new Date(),
    updated_at: new Date(),
    lastSignedIn: new Date(),
  };

  const ctx: TrpcContext = {
    user,
    req: {
      protocol: "https",
      headers: {},
    } as TrpcContext["req"],
    res: {
      clearCookie: () => {},
    } as TrpcContext["res"],
  };

  return ctx;
}

  const user: AuthenticatedUser = {
    id: 2,
    openId: "regular-user",
    email: "user@example.com",
    name: "Regular User",
    loginMethod: "manus",
    role: "user",
    createdAt: new Date(),

  const ctx: TrpcContext = {
    user,
    req: {
      protocol: "https",
      headers: {},
    } as TrpcContext["req"],
    res: {
      clearCookie: () => {},
    } as TrpcContext["res"],
  };

  return ctx;
}

    });
