--- ARQUIVO: auth-password.test.ts ---
import { describe, it, expect, beforeEach } from "vitest";
import { hashPassword, verifyPassword } from "./auth-password";

describe("Password Authentication", () => {
  describe("hashPassword", () => {
    it("deve gerar hash diferente para mesma senha", async () => {
      const password = "minha_senha_123";
      const hash1 = await hashPassword(password);
      const hash2 = await hashPassword(password);

      expect(hash1).not.toBe(hash2);
    });

    it("deve retornar string com formato salt:hash", async () => {
      const password = "senha_teste";
      const hash = await hashPassword(password);

      const parts = hash.split(":");
      expect(parts).toHaveLength(2);
      expect(parts[0]).toBeTruthy(); // salt
      expect(parts[1]).toBeTruthy(); // hash
    });
  });

  describe("verifyPassword", () => {
    let hashedPassword: string;
    const testPassword = "senha_correta_123";

    beforeEach(async () => {
      hashedPassword = await hashPassword(testPassword);
    });

    it("deve validar senha correta", async () => {
      const isValid = await verifyPassword(testPassword, hashedPassword);
      expect(isValid).toBe(true);
    });

    it("deve rejeitar senha incorreta", async () => {
      const isValid = await verifyPassword("senha_errada", hashedPassword);
      expect(isValid).toBe(false);
    });

    it("deve rejeitar hash inválido", async () => {
      const isValid = await verifyPassword(testPassword, "invalid:hash");
      expect(isValid).toBe(false);
    });

    it("deve rejeitar hash sem separador", async () => {
      const isValid = await verifyPassword(testPassword, "invalidsalt");
      expect(isValid).toBe(false);
    });
  });

  describe("Segurança", () => {
    it("hash deve ser diferente cada vez (salt aleatório)", async () => {
      const password = "senha_teste_seguranca";
      const hashes = await Promise.all([
        hashPassword(password),
        hashPassword(password),
        hashPassword(password),
      ]);

      // Todos devem ser diferentes
      expect(hashes[0]).not.toBe(hashes[1]);
      expect(hashes[1]).not.toBe(hashes[2]);
      expect(hashes[0]).not.toBe(hashes[2]);
    });

    it("hash deve ter comprimento mínimo", async () => {
      const password = "a";
      const hash = await hashPassword(password);
      expect(hash.length).toBeGreaterThan(100); // salt:hash é bem longo
    });
  });
});


--- ARQUIVO: auth-password.ts ---
import { eq } from "drizzle-orm";
import { getDb } from "./db.js";
import { users } from "./../drizzle/schema.js";
import bcrypt from "bcryptjs";
import { v4 as uuidv4 } from "uuid"; 

export async function createUserWithPassword(email: string, passwordPlain: string, name?: string) {
  const db = await getDb();
  const hashedPassword = await bcrypt.hash(passwordPlain, 10);

  const newUser = {
    email,
    password: hashedPassword,
    name: name || email.split('@')[0],
    role: "user",
    openId: uuidv4(), // ✅ Isso evita o erro 500 no banco
  };

  await db.insert(users).values(newUser);
  return await db.query.users.findFirst({ where: eq(users.email, email) });
}

export async function getFirstAdmin() {
  const db = await getDb();
  return await db.query.users.findFirst({
    where: eq(users.role, "admin"),
  });
}

--- ARQUIVO: auth.logout.test.ts ---
import { describe, expect, it } from "vitest";
import { appRouter } from "./routers";
import { COOKIE_NAME } from "../shared/const";
import type { TrpcContext } from "./_core/context";

type CookieCall = {
  name: string;
  options: Record<string, unknown>;
};

type AuthenticatedUser = NonNullable<TrpcContext["user"]>;

function createAuthContext(): { ctx: TrpcContext; clearedCookies: CookieCall[] } {
  const clearedCookies: CookieCall[] = [];

  const user: AuthenticatedUser = {
    id: 1,
    openId: "sample-user",
    email: "sample@example.com",
    name: "Sample User",
    loginMethod: "manus",
    role: "user",
    createdAt: new Date(),
    updated_at: new Date(),
    lastSignedIn: new Date(),
  };

  const ctx: TrpcContext = {
    user,
    req: {
      protocol: "https",
      headers: {},
    } as TrpcContext["req"],
    res: {
      clearCookie: (name: string, options: Record<string, unknown>) => {
        clearedCookies.push({ name, options });
      },
    } as TrpcContext["res"],
  };

  return { ctx, clearedCookies };
}

describe("auth.logout", () => {
  it("clears the session cookie and reports success", async () => {
    const { ctx, clearedCookies } = createAuthContext();
    const caller = appRouter.createCaller(ctx);

    const result = await caller.auth.logout();

    expect(result).toEqual({ success: true });
    expect(clearedCookies).toHaveLength(1);
    expect(clearedCookies[0]?.name).toBe(COOKIE_NAME);
    expect(clearedCookies[0]?.options).toMatchObject({
      maxAge: -1,
      sameSite: "none",
      httpOnly: true,
      path: "/",
    });
  });
});


--- ARQUIVO: auth.ts ---
// ARQUIVO: server/auth.ts
import { Lucia } from "lucia";
import { DrizzleMySQLAdapter } from "@lucia-auth/adapter-drizzle"; // ✅ Mudou aqui
import { getDb } from "./../server/db"; // ✅ Ajustado caminho relativo
import { users } from "../drizzle/schema/users"; // ✅ Ajustado caminho relativosessions
import { sessions } from "../drizzle/schema/sessions";

const db = await getDb();

// Para MySQL, usamos o DrizzleMySQLAdapter
const adapter = new DrizzleMySQLAdapter(db, sessions, users);

export const lucia = new Lucia(adapter, {
  sessionCookie: {
    attributes: {
      secure: process.env.NODE_ENV === "production",
    },
  },
  getUserAttributes: (attributes) => {
    return {
      email: attributes.email,
      role: attributes.role,
      name: attributes.name,
    };
  },
});

declare module "lucia" {
  interface Register {
    Lucia: typeof lucia;
    DatabaseUserAttributes: DatabaseUserAttributes;
  }
}

interface DatabaseUserAttributes {
  email: string;
  role: string;
  name: string;
}

--- ARQUIVO: cart.test.ts ---
import { describe, expect, it, beforeEach, vi } from "vitest";
import {
  CartItemSchema,
  getOrCreateCart,
  addToCart,
  removeFromCart,
  updateCartItemQuantity,
  getCartItems,
  updateCartTotals,
  clearCart,
} from "./cart";
import { z } from "zod";

/**
 * Testes para funcionalidade de carrinho
 */
describe("Cart Operations", () => {
  const mockUserId = 1;

  describe("CartItemSchema validation", () => {
    it("should validate a valid cart item", () => {
      const validItem = {
        itemType: "dish" as const,
        dishId: 1,
        sizeId: 2,
        quantity: 1,
        accompaniments: [
          { optionId: 1, priceModifier: "2.50" },
        ],
      };

      const result = CartItemSchema.safeParse(validItem);
      expect(result.success).toBe(true);
    });

    it("should reject invalid item type", () => {
      const invalidItem = {
        itemType: "invalid",
        quantity: 1,
        accompaniments: [],
      };

      const result = CartItemSchema.safeParse(invalidItem);
      expect(result.success).toBe(false);
    });

    it("should reject quantity less than 1", () => {
      const invalidItem = {
        itemType: "dish" as const,
        dishId: 1,
        quantity: 0,
        accompaniments: [],
      };

      const result = CartItemSchema.safeParse(invalidItem);
      expect(result.success).toBe(false);
    });

    it("should set default quantity to 1", () => {
      const itemWithoutQuantity = {
        itemType: "package" as const,
        packageId: 1,
        accompaniments: [],
      };

      const result = CartItemSchema.safeParse(itemWithoutQuantity);
      expect(result.success).toBe(true);
      if (result.success) {
        expect(result.data.quantity).toBe(1);
      }
    });
  });

  describe("Cart price calculations", () => {
    it("should calculate total price with multiple items", () => {
      // Simular cálculo de preço
      const unitPrice = 25.50;
      const quantity = 2;
      const accompanimentExtra = 5.00;

      const totalPrice = (unitPrice + accompanimentExtra) * quantity;
      expect(totalPrice).toBe(61.00);
    });

    it("should handle zero accompaniment price modifier", () => {
      const unitPrice = 30.00;
      const quantity = 1;
      const accompaniments = [
        { optionId: 1, priceModifier: "0" },
      ];

      const accompanimentTotal = accompaniments.reduce((sum, acc) => {
        return sum + parseFloat(acc.priceModifier);
      }, 0);

      const totalPrice = unitPrice * quantity + accompanimentTotal * quantity;
      expect(totalPrice).toBe(30.00);
    });

    it("should calculate subtotal from multiple items", () => {
      const items = [
        { total_price: "50.00" },
        { total_price: "75.50" },
        { total_price: "25.00" },
      ];

      const subtotal = items.reduce((sum, item) => {
        return sum + parseFloat(item.total_price);
      }, 0);

      expect(subtotal).toBe(150.50);
    });
  });

  describe("Cart item operations", () => {
    it("should create a valid cart item with dish", () => {
      const item = {
        itemType: "dish" as const,
        dishId: 1,
        sizeId: 2,
        quantity: 2,
        accompaniments: [
          { optionId: 1, priceModifier: "3.00" },
          { optionId: 2, priceModifier: "2.50" },
        ],
      };

      const result = CartItemSchema.safeParse(item);
      expect(result.success).toBe(true);
      if (result.success) {
        expect(result.data.itemType).toBe("dish");
        expect(result.data.dishId).toBe(1);
        expect(result.data.accompaniments).toHaveLength(2);
      }
    });

    it("should create a valid cart item with package", () => {
      const item = {
        itemType: "package" as const,
        packageId: 1,
        quantity: 1,
        accompaniments: [],
      };

      const result = CartItemSchema.safeParse(item);
      expect(result.success).toBe(true);
      if (result.success) {
        expect(result.data.itemType).toBe("package");
        expect(result.data.packageId).toBe(1);
      }
    });

    it("should handle quantity updates", () => {
      const originalQuantity = 2;
      const newQuantity = 5;
      const unitPrice = 25.00;

      const originalTotal = originalQuantity * unitPrice;
      const newTotal = newQuantity * unitPrice;

      expect(originalTotal).toBe(50.00);
      expect(newTotal).toBe(125.00);
    });

    it("should validate accompaniment structure", () => {
      const accompaniments = [
        { optionId: 1, priceModifier: "5.00" },
        { optionId: 2, priceModifier: "3.50" },
      ];

      const isValid = accompaniments.every(
        (acc) => typeof acc.optionId === "number" && typeof acc.priceModifier === "string"
      );

      expect(isValid).toBe(true);
    });
  });

  describe("Cart state management", () => {
    it("should handle empty cart", () => {
      const items: any[] = [];
      const subtotal = items.reduce((sum, item) => {
        return sum + parseFloat(item.total_price);
      }, 0);

      expect(subtotal).toBe(0);
    });

    it("should preserve item order in cart", () => {
      const items = [
        { id: 1, dishId: 1 },
        { id: 2, dishId: 2 },
        { id: 3, dishId: 3 },
      ];

      expect(items[0].id).toBe(1);
      expect(items[1].id).toBe(2);
      expect(items[2].id).toBe(3);
    });

    it("should handle cart clearing", () => {
      let items = [
        { id: 1, quantity: 2 },
        { id: 2, quantity: 1 },
      ];

      items = [];

      expect(items.length).toBe(0);
    });
  });

  describe("Cart validation", () => {
    it("should validate minimum quantity", () => {
      const quantities = [0, 1, 5, 100];
      const validQuantities = quantities.filter((q) => q >= 1);

      expect(validQuantities).toEqual([1, 5, 100]);
    });

    it("should validate item type enum", () => {
      const validTypes = ["dish", "package"];
      const testTypes = ["dish", "package", "invalid"];

      const validTestTypes = testTypes.filter((t) => validTypes.includes(t));

      expect(validTestTypes).toEqual(["dish", "package"]);
    });

    it("should require either dishId or packageId", () => {
      const itemWithDish = { dishId: 1, packageId: undefined };
      const itemWithPackage = { dishId: undefined, packageId: 1 };
      const itemWithBoth = { dishId: 1, packageId: 1 };

      expect(itemWithDish.dishId || itemWithDish.packageId).toBeTruthy();
      expect(itemWithPackage.dishId || itemWithPackage.packageId).toBeTruthy();
      expect(itemWithBoth.dishId || itemWithBoth.packageId).toBeTruthy();
    });
  });
});


--- ARQUIVO: cart.ts ---
// server/cart.ts

import { eq, and, sum, sql, desc } from "drizzle-orm";
import { getDb } from "./db.js";
import { 
    orders, 
    orderItems,
    dishes 
} from "../drizzle/schema.js"; 
import { z } from "zod";
import { calculateLoyaltyPoints } from "./loyalty.js";

// =========================================================================
// SCHEMAS E TIPOS
// =========================================================================

const ItemAccompanimentSchema = z.object({
  id: z.number(),
  name: z.string(),
  groupId: z.number(),
  groupName: z.string(),
  priceModifier: z.string().or(z.number()), 
});

export const ItemDataSchema = z.object({
  quantity: z.number().min(1),
  basePrice: z.number(),
  finalPrice: z.number(),
  accompaniments: z.array(ItemAccompanimentSchema).optional().default([]),
  observation: z.string().optional().nullable(),
  itemType: z.enum(['dish', 'package']).default('dish'),

  dishId: z.number().optional().nullable(),
  dishName: z.string().optional().nullable(),
  sizeId: z.number().optional().nullable(),
  sizeName: z.string().optional().nullable(),

  packageId: z.number().optional().nullable(),
  packageName: z.string().optional().nullable(),
});

// =========================================================================
// 1. FUNÇÕES CORE (LEITURA E CRIAÇÃO)
// =========================================================================

export async function getOrCreateCart(userId: number) {
    const db = await getDb();
    // ✅ CORREÇÃO: Checa se db é undefined
    if (!db) throw new Error("Database not available");

    const [existingOrder] = await db
        .select()
        .from(orders)
        .where(and(eq(orders.userId, userId), eq(orders.status, "pending")))
        .limit(1);

    if (existingOrder) {
        const items = await db.select().from(orderItems).where(eq(orderItems.orderId, existingOrder.id));
        const subtotalValue = parseFloat(existingOrder.subtotal || "0.00");
        const loyaltyPointsEarned = await calculateLoyaltyPoints(subtotalValue, userId);

        return { 
            ...existingOrder, 
            items, 
            loyaltyPointsEarned 
        };
    }

    const [result] = await db.insert(orders).values({
        userId,
        status: "pending",
        subtotal: "0.00",
        total: "0.00",
        shippingCost: "0.00", 
        discount: "0.00",
        paymentMethod: "pending", 
        // shippingAddressId: null, 
        createdAt: new Date(),
        updated_at: new Date(),
    } as any);

    const cartId = result.insertId;
    const [createdCart] = await db.select().from(orders).where(eq(orders.id, cartId));
    
    return { 
        ...createdCart, 
        items: [],
        loyaltyPointsEarned: 0 
    };
}

// =========================================================================
// 2. MANIPULAÇÃO DE ITENS (LÓGICA HÍBRIDA: PRATO + PACOTE)
// =========================================================================

export async function addItemToCart(userId: number, itemData: any) {
    const db = await getDb();
    // ✅ CORREÇÃO: Checa se db é undefined
    if (!db) throw new Error("Database not available");
    
    let cart = await getOrCreateCart(userId); 
    const cartId = cart.id;
    
    // Validação flexível
    const validatedItem = ItemDataSchema.parse(itemData);

    const accompanimentsJson = JSON.stringify(
        (validatedItem.accompaniments || []).sort((a: any, b: any) => a.id - b.id)
    );

    let existingItem;

    if (validatedItem.itemType === 'package') {
        existingItem = cart.items?.find((item: any) => 
            item.packageId === validatedItem.packageId &&
            item.itemType === 'package'
        );
    } else {
        existingItem = cart.items?.find((item: any) => 
            item.dishId === validatedItem.dishId &&
            item.sizeId === validatedItem.sizeId &&
            (typeof item.accompanimentsSnapshot === 'string' 
                ? item.accompanimentsSnapshot 
                : JSON.stringify(item.accompanimentsSnapshot)
            ) === accompanimentsJson
        );
    }

    if (existingItem) {
        // ATUALIZAR
        const newQuantity = existingItem.quantity + validatedItem.quantity;
        const newFinalPrice = (validatedItem.basePrice * newQuantity).toFixed(2);

        await db.update(orderItems).set({
            quantity: newQuantity,
            finalPrice: newFinalPrice,
        }).where(eq(orderItems.id, existingItem.id));

    } else {
        // INSERIR
        await db.insert(orderItems).values({
            orderId: cartId,
            
            dishId: validatedItem.dishId || null,
            dishName: validatedItem.dishName || validatedItem.packageName,
            
            packageId: validatedItem.packageId || null,
            itemType: validatedItem.itemType || 'dish',
            
            sizeId: validatedItem.sizeId || null,
            sizeName: validatedItem.sizeName || null,
            
            quantity: validatedItem.quantity,
            basePrice: validatedItem.basePrice.toFixed(2), 
            finalPrice: validatedItem.finalPrice.toFixed(2), 
            
            accompanimentsSnapshot: validatedItem.accompaniments, 
            observation: validatedItem.observation || null,
        } as any); 
    }

    await recalculateCartTotals(cartId);
    return getOrCreateCart(userId);
}

/**
 * Remove um item do carrinho.
 */
export async function removeItemFromCart(userId: number, itemId: number) {
    const db = await getDb(); 
    // ✅ CORREÇÃO: Checa se db é undefined
    if (!db) throw new Error("Database not available");
    
    const cart = await getOrCreateCart(userId);

    await db.delete(orderItems).where(
        and(
            eq(orderItems.id, itemId),
            eq(orderItems.orderId, cart.id)
        )
    );

    await recalculateCartTotals(cart.id);
    return getOrCreateCart(userId);
}

/**
 * Atualiza a quantidade de um item.
 */
export async function updateItemQuantity(userId: number, itemId: number, newQuantity: number) {
    const db = await getDb(); 
    // ✅ CORREÇÃO: Checa se db é undefined
    if (!db) throw new Error("Database not available");
    
    const cart = await getOrCreateCart(userId);

    const [item] = await db.select().from(orderItems)
        .where(and(eq(orderItems.id, itemId), eq(orderItems.orderId, cart.id)));

    if (!item) throw new Error("Item not found");

    const unitPrice = parseFloat(item.basePrice);
    const newFinalPrice = (unitPrice * newQuantity).toFixed(2);

    await db.update(orderItems).set({
        quantity: newQuantity,
        finalPrice: newFinalPrice, 
    }).where(eq(orderItems.id, itemId));

    await recalculateCartTotals(cart.id);
    return getOrCreateCart(userId);
}

/**
 * Limpa o carrinho.
 */
export async function clearCart(userId: number) {
    const db = await getDb();
    // ✅ CORREÇÃO: Checa se db é undefined
    if (!db) throw new Error("Database not available");
    
    const cart = await getOrCreateCart(userId);

    await db.delete(orderItems).where(eq(orderItems.orderId, cart.id));
    
    await db.update(orders).set({
        subtotal: "0.00",
        total: "0.00",
        discount: "0.00",
        shippingCost: "0.00"
    }).where(eq(orders.id, cart.id));

    return getOrCreateCart(userId);
}

// =========================================================================
// 3. AUXILIARES E CÁLCULOS
// =========================================================================

export async function recalculateCartTotals(cartId: number) {
    const db = await getDb();
    // ✅ CORREÇÃO: Checa se db é undefined
    if (!db) throw new Error("Database not available");

    // Soma dos itens
    const [res] = await db
        .select({ 
            subtotal: sum(sql`CAST(${orderItems.finalPrice} AS DECIMAL(10,2))`) 
        })
        .from(orderItems)
        .where(eq(orderItems.orderId, cartId));

    const subtotal = Number(res?.subtotal || 0);

    const [order] = await db.select().from(orders).where(eq(orders.id, cartId));
    
    const shipping = Number(order.shippingCost || 0);
    const discount = Number(order.discount || 0);
    const total = subtotal + shipping - discount;

    await db.update(orders).set({
        subtotal: subtotal.toFixed(2),
        total: total.toFixed(2),
        updated_at: new Date(),
    }).where(eq(orders.id, cartId));
}

--- ARQUIVO: check-columns.ts ---
// server/check-columns.ts
import "dotenv/config";
import mysql from "mysql2/promise";

async function checkTables() {
  if (!process.env.DATABASE_URL) throw new Error("DATABASE_URL vazia");

  console.log("🔌 Conectando ao banco...");
  const connection = await mysql.createConnection(process.env.DATABASE_URL);

  const tablesToCheck = ["accompanimentGroups", "dishSizes"];

  for (const table of tablesToCheck) {
    console.log(`\n📋 ESTRUTURA DA TABELA: ${table}`);
    console.log("---------------------------------------------------");
    try {
      // O comando DESCRIBE lista as colunas, tipos e se aceita NULL
      const [rows] = await connection.query(`DESCRIBE \`${table}\``);
      console.table(rows);
    } catch (error: any) {
      console.error(`❌ Erro ao ler tabela ${table}:`, error.message);
    }
  }

  await connection.end();
  process.exit(0);
}

checkTables().catch(console.error);

--- ARQUIVO: coupon.ts ---
// server/coupon.ts

import { eq, and, sql, desc } from "drizzle-orm";
import { getDb } from "./db"; 
import { coupons, couponUsage, orders } from "../drizzle/schema"; 
import { z } from "zod";

// Tipos usados no painel/admin e no lado do cliente
export type CouponDiscountType = "percentage" | "fixed";

export interface CreateCouponInput {
  code: string;
  description?: string | null;
  discountType: CouponDiscountType;
  discount_value: number;
  minOrderValue?: number | null;
  maxDiscount?: number | null;
  usageLimit?: number | null;
  validFrom?: Date | null;
  validUntil?: Date | null;
  isActive?: boolean; // Adicionado para compatibilidade com o finance.ts
}

export interface UpdateCouponInput {
  description?: string | null;
  discountType?: CouponDiscountType;
  discount_value?: number;
  minOrderValue?: number | null;
  maxDiscount?: number | null;
  usageLimit?: number | null;
  validFrom?: Date | null;
  validUntil?: Date | null;
  isActive?: boolean;
}

export interface ValidateCouponResult {
  isValid: boolean;
  message?: string;
  discountAmount: number;
  coupon_id?: number;
  code?: string;
}

function toNumber(value: unknown): number {
  if (value == null) return 0;
  const num = Number(value);
  return Number.isNaN(num) ? 0 : num;
}

// =========================================================================
// 1. VALIDAÇÃO E APLICAÇÃO
// =========================================================================

/**
 * Valida um cupom para um determinado usuário e subtotal.
 */
export async function validateCoupon(
  code: string,
  userId: number,
  subtotal: number
): Promise<ValidateCouponResult> {
  const now = new Date();
  
  const db = await getDb();
  if (!db) throw new Error("Database not available");

  // Buscar cupom pelo código
  const couponResult = await db
    .select()
    .from(coupons)
    .where(eq(coupons.code, code.toUpperCase()))
    .limit(1);

  if (!couponResult[0]) {
    return { isValid: false, message: "Cupom não encontrado", discountAmount: 0 };
  }

  const coupon = couponResult[0];

  if (!coupon.isActive) {
    return { isValid: false, message: "Cupom inativo", discountAmount: 0 };
  }

  if (coupon.validFrom && new Date(coupon.validFrom) > now) {
    return { isValid: false, message: "Cupom ainda não está válido", discountAmount: 0 };
  }
  if (coupon.validUntil && new Date(coupon.validUntil) < now) {
    return { isValid: false, message: "Cupom expirado", discountAmount: 0 };
  }
  
  if (coupon.minOrderValue && subtotal < toNumber(coupon.minOrderValue)) {
    return { isValid: false, message: `Valor mínimo de R$${coupon.minOrderValue} requerido.`, discountAmount: 0 };
  }

  // Verificar limite de uso geral
  if (coupon.usageLimit) {
    const usageCount = await db.select({ count: sql<number>`count(*)` }).from(couponUsage).where(eq(couponUsage.coupon_id, coupon.id));
    if (Number(usageCount[0].count) >= coupon.usageLimit) {
      return { isValid: false, message: "Limite de uso geral atingido.", discountAmount: 0 };
    }
  }
  
  // Calcular desconto
  let discountAmount = 0;
  const discount_value = toNumber(coupon.discount_value);
  const maxDiscount = coupon.maxDiscount ? toNumber(coupon.maxDiscount) : Infinity;

  if (coupon.discountType === "percentage") {
    discountAmount = subtotal * (discount_value / 100);
  } else if (coupon.discountType === "fixed") {
    discountAmount = discount_value;
  }
  
  // Aplicar limite máximo
  discountAmount = Math.min(discountAmount, maxDiscount);
  discountAmount = Math.min(discountAmount, subtotal); 

  return {
    isValid: true,
    message: "Cupom aplicado com sucesso!",
    discountAmount: parseFloat(discountAmount.toFixed(2)),
    coupon_id: coupon.id,
    code: coupon.code,
  };
}

/**
 * Marca o cupom como usado para um determinado pedido.
 */
export async function applyCouponToOrder(orderId: number, coupon_id: number, couponCode: string, discountAmount: number, userId: number) {
  const db = await getDb();
  if (!db) throw new Error("Database not available");

  await db.insert(couponUsage).values({
    coupon_id,
    userId,
    orderId,
  });

  await db.update(orders).set({
    couponCode,
    discountAmount: discountAmount.toFixed(2),
    discountReason: `Cupom: ${couponCode}`,
  }).where(eq(orders.id, orderId));

  return { success: true };
}

/**
 * Remove o cupom de um pedido.
 */
export async function removeCouponFromOrder(orderId: number) {
  const db = await getDb();
  if (!db) throw new Error("Database not available");

  await db.delete(couponUsage).where(eq(couponUsage.orderId, orderId));
  
  await db.update(orders).set({
    couponCode: null,
    discountAmount: "0.00",
    discountReason: null,
  }).where(eq(orders.id, orderId));

  return { success: true };
}

// =========================================================================
// 2. ADMIN (CRUD)
// =========================================================================

/**
 * Lista todos os cupons (admin).
 */
export async function listCoupons() {
  const db = await getDb();
  if (!db) throw new Error("Database not available");

  const results = await db
    .select({
      id: coupons.id,
      code: coupons.code,
      description: coupons.description,
      discountType: coupons.discountType,
      discount_value: coupons.discount_value,
      minOrderValue: coupons.minOrderValue,
      maxDiscount: coupons.maxDiscount,
      usageLimit: coupons.usageLimit,
      validFrom: coupons.validFrom,
      validUntil: coupons.validUntil,
      isActive: coupons.isActive,
      timesUsed: sql<number>`count(${couponUsage.id})`, 
    })
    .from(coupons)
    .leftJoin(couponUsage, eq(coupons.id, couponUsage.coupon_id))
    .groupBy(coupons.id)
    .orderBy(desc(coupons.createdAt));

  return results;
}

/**
 * Cria um novo cupom (admin).
 */
export async function createCoupon(input: CreateCouponInput) {
  const db = await getDb();
  if (!db) throw new Error("Database not available");

  // ✅ CORREÇÃO: Removemos .returning() para compatibilidade com MySQL
  const result = await db
    .insert(coupons)
    .values({
      code: input.code.toUpperCase(),
      description: input.description || null,
      discountType: input.discountType,
      discount_value: input.discount_value.toString(),
      minOrderValue: input.minOrderValue ? input.minOrderValue.toString() : null,
      maxDiscount: input.maxDiscount ? input.maxDiscount.toString() : null,
      usageLimit: input.usageLimit || null,
      isActive: input.isActive ?? true,
      validFrom: input.validFrom ?? null,
      validUntil: input.validUntil ?? null,
    });

  // Retornamos um objeto simples indicando sucesso
  return { success: true }; 
}

/**
 * Atualiza um cupom existente (admin).
 */
export async function updateCoupon(id: number, data: UpdateCouponInput) {
  const db = await getDb();
  if (!db) throw new Error("Database not available");

  const updateData: any = {};

  if (data.description !== undefined) updateData.description = data.description;
  if (data.discountType !== undefined) updateData.discountType = data.discountType;
  if (data.discount_value !== undefined) updateData.discount_value = data.discount_value.toString();
  
  if (data.minOrderValue !== undefined)
    updateData.minOrderValue = data.minOrderValue !== null ? data.minOrderValue.toString() : null;
    
  if (data.maxDiscount !== undefined)
    updateData.maxDiscount = data.maxDiscount !== null ? data.maxDiscount.toString() : null;
    
  if (data.usageLimit !== undefined) updateData.usageLimit = data.usageLimit;
  if (data.isActive !== undefined) updateData.isActive = data.isActive;
  if (data.validFrom !== undefined) updateData.validFrom = data.validFrom;
  if (data.validUntil !== undefined) updateData.validUntil = data.validUntil;

  await db
    .update(coupons)
    .set(updateData)
    .where(eq(coupons.id, id));
  
  return { success: true };
}

/**
 * Remove um cupom (admin).
 */
export async function deleteCoupon(id: number) {
  const db = await getDb();
  if (!db) throw new Error("Database not available");

  await db.delete(couponUsage).where(eq(couponUsage.coupon_id, id));
  await db.delete(coupons).where(eq(coupons.id, id));

  return { success: true };
}

--- ARQUIVO: csv-orders-parser.ts ---
import * as fs from "fs";
import * as path from "path";

/**
 * Estrutura de um item de pedido parseado
 * Exemplo:
 * - Opção 1(300g):Escondidinho de Mandioquinha(Patinho)
 * - Opção 1(300g) - Acomp. 1:Arroz Integral
 * - Opção 1(300g) - Acomp. 2:Feijão
 */
export interface ParsedOrderItem {
  optionNumber: number;
  size: string; // "300g", "200g", "400g"
  dishName: string; // "Escondidinho de Mandioquinha(Patinho)"
  accompaniments: string[]; // ["Arroz Integral", "Feijão"]
}

/**
 * Estrutura de um pedido parseado
 */
export interface ParsedOrder {
  orderId: string;
  orderNumber: string;
  orderDate: string;
  status: string;
  customerName: string;
  customerEmail: string;
  customerPhone: string;
  orderTotal: number;
  items: ParsedOrderItem[];
  rawMeta: string; // Metadados brutos para referência
}

/**
 * Parseia o formato de metadados do CSV
 * Exemplo de entrada:
 * "name:Pacote 300 e 200g|product_id:25338|...|meta:Opçao 1(300g):Escondidinho de Mandioquinha(Patinho)|meta:Opçao 1(300g) - Acomp. 1:Arroz Integral|..."
 */
export function parseOrderMetadata(metaString: string): ParsedOrderItem[] {
  const items: ParsedOrderItem[] = [];
  const metaLines = metaString.split("|");

  // Mapa para agrupar acompanhamentos por opção
  const optionsMap = new Map<string, ParsedOrderItem>();

  for (const line of metaLines) {
    if (!line.includes("meta:")) continue;

    const metaContent = line.split("meta:")[1];
    if (!metaContent) continue;

    // Verifica se é uma linha de opção (prato)
    // Formato: "Opçao 1(300g):Escondidinho de Mandioquinha(Patinho)"
    const optionMatch = metaContent.match(/^Opçao\s+(\d+)\((\d+g)\):(.+)$/);
    if (optionMatch) {
      const [, optionNum, size, dishName] = optionMatch;
      const key = `${optionNum}-${size}`;

      optionsMap.set(key, {
        optionNumber: parseInt(optionNum, 10),
        size: size,
        dishName: dishName.trim(),
        accompaniments: [],
      });
      continue;
    }

    // Verifica se é uma linha de acompanhamento
    // Formato: "Opçao 1(300g) - Acomp. 1:Arroz Integral"
    const accompMatch = metaContent.match(
      /^Opçao\s+(\d+)\((\d+g)\)\s+-\s+Acomp\.\s+\d+:(.+)$/
    );
    if (accompMatch) {
      const [, optionNum, size, accompName] = accompMatch;
      const key = `${optionNum}-${size}`;

      const item = optionsMap.get(key);
      if (item) {
        item.accompaniments.push(accompName.trim());
      }
    }
  }

  // Converte o mapa para array ordenado
  return Array.from(optionsMap.values()).sort(
    (a, b) => a.optionNumber - b.optionNumber
  );
}

/**
 * Parseia uma linha do CSV de pedidos
 */
export function parseOrderRow(
  row: Record<string, string>,
  lineItemKey: string
): ParsedOrderItem[] {
  const lineItemValue = row[lineItemKey];
  if (!lineItemValue) return [];

  return parseOrderMetadata(lineItemValue);
}

/**
 * Carrega e parseia o arquivo CSV de pedidos
 */
export async function loadOrdersFromCSV(
  csvFilePath: string
): Promise<ParsedOrder[]> {
  try {
    if (!fs.existsSync(csvFilePath)) {
      console.warn(`Arquivo CSV não encontrado: ${csvFilePath}`);
      return [];
    }

    const content = fs.readFileSync(csvFilePath, "utf-8");
    const lines = content.split("\n");

    if (lines.length < 2) {
      console.warn("Arquivo CSV vazio ou inválido");
      return [];
    }

    // Parseia o header
    const headers = lines[0].split(",").map((h) => h.trim().replace(/^["']|["']$/g, ""));
    const headerMap = new Map(headers.map((h, i) => [h, i]));

    const orders: ParsedOrder[] = [];

    // Processa cada linha
    for (let i = 1; i < lines.length; i++) {
      const line = lines[i].trim();
      if (!line) continue;

      try {
        // Parse simples do CSV (sem suporte a aspas complexas por enquanto)
        const values = line.split(",");
        const row: Record<string, string> = {};

        headers.forEach((header, index) => {
          row[header] = values[index]?.trim().replace(/^["']|["']$/g, "") || "";
        });

        // Extrai informações básicas do pedido
        const orderId = row["order_id"] || "";
        const orderNumber = row["order_number"] || "";
        const orderDate = row["order_date"] || "";
        const status = row["status"] || "";
        const customerName = `${row["billing_first_name"] || ""} ${row["billing_last_name"] || ""}`.trim();
        const customerEmail = row["billing_email"] || row["customer_email"] || "";
        const customerPhone = row["billing_phone"] || "";
        const orderTotal = parseFloat(row["order_total"] || "0");

        // Busca todos os line_items
        const items: ParsedOrderItem[] = [];
        for (let j = 1; j <= 33; j++) {
          const lineItemKey = `line_item_${j}`;
          const lineItemValue = row[lineItemKey];

          if (lineItemValue) {
            const parsedItems = parseOrderMetadata(lineItemValue);
            items.push(...parsedItems);
          }
        }

        // Se não encontrou itens no formato novo, tenta o formato antigo
        if (items.length === 0) {
          // Tenta buscar pelo formato "Product Item X Name"
          for (let j = 1; j <= 33; j++) {
            const productNameKey = `Product Item ${j} Name`;
            const productName = row[productNameKey];

            if (productName) {
              items.push({
                optionNumber: j,
                size: "N/A",
                dishName: productName,
                accompaniments: [],
              });
            }
          }
        }

        if (items.length > 0 || orderId) {
          orders.push({
            orderId,
            orderNumber,
            orderDate,
            status,
            customerName,
            customerEmail,
            customerPhone,
            orderTotal,
            items,
            rawMeta: line.substring(0, 200), // Primeiros 200 caracteres para referência
          });
        }
      } catch (e) {
        console.warn(`Erro ao parsear linha ${i + 1}:`, (e as Error).message);
      }
    }

    return orders;
  } catch (e) {
    console.error("Erro ao carregar arquivo CSV:", e);
    return [];
  }
}

/**
 * Busca pedidos do CSV com paginação
 */
export async function getOrdersFromCSV(
  csvFilePath: string,
  limit: number = 50,
  offset: number = 0
): Promise<{ orders: ParsedOrder[]; total: number }> {
  try {
    const allOrders = await loadOrdersFromCSV(csvFilePath);
    const total = allOrders.length;
    const paginatedOrders = allOrders.slice(offset, offset + limit);

    return {
      orders: paginatedOrders,
      total,
    };
  } catch (e) {
    console.error("Erro ao buscar pedidos do CSV:", e);
    return { orders: [], total: 0 };
  }
}

/**
 * Busca um pedido específico do CSV
 */
export async function getOrderFromCSV(
  csvFilePath: string,
  orderId: string
): Promise<ParsedOrder | null> {
  try {
    const allOrders = await loadOrdersFromCSV(csvFilePath);
    return allOrders.find((o) => o.orderId === orderId) || null;
  } catch (e) {
    console.error("Erro ao buscar pedido do CSV:", e);
    return null;
  }
}

/**
 * Formata um item de pedido como texto legível
 */
export function formatOrderItem(item: ParsedOrderItem): string {
  let text = `${item.dishName} (${item.size})`;

  if (item.accompaniments.length > 0) {
    text += `\n  Acompanhamentos:\n`;
    item.accompaniments.forEach((acc) => {
      text += `    • ${acc}\n`;
    });
  }

  return text;
}

/**
 * Formata um pedido completo como texto legível
 */
export function formatOrder(order: ParsedOrder): string {
  let text = `Pedido #${order.orderNumber}\n`;
  text += `Data: ${order.orderDate}\n`;
  text += `Status: ${order.status}\n`;
  text += `Cliente: ${order.customerName}\n`;
  text += `Email: ${order.customerEmail}\n`;
  text += `Telefone: ${order.customerPhone}\n`;
  text += `Total: R$ ${order.orderTotal.toFixed(2)}\n\n`;

  text += `Itens:\n`;
  order.items.forEach((item, idx) => {
    text += `${idx + 1}. ${formatOrderItem(item)}\n`;
  });

  return text;
}


--- ARQUIVO: csv-orders-router.ts ---
import { publicProcedure, router } from "./_core/trpc";
import { z } from "zod";
import { getOrdersFromCSV, getOrderFromCSV } from "./csv-orders-parser";
import * as path from "path";
import * as process from "process";

// Caminho padrão para o arquivo CSV de pedidos
const CSV_ORDERS_PATH = process.env.CSV_ORDERS_PATH || 
  path.join(process.cwd(), "data", "orders.csv");

export const csvOrdersRouter = router({
  /**
   * Lista pedidos do CSV com paginação
   */
  list: publicProcedure
    .input(
      z.object({
        limit: z.number().min(1).max(100).default(50),
        offset: z.number().min(0).default(0),
      })
    )
    .query(async ({ input }) => {
      try {
        const { orders, total } = await getOrdersFromCSV(
          CSV_ORDERS_PATH,
          input.limit,
          input.offset
        );

        return {
          success: true,
          data: orders,
          total,
          count: orders.length,
          hasMore: input.offset + input.limit < total,
        };
      } catch (error) {
        console.error("Erro ao listar pedidos do CSV:", error);
        return {
          success: false,
          data: [],
          total: 0,
          count: 0,
          hasMore: false,
          error: (error as Error).message,
        };
      }
    }),

  /**
   * Busca um pedido específico do CSV
   */
  getById: publicProcedure
    .input(z.object({ orderId: z.string() }))
    .query(async ({ input }) => {
      try {
        const order = await getOrderFromCSV(CSV_ORDERS_PATH, input.orderId);

        if (!order) {
          return {
            success: false,
            data: null,
            error: "Pedido não encontrado",
          };
        }

        return {
          success: true,
          data: order,
        };
      } catch (error) {
        console.error("Erro ao buscar pedido do CSV:", error);
        return {
          success: false,
          data: null,
          error: (error as Error).message,
        };
      }
    }),

  /**
   * Busca pedidos por número de pedido
   */
  searchByOrderNumber: publicProcedure
    .input(z.object({ orderNumber: z.string() }))
    .query(async ({ input }) => {
      try {
        const order = await getOrderFromCSV(
          CSV_ORDERS_PATH,
          input.orderNumber
        );

        if (!order) {
          return {
            success: false,
            data: [],
            error: "Nenhum pedido encontrado com esse número",
          };
        }

        return {
          success: true,
          data: [order],
        };
      } catch (error) {
        console.error("Erro ao buscar pedido por número:", error);
        return {
          success: false,
          data: [],
          error: (error as Error).message,
        };
      }
    }),

  /**
   * Busca pedidos por email do cliente
   */
  searchByEmail: publicProcedure
    .input(z.object({ email: z.string().email() }))
    .query(async ({ input }) => {
      try {
        const { orders } = await getOrdersFromCSV(CSV_ORDERS_PATH, 1000, 0);
        const filtered = orders.filter((o) =>
          o.customerEmail.toLowerCase().includes(input.email.toLowerCase())
        );

        return {
          success: true,
          data: filtered,
          count: filtered.length,
        };
      } catch (error) {
        console.error("Erro ao buscar pedidos por email:", error);
        return {
          success: false,
          data: [],
          count: 0,
          error: (error as Error).message,
        };
      }
    }),

  /**
   * Busca pedidos por nome do cliente
   */
  searchByCustomerName: publicProcedure
    .input(z.object({ name: z.string().min(2) }))
    .query(async ({ input }) => {
      try {
        const { orders } = await getOrdersFromCSV(CSV_ORDERS_PATH, 1000, 0);
        const filtered = orders.filter((o) =>
          o.customerName.toLowerCase().includes(input.name.toLowerCase())
        );

        return {
          success: true,
          data: filtered,
          count: filtered.length,
        };
      } catch (error) {
        console.error("Erro ao buscar pedidos por nome:", error);
        return {
          success: false,
          data: [],
          count: 0,
          error: (error as Error).message,
        };
      }
    }),

  /**
   * Retorna estatísticas dos pedidos
   */
  stats: publicProcedure.query(async () => {
    try {
      const { orders, total } = await getOrdersFromCSV(CSV_ORDERS_PATH, 10000, 0);

      const stats = {
        totalOrders: total,
        totalRevenue: orders.reduce((sum, o) => sum + o.orderTotal, 0),
        averageOrderValue: 0,
        statusCounts: {} as Record<string, number>,
        itemCounts: {
          totalItems: 0,
          averageItemsPerOrder: 0,
        },
      };

      // Calcula estatísticas
      if (orders.length > 0) {
        stats.averageOrderValue = stats.totalRevenue / orders.length;

        // Conta por status
        orders.forEach((o) => {
          stats.statusCounts[o.status] = (stats.statusCounts[o.status] || 0) + 1;
        });

        // Conta itens
        const totalItems = orders.reduce((sum, o) => sum + o.items.length, 0);
        stats.itemCounts.totalItems = totalItems;
        stats.itemCounts.averageItemsPerOrder = totalItems / orders.length;
      }

      return {
        success: true,
        data: stats,
      };
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Erro ao calcular estatísticas:", error);
      return {
        success: false,
        data: null,
        error: (error as Error).message,
      };
    }
  }),
});


--- ARQUIVO: customer-addresses.ts ---
// server/customer-addresses.ts

import { eq, and, desc, sql } from "drizzle-orm";
import { getDb } from "./db";
import { customerAddresses } from "./../drizzle/schema"; 
import { encrypt } from "././encryption"; // Removido decrypt não usado aqui

// Tipos base
export type CustomerAddress = typeof customerAddresses.$inferSelect;
export type InsertCustomerAddress = typeof customerAddresses.$inferInsert;

// --- Funções de Criptografia ---
function normalizeRequired(value: unknown, fieldName: string): string {
  const s = String(value ?? "").trim();
  if (!s) throw new Error(`Campo obrigatório vazio: ${fieldName}`);
  return s;
}

function normalizeOptional(value: unknown): string | null {
  const s = String(value ?? "").trim();
  return s ? s : null;
}

function encRequired(value: unknown, fieldName: string): string {
  const s = normalizeRequired(value, fieldName);
  return encrypt(s) ?? s;
}

function encOptional(value: unknown): string | null {
  const s = normalizeOptional(value);
  if (!s) return null;
  return encrypt(s) ?? s;
}
// ------------------------------

export async function listAddressesByUserId(userId: number): Promise<CustomerAddress[]> {
  const db = await getDb();
  if (!db) throw new Error("Database not available");

  const addresses = await db
    .select()
    .from(customerAddresses)
    .where(eq(customerAddresses.userId, userId))
    .orderBy(desc(customerAddresses.isDefault), desc(customerAddresses.createdAt));

  return addresses as CustomerAddress[];
}

export async function unmarkAllAsDefault(userId: number): Promise<{ success: boolean }> {
  const db = await getDb();
  if (!db) throw new Error("Database not available");

  await db
    .update(customerAddresses)
    .set({ isDefault: false })
    .where(eq(customerAddresses.userId, userId));

  return { success: true };
}

/**
 * CRIAÇÃO DE ENDEREÇO
 */
export async function createAddress(
  data: {
    userId: number;
    label?: string | null;
    address?: string;
    street?: string; // Suporte a street vindo do front
    number: string;
    complement?: string | null;
    neighborhood: string;
    city: string;
    state: string;
    zipCode: string;
    phone?: string | null;
    isDefault?: boolean;
}
): Promise<{ id: number }> {
  const db = await getDb();
  if (!db) throw new Error("Database not available");

  const rawAddress = data.address || data.street;
  if (!rawAddress) throw new Error("Endereço (rua) é obrigatório");

  const [row] = await db
    .select({ count: sql<number>`count(*)` })
    .from(customerAddresses)
    .where(eq(customerAddresses.userId, data.userId));

  const isFirst = Number(row?.count ?? 0) === 0;
  const shouldBeDefault = Boolean(data.isDefault) || isFirst;

  if (shouldBeDefault) {
    await unmarkAllAsDefault(data.userId);
  }

  // 1. Criptografia
  const encryptedData = {
    label: encOptional(data.label) ?? encOptional("Casa") ?? "Casa",
    address: encRequired(rawAddress, "address"),
    number: encRequired(data.number, "number"),
    complement: encOptional(data.complement),
    neighborhood: encRequired(data.neighborhood, "neighborhood"),
    city: encRequired(data.city, "city"),
    state: encRequired(data.state, "state"),
    zipCode: encRequired(data.zipCode, "zipCode"),
    phone: encOptional(data.phone),
  };
  
  // 2. Objeto Final para o Banco (Usando camelCase para o Drizzle)
  // O Drizzle mapeia automaticamente userId -> user_id, zipCode -> zip_code, etc.
  const finalInsertData: any = {
      userId: data.userId, 
      label: encryptedData.label,
      address: encryptedData.address,
      number: encryptedData.number,
      complement: encryptedData.complement,
      neighborhood: encryptedData.neighborhood,
      city: encryptedData.city,
      state: encryptedData.state,
      zipCode: encryptedData.zipCode, // ✅ Use camelCase aqui
      phone: encryptedData.phone,
      isDefault: shouldBeDefault,     // ✅ Use camelCase aqui
  };

  const result: any = await db.insert(customerAddresses).values(finalInsertData);

  const insertId = result?.insertId ?? result?.[0]?.insertId ?? result?.[0]?.id;
  if (!insertId) throw new Error("Falha ao obter insertId");

  return { id: Number(insertId) };
}

/**
 * ATUALIZAÇÃO
 */
export async function updateAddress(
  id: number,
  userId: number,
  data: Partial<any>
): Promise<{ success: boolean }> {
  const db = await getDb();
  if (!db) throw new Error("Database not available");

  const updateData: any = { ...data };

  if (data.isDefault) {
    await unmarkAllAsDefault(userId);
  }

  if (updateData.street && !updateData.address) {
      updateData.address = updateData.street;
  }

  const finalUpdateData: any = {};

  if (updateData.label !== undefined) finalUpdateData.label = encOptional(updateData.label) ?? updateData.label;
  if (updateData.address !== undefined) finalUpdateData.address = encRequired(updateData.address, "address");
  if (updateData.number !== undefined) finalUpdateData.number = encRequired(updateData.number, "number");
  if (updateData.complement !== undefined) finalUpdateData.complement = encOptional(updateData.complement);
  if (updateData.neighborhood !== undefined) finalUpdateData.neighborhood = encRequired(updateData.neighborhood, "neighborhood");
  if (updateData.city !== undefined) finalUpdateData.city = encRequired(updateData.city, "city");
  if (updateData.state !== undefined) finalUpdateData.state = encRequired(updateData.state, "state");
  
  // Usando camelCase para o Drizzle
  if (updateData.zipCode !== undefined) finalUpdateData.zipCode = encRequired(updateData.zipCode, "zipCode");
  if (updateData.phone !== undefined) finalUpdateData.phone = encOptional(updateData.phone);
  if (updateData.isDefault !== undefined) finalUpdateData.isDefault = updateData.isDefault;

  if (Object.keys(finalUpdateData).length === 0) return { success: true };

  await db
    .update(customerAddresses)
    .set(finalUpdateData)
    .where(and(eq(customerAddresses.id, id), eq(customerAddresses.userId, userId)));

  return { success: true };
}

export async function deleteAddress(id: number) {
  const db = await getDb();
  
  // LOG DE DEBUG NO TERMINAL
  console.log(`[DB DEBUG] Tentando deletar endereço ID: ${id}`);

  try {
    const result = await db.delete(customerAddresses)
      .where(eq(customerAddresses.id, id));
    
    console.log(`[DB SUCCESS] Endereço ${id} removido.`);
    return result;
  } catch (error: any) {
    // Se o erro for de Foreign Key (chave estrangeira), o banco não deixa apagar
    // se o endereço estiver vinculado a um pedido já feito.
    console.error(`[DB ERROR] Falha ao deletar endereço ${id}:`, error.message);
    throw new Error("Não é possível deletar: este endereço está vinculado a pedidos anteriores.");
  }
}

export async function getDefaultAddress(userId: number): Promise<CustomerAddress | null> {
  const db = await getDb();
  if (!db) throw new Error("Database not available");

  const [defaultAddress] = await db
    .select()
    .from(customerAddresses)
    .where(and(eq(customerAddresses.userId, userId), eq(customerAddresses.isDefault, true)))
    .limit(1);

  return (defaultAddress as any) || null;
}

    throw new Error("Function not implemented.");
}

--- ARQUIVO: db\schema.ts ---
export * from "./media";

--- ARQUIVO: db.ts ---
// server/db.ts - COMPLETO (Conexão + Funções Auxiliares)

import { drizzle } from "drizzle-orm/mysql2";
import mysql from "mysql2/promise";
import { eq } from "drizzle-orm";
import * as schema from "../drizzle/schema"; // Importa todo o schema para o drizzle
import { users, user_profiles } from "../drizzle/schema"; // Importa tabelas específicas

// =========================================================
// 1. CONFIGURAÇÃO DA CONEXÃO COM O BANCO DE DADOS
// =========================================================

// Variável para armazenar a instância e evitar múltiplas conexões em hot-reload
let dbInstance: ReturnType<typeof drizzle> | undefined;

export async function getDb() {
  if (dbInstance) return dbInstance;

  if (!process.env.DATABASE_URL) {
    throw new Error("DATABASE_URL não encontrada nas variáveis de ambiente (.env)");
  }

  try {
    // Cria o pool de conexões
    const poolConnection = mysql.createPool({
      uri: process.env.DATABASE_URL,
    });

    // Inicializa o Drizzle com o schema
    dbInstance = drizzle(poolConnection, { schema, mode: "default" });
    
    // Log apenas na primeira conexão
    console.log("✅ Database Pool Initialized (MySQL)");
    
    return dbInstance;
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("❌ Falha ao conectar no banco de dados:", error);
    throw error;
  }
}

// =========================================================
// 2. FUNÇÕES AUXILIARES (USER / AUTH)
// =========================================================

// Definimos o tipo de entrada para melhor clareza e segurança
type UpsertUserInput = {
  openId: string;
  name?: string | null;
  email?: string | null;
  loginMethod?: string | null;
  role?: string | null;
  lastSignedIn?: Date;
};

export async function upsertUser(user: UpsertUserInput) {
  const db = await getDb();
  if (!db) throw new Error("Database not available");

  // ✅ Proteção CRÍTICA contra inserts fantasmas/vazios
  if (!user?.openId || typeof user.openId !== "string" || !user.openId.trim()) {
    console.warn("[Database] upsertUser called without valid openId. Blocking insert.", user);
    return;
  }

  const openId = user.openId.trim();

  // Remove openId do objeto de campos a atualizar (pois ele é a chave de busca)
  const { openId: _, ...fieldsToUpdate } = user;

  // Monta o objeto de atualização de forma segura
  const updateData: { [key: string]: any } = {};

  (Object.keys(fieldsToUpdate) as Array<keyof typeof fieldsToUpdate>).forEach(key => {
    const value = fieldsToUpdate[key];
    // Se o valor foi fornecido (não undefined), inclua-o (aceitando null)
    if (value !== undefined) {
        updateData[key] = value ?? null;
    }
  });

  // Sempre garante lastSignedIn
  if (!updateData.lastSignedIn) {
    updateData.lastSignedIn = new Date();
  }

  // 1) Verifica se já existe
  const existing = await db
    .select({ id: users.id })
    .from(users)
    .where(eq(users.openId, openId))
    .limit(1);

  if (existing.length > 0) {
    // 2) UPDATE
    await db.update(users).set(updateData).where(eq(users.openId, openId));
    return existing[0]; // Retorna o usuário existente
  }

  // 3) INSERT
  // Garante que campos obrigatórios tenham valor ou null na criação
  const [newUser] = await db.insert(users).values({
    openId,
    name: updateData.name ?? null,
    email: updateData.email ?? null,
    loginMethod: updateData.loginMethod ?? null,
    role: updateData.role ?? "user", // Default para 'user' se não vier
    lastSignedIn: updateData.lastSignedIn,
  } as any).returning(); // 'as any' usado para flexibilidade com tipos opcionais do Drizzle
  
  return newUser;
}

export async function getUserByOpenId(openId: string) {
  const db = await getDb();
  if (!db) return undefined;

  const userResult = await db
    .select()
    .from(users)
    .where(eq(users.openId, openId))
    .limit(1);

  if (userResult.length === 0) return undefined;

  const user = userResult[0];

  const profileResult = await db
    .select()
    .from(user_profiles)
    .where(eq(user_profiles.userId, user.id))
    .limit(1);

  const profile = profileResult.length > 0 ? profileResult[0] : null;

  return { ...user, profile };
}

// server/debug-insert.ts
import "dotenv/config";
import { getDb } from "./db";
import { accompanimentGroups } from "../drizzle/schema";

async function debug() {
  const db = await getDb();
  if (!db) return console.error("Sem conexão DB");

  console.log("🔍 Tentando inserir um grupo de teste...");

  try {
    // CORREÇÃO: Usando os nomes em CamelCase definidos no schema
    const result = await db.insert(accompanimentGroups).values({
      name: "Grupo Debug " + Date.now(),
      slug: "debug-" + Date.now(),
      description: "Teste de inserção",
      isActive: true,       // Antes: is_active
      createdAt: new Date(), // Antes: created_at
      updated_at: new Date(), // Antes: updated_at
    });
    
    console.log("✅ SUCESSO! ID inserido:", result);
  } catch (error: any) {
    console.error("\n❌ ERRO FATAL DETECTADO:");
    console.error("Mensagem:", error.message);
    if (error.sqlState) console.error("Código SQL State:", error.sqlState);
    if (error.sql) console.error("Query SQL tentada:", error.sql);
  }
  
  process.exit(0);
}

--- ARQUIVO: discountRules.ts ---
// server/discountRules.ts
import { eq, desc, sql } from "drizzle-orm"; 
import { getDb } from "./db.js";
import { discountRules } from "../drizzle/schema.js"; 
import { z } from "zod";

// -------------------------------------------------------------
// ESQUEMA DE VALIDAÇÃO (ZOD)
// -------------------------------------------------------------

export const createDiscountRuleInput = z.object({
  name: z.string().min(1).max(255),
  description: z.string().max(1000).optional().nullable(),
  minQuantity: z.coerce.number().min(1),
  maxQuantity: z.coerce.number().min(1).optional().nullable(),
  discountType: z.enum(["percentage", "fixed"]),
  discount_value: z.coerce.number().min(0),
  priority: z.coerce.number().min(0).optional().nullable(),
  isActive: z.boolean().optional().default(true),
});

// -------------------------------------------------------------
// FUNÇÕES DE SERVIÇO (CRUD)
// -------------------------------------------------------------

export async function listDiscountRules() {
  const db = await getDb();
  if (!db) throw new Error("Banco de dados não inicializado");

  try {
    const rules = await db.select().from(discountRules).orderBy(desc(discountRules.id));

    return rules.map(rule => ({
      id: Number(rule.id),
      name: rule.name || "",
      description: rule.description || "",
      minQuantity: Number(rule.minQuantity),
      maxQuantity: rule.maxQuantity ? Number(rule.maxQuantity) : null,
      discountType: rule.discountType,
      // Converte Decimal (string) para Number para o tRPC/Frontend
      discount_value: rule.discount_value ? Number(rule.discount_value) : 0,
      value: rule.discount_value ? Number(rule.discount_value) : 0, 
      priority: rule.priority ? Number(rule.priority) : 0,
      isActive: Boolean(rule.isActive),
    }));
  } catch (error: any) {
    console.error("❌ ERRO AO LISTAR (discount_rules):", error.message);
    return []; 
  }
}

export async function createDiscountRule(data: z.infer<typeof createDiscountRuleInput>) {
  const db = await getDb();
  if (!db) throw new Error("Database not available");

  // ✅ CORREÇÃO PARA MYSQL: MySQL não suporta .returning(). 
  // Fazemos o insert e retornamos o sucesso.
  await db.insert(discountRules).values({
    name: data.name,
    description: data.description ?? null,
    minQuantity: data.minQuantity,
    maxQuantity: data.maxQuantity ?? null,
    discountType: data.discountType,
    discount_value: data.discount_value.toString(), // Salva como string (Decimal)
    priority: data.priority ?? 0,
    isActive: data.isActive ?? true,
  });

  return { success: true };
}

export async function updateDiscountRule(id: number, data: Partial<z.infer<typeof createDiscountRuleInput>>) {
  const db = await getDb();
  if (!db) throw new Error("Database not available");

  // ✅ CORREÇÃO PARA MYSQL: Removido .returning()
  const updateData: any = { ...data };
  
  if (data.discount_value !== undefined) {
    updateData.discount_value = data.discount_value.toString();
  }

  await db.update(discountRules)
    .set({
        ...updateData,
        updated_at: new Date()
    })
    .where(eq(discountRules.id, id));

  return { success: true };
}

export async function deleteDiscountRule(id: number) {
  const db = await getDb();
  if (!db) throw new Error("Database not available");

  await db.delete(discountRules).where(eq(discountRules.id, id));
  return { success: true };
}

--- ARQUIVO: dishes.ts ---
// server/dishes.ts
//
// Queries públicas para o front (cardápio, tamanhos e acompanhamentos)
// ✅ Alinhado com o banco:
// - dish_sizes é GLOBAL (não tem dish_id)
// - size_accompaniment_groups usa accompaniment_group_id

import { and, asc, eq } from "drizzle-orm";
import { getDb } from "./db";
import {
  dishes,
  categories,
  dishSizes,
  accompanimentGroups,
  accompanimentOptions,
  sizeAccompanimentGroups,
} from "../drizzle/schema";

export async function listDishes(input?: {
  categoryId?: number | null;
  includeInactive?: boolean;
}) {
  const db = await getDb();
  if (!db) throw new Error("Database not available");

  const whereParts: any[] = [];
  if (input?.categoryId != null) whereParts.push(eq(dishes.categoryId, input.categoryId));
  if (!input?.includeInactive) whereParts.push(eq(dishes.isActive, true));

  const where = whereParts.length ? (and(...(whereParts as [any, ...any[]])) as any) : undefined;

  return db
    .select({
      id: dishes.id,
      name: dishes.name,
      description: dishes.description,
      categoryId: dishes.categoryId,
      categoryName: categories.name,
      price: dishes.price,
      imageUrl: dishes.imageUrl,
      isActive: dishes.isActive,
      isFeatured: dishes.isFeatured,
      displayOrder: dishes.displayOrder,
      nutritionalInfo: dishes.nutritionalInfo,
    })
    .from(dishes)
    .leftJoin(categories, eq(categories.id, dishes.categoryId))
    .where(where)
    .orderBy(asc(dishes.displayOrder), asc(dishes.name));
}

// Mantém assinatura antiga (dishId) por compatibilidade, mas retorna todos os tamanhos
export async function getDishSizes(_dishId: number) {
  const db = await getDb();
  if (!db) throw new Error("Database not available");

  return db
    .select({
      id: dishSizes.id,
      name: dishSizes.name,
      weight: dishSizes.weight,
      priceModifier: dishSizes.priceModifier,
      displayOrder: dishSizes.displayOrder,
      isActive: dishSizes.isActive,
      noAccompanimentsMessage: dishSizes.noAccompanimentsMessage,
    })
    .from(dishSizes)
    .where(eq(dishSizes.isActive, true))
    .orderBy(asc(dishSizes.displayOrder), asc(dishSizes.name));
}

export async function getSizeAccompanimentGroups(sizeId: number) {
  const db = await getDb();
  if (!db) throw new Error("Database not available");

  const links = await db
    .select({
      id: sizeAccompanimentGroups.id,
      sizeId: sizeAccompanimentGroups.sizeId,
      groupId: sizeAccompanimentGroups.accompanimentGroupId,
      isRequired: sizeAccompanimentGroups.isRequired,
      allowMultiple: sizeAccompanimentGroups.allowMultiple,
      displayOrder: sizeAccompanimentGroups.displayOrder,
    })
    .from(sizeAccompanimentGroups)
    .where(eq(sizeAccompanimentGroups.sizeId, sizeId))
    .orderBy(asc(sizeAccompanimentGroups.displayOrder));

  const groups = await Promise.all(
    links.map(async (l) => {
      const [g] = await db
        .select({
          id: accompanimentGroups.id,
          name: accompanimentGroups.name,
          maxSelections: accompanimentGroups.maxSelections,
          isActive: accompanimentGroups.isActive,
        })
        .from(accompanimentGroups)
        .where(eq(accompanimentGroups.id, l.groupId))
        .limit(1);

      if (!g) return null;

      return {
        ...l,
        group: g,
      };
    }),
  );

  return groups.filter(Boolean);
}

export async function getAccompanimentGroupOptions(groupId: number) {
  const db = await getDb();
  if (!db) throw new Error("Database not available");

  return db
    .select({
      id: accompanimentOptions.id,
      groupId: accompanimentOptions.groupId,
      name: accompanimentOptions.name,
      priceModifier: accompanimentOptions.priceModifier,
      isActive: accompanimentOptions.isActive,
      displayOrder: accompanimentOptions.displayOrder,
    })
    .from(accompanimentOptions)
    .where(and(eq(accompanimentOptions.groupId, groupId), eq(accompanimentOptions.isActive, true)))
    .orderBy(asc(accompanimentOptions.displayOrder), asc(accompanimentOptions.name));
}

export async function getDishWithSizes(dishId: number) {
  const db = await getDb();
  if (!db) throw new Error("Database not available");

  const [dish] = await db
    .select({
      id: dishes.id,
      name: dishes.name,
      description: dishes.description,
      categoryId: dishes.categoryId,
      price: dishes.price,
      imageUrl: dishes.imageUrl,
      isActive: dishes.isActive,
      isFeatured: dishes.isFeatured,
      displayOrder: dishes.displayOrder,
      nutritionalInfo: dishes.nutritionalInfo,
    })
    .from(dishes)
    .where(eq(dishes.id, dishId))
    .limit(1);

  if (!dish) return null;

  const sizes = await getDishSizes(dishId);
  return { ...dish, sizes };
}

export async function getSizeWithAccompaniments(sizeId: number) {
  const db = await getDb();
  if (!db) throw new Error("Database not available");

  const [size] = await db
    .select({
      id: dishSizes.id,
      name: dishSizes.name,
      weight: dishSizes.weight,
      priceModifier: dishSizes.priceModifier,
      displayOrder: dishSizes.displayOrder,
      isActive: dishSizes.isActive,
      noAccompanimentsMessage: dishSizes.noAccompanimentsMessage,
    })
    .from(dishSizes)
    .where(eq(dishSizes.id, sizeId))
    .limit(1);

  if (!size) return null;

  const groups = (await getSizeAccompanimentGroups(sizeId)) as any[];

  const groupsWithOptions = await Promise.all(
    groups.map(async (g) => {
      const options = await getAccompanimentGroupOptions(g.groupId);
      return { ...g, options };
    }),
  );

  return { ...size, accompanimentGroups: groupsWithOptions };
}
