--- ARQUIVO: encryption.ts ---
// server/encryption.ts
import * as crypto from "crypto";

/**
 * Módulo de criptografia AES-256-GCM para proteger dados sensíveis.
 *
 * ✅ Senhas NÃO usam este módulo (senhas = hash PBKDF2/Argon2/bcrypt).
 * ✅ PII usa criptografia reversível (AES-GCM).
 * ✅ Para busca/deduplicação de PII criptografada, use hashes com pepper (piiHashDigits / piiHashText).
 *
 * Observação importante:
 * - decrypt() é "backward-compatible": se o valor NÃO estiver no formato iv:tag:cipher,
 *   ele retorna o texto original (útil para dados antigos em texto puro).
 */

const ALGORITHM = "aes-256-gcm";
const IV_LENGTH = 16;

// Pepper para hashing de PII (NÃO é a chave do AES).
// Configure no .env: PII_PEPPER="uma-string-bem-longa-aleatoria"
const PII_PEPPER = process.env.PII_PEPPER || "";

/**
 * Obtém a chave de criptografia AES do ambiente.
 * Procura por DB_ENCRYPTION_KEY (preferido) ou ENCRYPTION_KEY (fallback).
 */
function getEncryptionKey(): Buffer {
  let key = process.env.DB_ENCRYPTION_KEY || process.env.ENCRYPTION_KEY;

  if (!key) {
    if (process.env.NODE_ENV === "production") {
      throw new Error(
        "DB_ENCRYPTION_KEY não configurada no ambiente de produção! " +
          "Gere uma chave com: openssl rand -base64 32"
      );
    }

    console.warn(
      "[ENCRYPTION] ⚠️  DB_ENCRYPTION_KEY não encontrada. Usando chave temporária (apenas desenvolvimento)."
    );
    key = crypto.randomBytes(32).toString("base64");
  }

  // Deriva 32 bytes (256 bits). Salt fixo é ok aqui pois a entropia vem do segredo do env.
  return crypto.scryptSync(key, "salt", 32);
}

/**
 * Helpers de normalização e hashing (para busca/deduplicação de PII)
 */
export function normalizeDigits(v: string | null | undefined): string {
  return (v ?? "").replace(/\D/g, "");
}

export function sha256Hex(input: string): string {
  return crypto.createHash("sha256").update(input).digest("hex");
}

/**
 * Hash para PII numérica (CPF/telefone). Recomendado guardar no DB (ex: *_hash).
 * Exige PII_PEPPER no .env.
 */
export function piiHashDigits(digits: string | null | undefined): string | null {
  const d = normalizeDigits(digits);
  if (!d) return null;
  if (!PII_PEPPER) throw new Error("PII_PEPPER não configurado no .env");
  return sha256Hex(`${PII_PEPPER}:${d}`);
}

/**
 * Hash para PII textual.
 * Exige PII_PEPPER no .env.
 */
export function piiHashText(text: string | null | undefined): string | null {
  const t = (text ?? "").trim();
  if (!t) return null;
  if (!PII_PEPPER) throw new Error("PII_PEPPER não configurado no .env");
  return sha256Hex(`${PII_PEPPER}:${t}`);
}

/**
 * Criptografa um texto usando AES-256-GCM
 * @returns String no formato: iv:authTag:encryptedData (hex)
 */
export function encrypt(text: string | null | undefined): string | null {
  const t = (text ?? "").trim();
  if (!t) return null;

  try {
    const key = getEncryptionKey();
    const iv = crypto.randomBytes(IV_LENGTH);
    const cipher = crypto.createCipheriv(ALGORITHM, key, iv);

    let encrypted = cipher.update(t, "utf8", "hex");
    encrypted += cipher.final("hex");

    const authTag = cipher.getAuthTag();
    return `${iv.toString("hex")}:${authTag.toString("hex")}:${encrypted}`;
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("[ENCRYPTION] Erro ao criptografar:", error);
    throw new Error("Falha ao criptografar dados sensíveis");
  }
}

/**
 * Descriptografa AES-256-GCM.
 *
 * ✅ Backward compatible:
 * - Se não estiver no formato iv:tag:cipher, retorna o valor original (texto puro legado).
 */
export function decrypt(encryptedText: string | Buffer | null | undefined): string | null {
  if (!encryptedText) return null;

  let keyString: string;
  if (encryptedText instanceof Buffer) {
    keyString = encryptedText.toString("utf8").trim();
  } else if (typeof encryptedText === "string") {
    keyString = encryptedText.trim();
  } else {
    return null;
  }

  if (keyString === "") return null;

  try {
    const parts = keyString.split(":");
    if (parts.length !== 3) {
      // legado (texto puro) ou formato antigo: devolve como está
      return keyString;
    }

    const key = getEncryptionKey();
    const iv = Buffer.from(parts[0], "hex");
    const authTag = Buffer.from(parts[1], "hex");
    const encrypted = parts[2];

    const decipher = crypto.createDecipheriv(ALGORITHM, key, iv);
    decipher.setAuthTag(authTag);

    let decrypted = decipher.update(encrypted, "hex", "utf8");
    decrypted += decipher.final("utf8");
    return decrypted;
  } catch (error) {
    // fallback para não “sumir” dados legados/formato estranho
    console.error("[ENCRYPTION] Erro ao descriptografar:", (error as Error).message);
    return keyString;
  }
}

/**
 * Criptografa campos de um objeto
 */
export function encryptFields<T extends Record<string, any>>(data: T, fields: (keyof T)[]): T {
  const encrypted = { ...data };
  for (const field of fields) {
    if (encrypted[field] !== undefined && encrypted[field] !== null) {
      const v = encrypted[field];
      encrypted[field] = encrypt(typeof v === "string" ? v : String(v)) as any;
    }
  }
  return encrypted;
}

/**
 * Descriptografa campos de um objeto
 */
export function decryptFields<T extends Record<string, any>>(data: T, fields: (keyof T)[]): T {
  const decrypted = { ...data };
  for (const field of fields) {
    if (decrypted[field] !== undefined && decrypted[field] !== null) {
      decrypted[field] = decrypt(decrypted[field]) as any;
    }
  }
  return decrypted;
}

export function generateEncryptionKey(): string {
  return crypto.randomBytes(32).toString("base64");
}

/**
 * Lista de campos sensíveis por “camada” (nomes DEV / do schema do Drizzle!)
 *
 * ✅ Como você decidiu: CPF fica em users.customerDocument (e pode ser criptografado como string).
 * ✅ phone e birthDate ficam em user_profiles.
 *
 * IMPORTANTE: customer_addresses e outros você pode ir adicionando conforme for de fato criptografar no router.
 */
export const SENSITIVE_FIELDS = {
  customer_addresses: [
    "street",
    "number",
    "complement",
    "neighborhood",
    "city",
    "zipCode",
    "phone",
  ] as const,

  // ✅ CPF NÃO fica mais aqui
  user_profiles: [
    "phone",
    "birthDate",
    // se você realmente usa esses campos no profile, ok manter:
    "address",
    "city",
    "state",
    "zipCode",
  ] as const,

  orders: ["deliveryAddress", "deliveryPhone"] as const,

  // ✅ users (NOME DO CAMPO NO DRIZZLE SCHEMA)
  users: ["customerDocument"] as const,
} as const;


--- ARQUIVO: fix-db.ts ---
// server/fix-db.ts
import "dotenv/config";
import mysql from "mysql2/promise";

async function fixDatabase() {
  if (!process.env.DATABASE_URL) throw new Error("DATABASE_URL vazia");

  console.log("🔧 Reparando banco de dados...");
  const connection = await mysql.createConnection(process.env.DATABASE_URL);

  // Tabelas que precisam da coluna updated_at
  const tablesToFix = ["accompanimentGroups", "dishSizes"];

  for (const table of tablesToFix) {
    try {
      console.log(`Verificando tabela ${table}...`);
      // Tenta adicionar a coluna. Se já existir, o banco vai reclamar (e nós ignoramos o erro).
      await connection.query(`
        ALTER TABLE \`${table}\`
        ADD COLUMN \`updated_at\` timestamp DEFAULT NOW() ON UPDATE NOW();
      `);
      console.log(`✅ Coluna 'updated_at' adicionada em '${table}'!`);
    } catch (error: any) {
      if (error.code === 'ER_DUP_FIELDNAME') {
        console.log(`ℹ️ A coluna 'updated_at' já existe em '${table}'.`);
      } else {
        console.error(`❌ Erro ao alterar '${table}':`, error.message);
      }
    }
  }

  await connection.end();
  console.log("🏁 Reparação concluída!");
  process.exit(0);
}

fixDatabase().catch(console.error);

--- ARQUIVO: fix-final.ts ---
// server/fix-final.ts
import "dotenv/config";
import mysql from "mysql2/promise";

async function run() {
  const connection = await mysql.createConnection(process.env.DATABASE_URL!);
  console.log("🔧 Corrigindo colunas faltantes...");

  try {
    // Adiciona updated_at em accompanimentGroups
    await connection.query(`
      ALTER TABLE \`accompanimentGroups\` 
      ADD COLUMN \`updated_at\` timestamp DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP;
    `);
    console.log("✅ updated_at adicionado em accompanimentGroups");
  } catch (e) { console.log("⚠️ (Info) accompanimentGroups já deve estar ok"); }

  try {
    // Adiciona updated_at em dishSizes
    await connection.query(`
      ALTER TABLE \`dishSizes\` 
      ADD COLUMN \`updated_at\` timestamp DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP;
    `);
    console.log("✅ updated_at adicionado em dishSizes");
  } catch (e) { console.log("⚠️ (Info) dishSizes já deve estar ok"); }

  process.exit(0);
}
run();

--- ARQUIVO: fix-loyalty-final.ts ---
// server/fix-loyalty-final.ts
import "dotenv/config";
import mysql from "mysql2/promise";

async function fixLoyaltyTable() {
  if (!process.env.DATABASE_URL) throw new Error("DATABASE_URL vazia");

  const connection = await mysql.createConnection(process.env.DATABASE_URL);
  console.log("🔌 Conectado ao banco.");

  // Função segura para adicionar coluna se não existir
  async function addCol(colName: string, def: string) {
    try {
      const [rows] = await connection.query<any[]>(
        `SELECT * FROM information_schema.COLUMNS WHERE TABLE_SCHEMA = DATABASE() AND TABLE_NAME = 'loyaltySettings' AND COLUMN_NAME = ?`,
        [colName]
      );
      if (rows.length === 0) {
        console.log(`➕ Adicionando: ${colName}`);
        await connection.query(`ALTER TABLE \`loyaltySettings\` ADD COLUMN \`${colName}\` ${def}`);
      } else {
        console.log(`✅ Já existe: ${colName}`);
      }
    } catch (e: any) {
      console.error(`Erro ${colName}: ${e.message}`);
    }
  }

  // Garante que a tabela existe
  await connection.query(`
    CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS \`loyaltySettings\` (
      \`id\` serial PRIMARY KEY,
      \`enabled\` boolean DEFAULT true
    );
  `);

  // Adiciona as colunas que o código novo exige
  await addCol("conversion_rate_points", "int DEFAULT 1");
  await addCol("conversion_rate_money", "decimal(10,2) DEFAULT '1.00'");
  await addCol("redemption_rate_points", "int DEFAULT 100");
  await addCol("redemption_rate_money", "decimal(10,2) DEFAULT '1.00'");
  await addCol("max_discount_amount", "decimal(10,2) DEFAULT '50.00'");
  await addCol("min_cart_amount", "decimal(10,2) DEFAULT '0.00'");
  await addCol("min_discount_required", "decimal(10,2) DEFAULT '0.00'");
  await addCol("points_expiration_days", "int DEFAULT 365");
  await addCol("points_per_signup", "int DEFAULT 0");
  await addCol("points_per_review", "int DEFAULT 0");
  await addCol("updated_at", "timestamp DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP");

  console.log("🏁 Tabela loyaltySettings corrigida!");
  await connection.end();
  process.exit(0);
}

fixLoyaltyTable();

--- ARQUIVO: fix-orders-db.ts ---
// server/fix-orders-v2.ts
import "dotenv/config";
import mysql from "mysql2/promise";

async function fixOrdersDatabase() {
  if (!process.env.DATABASE_URL) throw new Error("DATABASE_URL vazia");

  console.log("🔌 Conectando ao banco...");
  const connection = await mysql.createConnection(process.env.DATABASE_URL);

  // Função auxiliar para verificar se coluna existe
  async function columnExists(tableName: string, columnName: string) {
    const [rows] = await connection.query<any[]>(
      `SELECT * FROM information_schema.COLUMNS 
       WHERE TABLE_SCHEMA = DATABASE() 
       AND TABLE_NAME = ? 
       AND COLUMN_NAME = ?`,
      [tableName, columnName]
    );
    return rows.length > 0;
  }

  // Função para adicionar coluna com segurança
  async function addColumnSafely(tableName: string, columnName: string, definition: string) {
    const exists = await columnExists(tableName, columnName);
    if (!exists) {
      console.log(`➕ Adicionando coluna '${columnName}' na tabela '${tableName}'...`);
      await connection.query(`ALTER TABLE \`${tableName}\` ADD COLUMN \`${columnName}\` ${definition}`);
    } else {
      console.log(`✅ Coluna '${columnName}' já existe em '${tableName}'.`);
    }
  }

  console.log("\n🔧 Verificando tabela 'orders'...");
  
  await addColumnSafely("orders", "shipping_address", "varchar(255)");
  await addColumnSafely("orders", "shipping_city", "varchar(100)");
  await addColumnSafely("orders", "shipping_state", "varchar(50)");
  await addColumnSafely("orders", "shipping_zip_code", "varchar(20)");
  await addColumnSafely("orders", "updated_at", "timestamp DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP");
  await addColumnSafely("orders", "payment_method", "varchar(50)");

  console.log("\n🔧 Verificando tabela 'orderItems'...");
  
  // Verifica se a tabela existe antes
  try {
    await connection.query("SELECT 1 FROM `orderItems` LIMIT 1");
    await addColumnSafely("orderItems", "item_type", "varchar(20) DEFAULT 'dish'");
    await addColumnSafely("orderItems", "package_id", "int");
  } catch (e) {
    console.log("⚠️ Tabela orderItems não existe, criando do zero...");
    await connection.query(`
      CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS \`orderItems\` (
        \`id\` serial PRIMARY KEY,
        \`order_id\` int NOT NULL,
        \`dish_id\` int,
        \`package_id\` int,
        \`item_type\` varchar(20) DEFAULT 'dish',
        \`quantity\` int DEFAULT 1,
        \`unit_price\` decimal(10,2) DEFAULT '0.00',
        \`total_price\` decimal(10,2) DEFAULT '0.00',
        \`created_at\` timestamp DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
      );
    `);
  }

  console.log("\n🏁 Reparo concluído com sucesso!");
  await connection.end();
  process.exit(0);
}

fixOrdersDatabase().catch((err) => {
  console.error("❌ Erro fatal:", err);
  process.exit(1);
});

--- ARQUIVO: loyalty.test.ts ---
import { describe, expect, it } from "vitest";
import {
  LOYALTY_CONFIG,
  calculatePointsFromPurchase,
  calculateDiscountFromPoints,
} from "./loyalty";

/**
 * Testes para sistema de fidelidade
 */
describe("Loyalty System", () => {
  describe("Configuration", () => {
    it("should have correct loyalty configuration", () => {
      expect(LOYALTY_CONFIG.POINTS_PER_REAL).toBe(1);
      expect(LOYALTY_CONFIG.DISCOUNT_PER_POINT).toBe(0.01);
      expect(LOYALTY_CONFIG.MIN_POINTS_TO_REDEEM).toBe(100);
    });
  });

  describe("Points Calculation", () => {
    it("should calculate points from purchase amount", () => {
      expect(calculatePointsFromPurchase(50.0)).toBe(50);
      expect(calculatePointsFromPurchase(100.0)).toBe(100);
      expect(calculatePointsFromPurchase(250.75)).toBe(250);
    });

    it("should handle zero purchase amount", () => {
      expect(calculatePointsFromPurchase(0)).toBe(0);
    });

    it("should handle fractional amounts", () => {
      expect(calculatePointsFromPurchase(99.99)).toBe(99);
      expect(calculatePointsFromPurchase(100.50)).toBe(100);
    });

    it("should calculate discount from points", () => {
      expect(calculateDiscountFromPoints(100)).toBe(1.0);
      expect(calculateDiscountFromPoints(500)).toBe(5.0);
      expect(calculateDiscountFromPoints(1000)).toBe(10.0);
    });

    it("should handle zero points for discount", () => {
      expect(calculateDiscountFromPoints(0)).toBe(0);
    });
  });

  describe("Points Accumulation", () => {
    it("should accumulate points correctly", () => {
      const purchase1 = 50.0;
      const purchase2 = 75.0;
      const purchase3 = 25.0;

      const points1 = calculatePointsFromPurchase(purchase1);
      const points2 = calculatePointsFromPurchase(purchase2);
      const points3 = calculatePointsFromPurchase(purchase3);

      const totalPoints = points1 + points2 + points3;
      expect(totalPoints).toBe(150);
    });

    it("should calculate total spent correctly", () => {
      const purchase1 = 50.0;
      const purchase2 = 75.0;
      const purchase3 = 25.0;

      const totalSpent = purchase1 + purchase2 + purchase3;
      expect(totalSpent).toBe(150.0);
    });
  });

  describe("Points Redemption", () => {
    it("should validate minimum points for redemption", () => {
      const minPoints = LOYALTY_CONFIG.MIN_POINTS_TO_REDEEM;
      expect(minPoints).toBe(100);
    });

    it("should calculate correct discount for redemption", () => {
      const pointsToRedeem = 200;
      const expectedDiscount = pointsToRedeem * LOYALTY_CONFIG.DISCOUNT_PER_POINT;
      expect(expectedDiscount).toBe(2.0);
    });

    it("should handle multiple redemptions", () => {
      const points1 = 150;
      const points2 = 100;
      const points3 = 50;

      const discount1 = calculateDiscountFromPoints(points1);
      const discount2 = calculateDiscountFromPoints(points2);
      const discount3 = calculateDiscountFromPoints(points3);

      const totalDiscount = discount1 + discount2 + discount3;
      expect(totalDiscount).toBe(3.0);
    });
  });

  describe("Points Balance", () => {
    it("should track points balance correctly", () => {
      let balance = 0;

      // Add points from purchase
      const purchasePoints = calculatePointsFromPurchase(100.0);
      balance += purchasePoints;
      expect(balance).toBe(100);

      // Redeem points
      const redeemPoints = 50;
      balance -= redeemPoints;
      expect(balance).toBe(50);

      // Add more points
      const morePoints = calculatePointsFromPurchase(75.0);
      balance += morePoints;
      expect(balance).toBe(125);
    });

    it("should prevent negative balance", () => {
      let balance = 100;
      const redeemPoints = 150;

      // Should not allow redemption if balance is insufficient
      const canRedeem = balance >= redeemPoints;
      expect(canRedeem).toBe(false);
    });
  });

  describe("Loyalty Tier Simulation", () => {
    it("should calculate tier based on total spent", () => {
      const totalSpent1 = 500.0;
      const totalSpent2 = 1500.0;
      const totalSpent3 = 5000.0;

      // Simulate tier levels
      const getTier = (spent: number) => {
        if (spent >= 5000) return "Gold";
        if (spent >= 1000) return "Silver";
        if (spent >= 500) return "Bronze";
        return "Regular";
      };

      expect(getTier(totalSpent1)).toBe("Bronze");
      expect(getTier(totalSpent2)).toBe("Silver");
      expect(getTier(totalSpent3)).toBe("Gold");
    });
  });


  describe("Bonus Points (Future Feature)", () => {
    it("should calculate bonus points for special occasions", () => {
      const basePoints = 100;
      const bonusMultiplier = 1.5; // 50% bonus

      const totalPoints = basePoints * bonusMultiplier;
      expect(totalPoints).toBe(150);
    });

    it("should apply referral bonus", () => {
      const referrerPoints = 50;
      const refereePoints = 50;

      const totalBonusPoints = referrerPoints + refereePoints;
      expect(totalBonusPoints).toBe(100);
    });
  });

  describe("Transaction History", () => {
    it("should track transaction types", () => {
      const transactionTypes = [
        "Compra",
        "Resgate de pontos",
        "Bônus de referência",
        "Ajuste administrativo",
      ];

      expect(transactionTypes).toContain("Compra");
      expect(transactionTypes).toContain("Resgate de pontos");
      expect(transactionTypes).toContain("Bônus de referência");
    });
  });
});


--- ARQUIVO: loyalty.ts ---
// server/loyalty.ts

import { eq, desc, like, or, count, and, sum, sql } from "drizzle-orm";
import { getDb } from "./db"; 
import { loyaltySettings, users, loyaltyHistory, orders } from "../drizzle/schema/index.js";

// =================================================================
// 1. CONFIGURAÇÕES (CRUD)
// =================================================================

export async function getLoyaltySettings() {
    const db = await getDb();
    if (!db) throw new Error("Database not available"); 
    
    const settings = await db.select().from(loyaltySettings).limit(1);
    
    if (settings.length === 0) {
        console.log("Criando configurações padrão de fidelidade...");
        await db.insert(loyaltySettings).values({
            enabled: true,
            conversionRatePoints: 1,
            conversionRateMoney: "1.00",
            redemptionRatePoints: 100,
            redemptionRateMoney: "1.00",
            maxDiscountAmount: "50.00",
            minCartAmount: "0.00", 
            minDiscountRequired: "0.00",
            pointsExpirationDays: 365,
            pointsPerSignup: 100,
            pointsPerReview: 10,
        });
        return (await db.select().from(loyaltySettings).limit(1))[0];
    }
    
    return settings[0];
}

export async function updateLoyaltySettings(data: any) {
    const db = await getDb();
    if (!db) throw new Error("Database not available");

    const updateData: any = {};
    
    if (data.enabled !== undefined) updateData.enabled = data.enabled;
    if (data.conversionRatePoints !== undefined) updateData.conversionRatePoints = data.conversionRatePoints;
    if (data.conversionRateMoney !== undefined) updateData.conversionRateMoney = data.conversionRateMoney.toString();
    if (data.redemptionRatePoints !== undefined) updateData.redemptionRatePoints = data.redemptionRatePoints;
    if (data.redemptionRateMoney !== undefined) updateData.redemptionRateMoney = data.redemptionRateMoney.toString();
    if (data.maxDiscountAmount !== undefined) updateData.maxDiscountAmount = data.maxDiscountAmount.toString();
    if (data.minCartAmount !== undefined) updateData.minCartAmount = data.minCartAmount.toString();
    if (data.minDiscountRequired !== undefined) updateData.minDiscountRequired = data.minDiscountRequired.toString();
    if (data.pointsExpirationDays !== undefined) updateData.pointsExpirationDays = data.pointsExpirationDays;
    if (data.pointsPerSignup !== undefined) updateData.pointsPerSignup = data.pointsPerSignup;
    if (data.pointsPerReview !== undefined) updateData.pointsPerReview = data.pointsPerReview;

    await db.update(loyaltySettings).set(updateData);
    return (await db.select().from(loyaltySettings).limit(1))[0];
}

// =================================================================
// 2. LÓGICA DE CÁLCULO
// =================================================================

export async function calculateLoyaltyPoints(subtotal: number, userId: number): Promise<number> {
    if (!userId || subtotal <= 0) return 0;
    try {
        const settings = await getLoyaltySettings();
        if (!settings.enabled) return 0;

        const moneyBase = parseFloat(settings.conversionRateMoney || "1.00");
        const pointsBase = settings.conversionRatePoints || 1;

        if (moneyBase <= 0) return 0;
        return Math.floor(subtotal / moneyBase) * pointsBase;
    } catch (error) {
        console.error("Erro ao calcular pontos de fidelidade:", error);
        return 0;
    }
}

// =================================================================
// 3. CLIENTES FIDELIDADE (RELATÓRIO ADMIN)
// =================================================================

export async function getLoyaltyCustomers(params: {
    page: number;
    limit: number;
    search?: string;
}) {
    const db = await getDb();
    if (!db) throw new Error("Database not available");

    const offset = (params.page - 1) * params.limit;
    const conditions = [];

    if (params.search) {
        const term = `%${params.search}%`;
        conditions.push(or(like(users.name, term), like(users.email, term)));
    }

    const whereClause = conditions.length > 0 ? and(...conditions) : undefined;
    
    const pointsSubQuery = db
        .select({
            userId: loyaltyHistory.userId,
            points: sql<number>`CAST(SUM(${loyaltyHistory.pointsChange}) AS SIGNED)`.as('points_total'),
        })
        .from(loyaltyHistory)
        .groupBy(loyaltyHistory.userId)
        .as('ph');
        
    const spentSubQuery = db
        .select({
            userId: orders.userId,
            totalSpent: sum(orders.total).as('spent_total'),
        })
        .from(orders)
        .groupBy(orders.userId)
        .as('os');

    const dataQuery = db
        .select({
            id: users.id,
            name: users.name,
            email: users.email,
            points: sql<number>`COALESCE(${pointsSubQuery.points}, 0)`,
            totalSpent: sql<string>`CAST(COALESCE(${spentSubQuery.totalSpent}, '0.00') AS CHAR)`,
            lastActivity: users.lastSignedIn,
        })
        .from(users)
        .leftJoin(pointsSubQuery, eq(users.id, pointsSubQuery.userId))
        .leftJoin(spentSubQuery, eq(users.id, spentSubQuery.userId))
        .orderBy(desc(sql`COALESCE(${pointsSubQuery.points}, 0)`)) 
        .where(whereClause)
        .limit(params.limit)
        .offset(offset);

    const countQuery = db.select({ value: count() }).from(users).where(whereClause);
    const [items, totalResult] = await Promise.all([dataQuery, countQuery]);

    return {
        items: items.map(item => ({
            ...item,
            totalSpent: item.totalSpent || "0.00",
            points: item.points || 0,
        })),
        total: Number(totalResult[0].value),
        totalPages: Math.ceil(Number(totalResult[0].value) / params.limit),
    };
}

export async function getCustomerHistory(userId: number) {
    const db = await getDb();
    if (!db) throw new Error("Database not available");
    return db.select()
        .from(loyaltyHistory)
        .where(eq(loyaltyHistory.userId, userId))
        .orderBy(desc(loyaltyHistory.createdAt));
}

// =================================================================
// 4. MÉTODOS PÚBLICOS / PERFIL DO USUÁRIO
// =================================================================

/**
 * Busca o saldo de pontos do usuário com soma manual para garantir precisão de tipos.
 */
export async function getUserPoints(userId: number) {
    const db = await getDb();
    if (!db) return { current_points: 0, lifetime_points: 0 };

    try {
        const history = await db.select()
            .from(loyaltyHistory)
            .where(eq(loyaltyHistory.userId, userId));

        let current = 0;
        let lifetime = 0;

        history.forEach(row => {
            const p = Number(row.pointsChange) || 0;
            current += p;
            if (p > 0) lifetime += p;
        });

      return { current_points: current,
      lifetime_points: lifetime,
      points: current,      // Nome comum
      balance: current,     // Nome comum
      total: current        // Nome comum
    };
    } catch (error) {
      return { current_points: 0, lifetime_points: 0 };
    }
}

export async function getUserLoyaltyPoints(userId: number) {
    return getUserPoints(userId);
}

export async function getLoyaltyHistory(userId: number, limit: number = 10) {
    const db = await getDb();
    if (!db) return [];
    try {
        return await db.select()
            .from(loyaltyHistory)
            .where(eq(loyaltyHistory.userId, userId))
            .orderBy(desc(loyaltyHistory.createdAt))
            .limit(limit);
    } catch (error) {
       
        return [];
    }
}

export async function addPoints(userId: number, points: number, reason: string) {
    const db = await getDb();
    if (!db) return false;
    try {
        await db.insert(loyaltyHistory).values({
            userId,
            pointsChange: points,
            reason,
            createdAt: new Date()
        });
       
        return true;
    } catch (e) {
        console.error("[Loyalty] Erro ao adicionar pontos:", e);
        return false;
    }
}

--- ARQUIVO: media-library.ts ---
/**
 * Sistema de gerenciamento de biblioteca de imagens (Media Library)
 * Upload de imagens para S3 e gerenciamento de metadados
 */

import { eq, desc } from "drizzle-orm";
import { getDb } from "./db";
// ✅ CORREÇÃO: Troca media_library pelo nome correto 'mediaLibrary'
import { mediaLibrary } from "../drizzle/schema"; 
import { storagePut } from "./storage"; // Presumindo que 'storage.ts' existe

// Tipos base
export type MediaLibraryItem = typeof mediaLibrary.$inferSelect;
export type InsertMediaLibraryItem = typeof mediaLibrary.$inferInsert;

/**
 * Gera nome único para arquivo
 */
function generateUniqueFilename(originalFilename: string): string {
  const timestamp = Date.now();
  const randomStr = Math.random().toString(36).substring(2, 8);
  // Garante que a extensão seja tratada de forma segura
  const parts = originalFilename.split('.');
  const extension = parts.length > 1 ? parts.pop() : 'bin'; 
  return `${timestamp}-${randomStr}.${extension}`;
}

/**
 * Faz upload de imagem para S3 e salva metadados no banco
 */
export async function uploadImage(data: {
  file: Buffer | Uint8Array;
  originalFilename: string;
  mimeType: string;
  uploadedBy: number;
  fileSize: number; // Adicionado para inserção no DB
  altText?: string;
}): Promise<MediaLibraryItem> {
  const db = await getDb();
  if (!db) {
    throw new Error("Database not available");
  }

  try {
    // Gerar nome único para o arquivo
    const filename = generateUniqueFilename(data.originalFilename);
    const fileKey = `media-library/${filename}`;

    // Upload para S3
    // NOTE: A função 'storagePut' precisa ser ajustada para retornar o URL final, se for o caso.
    const { url } = await storagePut(data.file, fileKey, data.mimeType); 

    // Salva metadados no banco
    const [inserted] = await db.insert(mediaLibrary).values({
      url,
      fileName: filename,
      mimeType: data.mimeType,
      size: data.fileSize,
      altText: data.altText,
      uploadedBy: data.uploadedBy,
    });
    // .returning(); // Se o seu Drizzle suportar

    // Busca o item inserido se o .returning() não for suportado
    const [newItem] = await db.select().from(mediaLibrary).where(eq(mediaLibrary.url, url)).limit(1);

    return newItem;
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("[MediaLibrary] Error uploading image:", error);
    throw error;
  }
}

/**
 * Lista todas as imagens da biblioteca
 */
export async function listMediaLibrary(): Promise<MediaLibraryItem[]> {
  const db = await getDb(); // ✅ CORREÇÃO: Usar getDb()
  if (!db) {
    throw new Error("Database not available");
  }

  try {
    // ✅ CORREÇÃO: Usar mediaLibrary (camelCase)
    return await db.select().from(mediaLibrary).orderBy(desc(mediaLibrary.createdAt)); 
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("[MediaLibrary] Error listing media:", error);
    throw error;
  }
}

/**
 * Busca imagem por ID
 */
export async function getMediaById(id: number): Promise<MediaLibraryItem | null> {
  const db = await getDb(); // ✅ CORREÇÃO: Usar getDb()
  if (!db) {
    throw new Error("Database not available");
  }

  try {
    // ✅ CORREÇÃO: Usar mediaLibrary (camelCase)
    const results = await db.select().from(mediaLibrary).where(eq(mediaLibrary.id, id)).limit(1); 

    return results.length > 0 ? results[0] : null;
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("[MediaLibrary] Error getting media:", error);
    throw error;
  }
}

/**
 * Deleta imagem da biblioteca
 */
export async function deleteMedia(id: number): Promise<{ success: boolean }> {
  const db = await getDb(); // ✅ CORREÇÃO: Usar getDb()
  if (!db) {
    throw new Error("Database not available");
  }

  try {
    // ✅ CORREÇÃO: Usar mediaLibrary (camelCase)
    await db.delete(mediaLibrary).where(eq(mediaLibrary.id, id)); 
    return { success: true };
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("[MediaLibrary] Error deleting media:", error);
    throw error;
  }
}

--- ARQUIVO: order.js ---
// server/order.ts
import { eq, and } from "drizzle-orm";
import { getDb } from "./db.js";
import { 
  orders, 
  orderItems, 
  cartItems as cartItemsTable, 
  carts, 
  loyaltyHistory 
} from "../drizzle/schema.js";
import { sendOrderEmail } from "./email.js";

export async function createOrder(input: any, user: any) {
  const db = await getDb();
  if (!db) throw new Error("Database not available");

  // Iniciamos a transação para garantir integridade total
  return await db.transaction(async (tx) => {
    
    // 1. Inserir o Pedido Principal
    const [orderResult] = await tx.insert(orders).values({
      userId: user.id,
      status: 'pending', // Começa como pendente até aprovação (se houver pagamento online)
      total: String(input.total),
      subtotal: String(input.subtotal),
      shippingCost: String(input.shippingCost),
      paymentMethod: input.paymentMethod,
      // addressSnapshot guarda o endereço como era no momento da compra (segurança jurídica)
      addressSnapshot: typeof input.address === 'string' ? input.address : JSON.stringify(input.address),
      idempotencyKey: input.idempotencyKey,
      trafficSource: input.trafficSource || 'direto',
      createdAt: new Date(),
    });

    const orderId = orderResult.insertId;

    // 2. Mover itens do Carrinho Ativo para o Histórico do Pedido
    const currentItems = await tx.select()
      .from(cartItemsTable)
      .where(eq(cartItemsTable.userId, user.id));

    if (currentItems.length === 0) {
      throw new Error("Carrinho vazio");
    }

    for (const item of currentItems) {
      await tx.insert(orderItems).values({
        orderId: orderId,
        dishId: item.dishId,
        packageId: item.packageId,
        quantity: item.quantity,
        price: item.unitPrice,
        accompaniments: item.accompaniments, // Snapshot dos acompanhamentos
      });
    }

    // 🏆 3. Lógica de Fidelidade (Cálculo de Pontos)
    // Regra: 1 ponto por R$ 1,00 gasto no subtotal
    const pointsEarned = Math.floor(parseFloat(input.subtotal));
    
    // Registrar ganho
    await tx.insert(loyaltyHistory).values({
      userId: user.id,
      pointsChange: pointsEarned,
      type: 'earned',
      description: `Pontos ganhos no pedido #${orderId}`,
      createdAt: new Date(),
    });

    // Registrar gasto (se o cliente usou pontos como desconto)
    if (input.usedLoyaltyPoints && input.usedLoyaltyPoints > 0) {
      await tx.insert(loyaltyHistory).values({
        userId: user.id,
        pointsChange: -Math.abs(input.usedLoyaltyPoints),
        type: 'burned',
        description: `Desconto usado no pedido #${orderId}`,
        createdAt: new Date(),
      });
    }

    // 4. Limpeza: Deleta os itens e marca o carrinho como completado
    await tx.delete(cartItemsTable).where(eq(cartItemsTable.userId, user.id));
    await tx.update(carts)
      .set({ status: 'completed' })
      .where(and(eq(carts.userId, user.id), eq(carts.status, 'active')));

    // 📧 5. Disparo de E-mail (Assíncrono)
    // Não usamos 'await' aqui para o cliente não ficar esperando o servidor de e-mail responder
    sendOrderEmail(user.email, {
      orderId,
      total: input.total,
      pointsEarned,
      itemsCount: currentItems.length
    }).catch(err => console.error("Falha ao enviar e-mail de confirmação:", err));

    return { 
      success: true, 
      orderId, 
      pointsEarned 
    };
  });
}

--- ARQUIVO: order.ts ---
// server/order.ts
// Lógica para Finalizar Pedidos (Checkout)

import { z } from "zod";
import { getDb } from "./db.js";
import { TRPCError } from "@trpc/server";
import { eq, and } from "drizzle-orm";
// ✅ Importando schemas reais
import { orders } from "../drizzle/schema.js"; 

// TIPAGEM DE INPUT DO CHECKOUT
// Sincronizada com o que o Cart.tsx envia no handleFinalizeOrder
const createOrderInputSchema = z.object({
    cartId: z.number(),
    shippingType: z.enum(['delivery', 'pickup']),
    selectedAddressId: z.number().optional().nullable(),
    shippingCost: z.number(), // Vem do frontend ou recalculado
    paymentMethod: z.string(),
    notes: z.string().optional().nullable(),
    changeFor: z.number().optional().nullable(),
    loyaltyDiscount: z.number().optional().default(0), 
    // ✅ NOVO CAMPO: Desconto do meio de pagamento
    paymentDiscount: z.number().optional().default(0),
});

type CreateOrderInput = z.infer<typeof createOrderInputSchema>;

/**
 * Finaliza o pedido (transforma o Carrinho em Pedido Real).
 */
export async function createOrder(input: CreateOrderInput) {
    const db = await getDb();
    if (!db) {
        throw new TRPCError({ code: 'INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR', message: "Falha na conexão com o banco de dados." });
    }

    const parsedInput = createOrderInputSchema.parse(input);
    const { 
        cartId, 
        shippingType, 
        shippingCost, 
        paymentMethod, 
        notes, 
        changeFor, 
        loyaltyDiscount,
        paymentDiscount 
    } = parsedInput;

    // 1. Buscar o carrinho atual no banco para garantir integridade do subtotal
    const [cart] = await db
        .select()
        .from(orders)
        .where(and(eq(orders.id, cartId), eq(orders.status, "pending")))
        .limit(1);

    if (!cart) {
        throw new TRPCError({ 
            code: 'NOT_FOUND', 
            message: "Carrinho não encontrado ou pedido já finalizado." 
        });
    }

    // 2. Cálculos Finais (Server-Side)
    const subtotal = Number(cart.subtotal || 0);
    
    // O campo 'discount' no banco pode já ter valor de cupom aplicado anteriormente?
    // Vamos assumir que 'cart.discount' é o cupom. Somamos tudo para o registro final.
    const currentCouponDiscount = Number(cart.discount || 0);
    const totalDiscount = currentCouponDiscount + loyaltyDiscount + paymentDiscount;

    // Cálculo do Total Final
    // Math.max(0, ...) impede valores negativos
    const finalTotal = Math.max(0, subtotal + shippingCost - totalDiscount);

    // Formata observações com troco, se houver
    let finalNotes = notes || "";
    if (changeFor && changeFor > 0) {
        finalNotes += ` (Troco para: R$ ${changeFor.toFixed(2)})`;
    }

    // 3. Atualizar o registro no Banco (Transição de Carrinho -> Pedido)
    try {
        await db.update(orders).set({
            status: "placed", // ou "awaiting_confirmation", "new" dependendo do seu fluxo
            
            // Valores Financeiros (Convertendo para string decimal para o banco)
            shippingCost: shippingCost.toFixed(2),
            discount: totalDiscount.toFixed(2),
            total: finalTotal.toFixed(2),
            
            // Dados de Entrega e Pagamento
            shippingAddressId: shippingType === 'delivery' ? selectedAddressId : null,
            paymentMethod: paymentMethod,
            
            // Metadados
            observation: finalNotes.trim() || null,
            updated_at: new Date(),
            
            // Se você tiver uma coluna específica para tipo de entrega, use-a.
            // Caso contrário, pode salvar no 'observation' ou criar a coluna.
            // Exemplo: type: shippingType 
        })
        .where(eq(orders.id, cartId));

        // 4. Retorna o pedido atualizado
        const [updatedOrder] = await db.select().from(orders).where(eq(orders.id, cartId));
        
        console.log(`✅ PEDIDO FINALIZADO: ID ${updatedOrder.id} | Total R$ ${updatedOrder.total}`);
        
        return updatedOrder;

    } catch (error: any) {
        console.error("Erro ao finalizar pedido:", error);
        throw new TRPCError({ 
            code: 'INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR', 
            message: "Erro ao processar o pedido: " + error.message
        });
    }
}

--- ARQUIVO: packages.test.ts ---
import { describe, it, expect, beforeAll, afterAll } from "vitest";
import {
  createPackage,
  getAllPackages,
  getPackageWithOptions,
  updatePackage,
  deletePackage,
} from "./packages";

describe("Packages API", () => {
  let createdPackageId: number;
  const timestamp = Date.now();

  const testPackageData = {
    name: "Pacote Teste",
    slug: `pacote-teste-${timestamp}`,
    description: "Pacote para testes",
    image_url: "https://example.com/image.jpg",
    base_price: "99.90",
    number_of_options: 3,
    month: "2025-01",
  };

  it("should create a new package", async () => {
    const result = await createPackage(testPackageData);
    expect(result).toBeDefined();
    createdPackageId = (result as any)[0];
  });

  it("should get all packages", async () => {
    const packages = await getAllPackages();
    expect(Array.isArray(packages)).toBe(true);
    expect(packages.length).toBeGreaterThan(0);
  });

  it("should get package by ID with options", async () => {
    const pkg = await getPackageWithOptions(createdPackageId);
    expect(pkg).toBeDefined();
    expect(pkg?.name).toBe(testPackageData.name);
    expect(pkg?.base_price).toBe(testPackageData.base_price);
    expect(Array.isArray(pkg?.options)).toBe(true);
  });

  it("should update package", async () => {
    const updateData = {
      name: "Pacote Teste Atualizado",
      description: "Descrição atualizada",
    };
    await updatePackage(createdPackageId, updateData);

    const updated = await getPackageWithOptions(createdPackageId);
    expect(updated?.name).toBe(updateData.name);
    expect(updated?.description).toBe(updateData.description);
  });

  it("should delete package", async () => {
    await deletePackage(createdPackageId);

    // Verify it's deleted by checking if it returns null
    const deleted = await getPackageWithOptions(createdPackageId);
    expect(deleted).toBeNull();
  });
});


--- ARQUIVO: packages.ts ---
// server/packages.ts
import { eq } from "drizzle-orm";
import { getDb } from "./db";
import { 
  packages, 
  packageOptions, 
  packageOptionDishes, 
  packageOptionGroups,
  accompanimentGroups,
  dishes,
} from "../drizzle/schema";

// --- FUNÇÕES DE PACOTES ---

export async function getAllPackages() {
  const db = await getDb();
  if (!db) throw new Error("DB Off");
  return db.select().from(packages).orderBy(packages.createdAt);
}

export async function getPackageWithOptions(packageId: number) {
  const db = await getDb();
  const pkg = await db.select().from(packages).where(eq(packages.id, packageId)).limit(1);
  if (!pkg[0]) return null;

  const options = await db.select().from(packageOptions)
    .where(eq(packageOptions.packageId, packageId))
    .orderBy(packageOptions.optionOrder);

  const optionsWithDetails = await Promise.all(options.map(async (opt) => {
    const optDishes = await db.select({ id: dishes.id, name: dishes.name })
      .from(packageOptionDishes)
      .innerJoin(dishes, eq(packageOptionDishes.dishId, dishes.id))
      .where(eq(packageOptionDishes.optionId, opt.id));

    const optGroups = await db.select({ id: accompanimentGroups.id, name: accompanimentGroups.name })
      .from(packageOptionGroups)
      .innerJoin(accompanimentGroups, eq(packageOptionGroups.groupId, accompanimentGroups.id))
      .where(eq(packageOptionGroups.optionId, opt.id));

    return { ...opt, dishes: optDishes, accompanimentGroups: optGroups };
  }));

  return { ...pkg[0], options: optionsWithDetails };
}

export async function createFullPackage(data: any) {
  const db = await getDb();
  const res = await db.insert(packages).values({
    name: data.name,
    slug: data.slug,
    description: data.description,
    imageUrl: data.imageUrl,
    price: data.basePrice.toString(), 
    numberOfOptions: data.numberOfOptions,
    month: data.month,
    isActive: true,
  });
  // Retorno compatível com MySQL/Postgres
  const id = (res as any).insertId || (res as any)[0]?.insertId || (res as any)[0]?.id;
  return { success: true, packageId: id };
}

export async function updatePackage(id: number, data: any) {
  const db = await getDb();
  await db.update(packages).set({
    name: data.name,
    slug: data.slug,
    description: data.description,
    imageUrl: data.imageUrl,
    price: data.basePrice ? data.basePrice.toString() : undefined,
    numberOfOptions: data.numberOfOptions,
    month: data.month,
    isActive: data.isActive,
    updated_at: new Date(),
  }).where(eq(packages.id, id));
  return { success: true };
}

export async function deletePackage(id: number) {
  const db = await getDb();
  return db.delete(packages).where(eq(packages.id, id));
}

// --- FUNÇÕES DE OPÇÕES E VÍNCULOS ---

export async function createPackageOption(data: { packageId: number, name: string, optionOrder?: number }) {
  const db = await getDb();
  await db.insert(packageOptions).values(data);
  return { success: true };
}

export async function deletePackageOption(optionId: number) {
  const db = await getDb();
  // Limpeza em cascata manual para evitar erro de chave estrangeira
  await db.delete(packageOptionDishes).where(eq(packageOptionDishes.optionId, optionId));
  await db.delete(packageOptionGroups).where(eq(packageOptionGroups.optionId, optionId));
  await db.delete(packageOptions).where(eq(packageOptions.id, optionId));
  return { success: true };
}

export async function addDishesToOption(optionId: number, dishIds: number[]) {
  const db = await getDb();
  await db.delete(packageOptionDishes).where(eq(packageOptionDishes.optionId, optionId));
  if (dishIds.length > 0) {
    await db.insert(packageOptionDishes).values(dishIds.map(id => ({ optionId, dishId: id })));
  }
  return { success: true };
}

export async function addGroupsToOption(optionId: number, groupIds: number[]) {
  const db = await getDb();
  // ✅ CORRIGIDO: Removido referência a 'package_dishes' inexistente
  await db.delete(packageOptionGroups).where(eq(packageOptionGroups.optionId, optionId));
  if (groupIds.length > 0) {
    await db.insert(packageOptionGroups).values(groupIds.map(id => ({ optionId, groupId: id })));
  }
  return { success: true };
}

--- ARQUIVO: payment.test.ts ---
import { describe, expect, it } from "vitest";
import {
  PaymentMethodSchema,
  FoodCardBrandSchema,
} from "./payment";

/**
 * Testes para sistema de pagamento
 */
describe("Payment System", () => {
  describe("Payment Method Schema Validation", () => {
    it("should validate payment method with required fields", () => {
      const validMethod = {
        name: "Dinheiro",
        description: "Pagamento em dinheiro na entrega",
        icon: "💵",
        is_active: true,
        display_order: 1,
      };

      const result = PaymentMethodSchema.parse(validMethod);
      expect(result.name).toBe("Dinheiro");
      expect(result.is_active).toBe(true);
    });

    it("should validate payment method with minimal fields", () => {
      const minimalMethod = {
        name: "Pix",
      };

      const result = PaymentMethodSchema.parse(minimalMethod);
      expect(result.name).toBe("Pix");
      expect(result.is_active).toBe(true);
    });

    it("should reject payment method with empty name", () => {
      const invalidMethod = {
        name: "",
      };

      expect(() => PaymentMethodSchema.parse(invalidMethod)).toThrow();
    });

    it("should reject payment method with name exceeding max length", () => {
      const invalidMethod = {
        name: "A".repeat(101),
      };

      expect(() => PaymentMethodSchema.parse(invalidMethod)).toThrow();
    });
  });

  describe("Food Card Brand Schema Validation", () => {
    it("should validate food card brand with required fields", () => {
      const validBrand = {
        name: "Ticket Alimentação",
        type: "va" as const,
        logo_url: "https://example.com/logo.png",
        is_active: true,
      };

      const result = FoodCardBrandSchema.parse(validBrand);
      expect(result.name).toBe("Ticket Alimentação");
      expect(result.type).toBe("va");
    });

    it("should validate VR type", () => {
      const vrBrand = {
        name: "Sodexo Refeição",
        type: "vr" as const,
      };

      const result = FoodCardBrandSchema.parse(vrBrand);
      expect(result.type).toBe("vr");
    });

    it("should reject invalid brand type", () => {
      const invalidBrand = {
        name: "Invalid Brand",
        type: "invalid" as any,
      };

      expect(() => FoodCardBrandSchema.parse(invalidBrand)).toThrow();
    });

    it("should reject brand with empty name", () => {
      const invalidBrand = {
        name: "",
        type: "va" as const,
      };

      expect(() => FoodCardBrandSchema.parse(invalidBrand)).toThrow();
    });
  });

  describe("Payment Methods", () => {
    it("should have standard payment methods", () => {
      const standardMethods = [
        "Dinheiro",
        "Pix",
        "Débito",
        "Crédito",
        "VA/VR",
      ];

      expect(standardMethods).toContain("Dinheiro");
      expect(standardMethods).toContain("Pix");
      expect(standardMethods).toContain("Débito");
      expect(standardMethods).toContain("Crédito");
      expect(standardMethods).toContain("VA/VR");
    });

    it("should have correct display order", () => {
      const methods = [
        { name: "Dinheiro", display_order: 1 },
        { name: "Pix", display_order: 2 },
        { name: "Débito", display_order: 3 },
        { name: "Crédito", display_order: 4 },
        { name: "VA/VR", display_order: 5 },
      ];

      expect(methods[0].display_order).toBe(1);
      expect(methods[4].display_order).toBe(5);
    });
  });

  describe("Food Card Brands", () => {
    it("should have VA brands", () => {
      const vaBrands = [
        "Ticket Alimentação",
        "Sodexo Alimentação",
        "Alelo Alimentação",
      ];

      expect(vaBrands.length).toBe(3);
      expect(vaBrands).toContain("Ticket Alimentação");
    });

    it("should have VR brands", () => {
      const vrBrands = [
        "Ticket Refeição",
        "Sodexo Refeição",
        "Alelo Refeição",
      ];

      expect(vrBrands.length).toBe(3);
      expect(vrBrands).toContain("Ticket Refeição");
    });

    it("should distinguish between VA and VR types", () => {
      const vaBrand = { type: "va" as const };
      const vrBrand = { type: "vr" as const };

      expect(vaBrand.type).not.toBe(vrBrand.type);
    });
  });

  describe("Payment Method Selection", () => {
    it("should select cash payment", () => {
      const selectedMethod = "Dinheiro";
      expect(selectedMethod).toBe("Dinheiro");
    });

    it("should select PIX payment", () => {
      const selectedMethod = "Pix";
      expect(selectedMethod).toBe("Pix");
    });

    it("should select debit card payment", () => {
      const selectedMethod = "Débito";
      expect(selectedMethod).toBe("Débito");
    });

    it("should select credit card payment", () => {
      const selectedMethod = "Crédito";
      expect(selectedMethod).toBe("Crédito");
    });

    it("should select food card payment", () => {
      const selectedMethod = "VA/VR";
      expect(selectedMethod).toBe("VA/VR");
    });
  });

  describe("Food Card Brand Selection", () => {
    it("should select VA brand", () => {
      const selectedBrand = {
        name: "Ticket Alimentação",
        type: "va" as const,
      };

      expect(selectedBrand.type).toBe("va");
    });

    it("should select VR brand", () => {
      const selectedBrand = {
        name: "Sodexo Refeição",
        type: "vr" as const,
      };

      expect(selectedBrand.type).toBe("vr");
    });
  });

  describe("Payment Validation Rules", () => {
    it("should require payment method selection", () => {
      const paymentData = {
        method: null,
      };

      expect(paymentData.method).toBeNull();
    });

    it("should validate payment method exists", () => {
      const validMethods = ["Dinheiro", "Pix", "Débito", "Crédito", "VA/VR"];
      const selectedMethod = "Dinheiro";

      expect(validMethods).toContain(selectedMethod);
    });

    it("should validate food card brand when VA/VR is selected", () => {
      const selectedMethod = "VA/VR";
      const selectedBrand = "Ticket Alimentação";

      expect(selectedMethod).toBe("VA/VR");
      expect(selectedBrand).toBeTruthy();
    });
  });

  describe("Payment Method Icons", () => {
    it("should have icons for all payment methods", () => {
      const methods = [
        { name: "Dinheiro", icon: "💵" },
        { name: "Pix", icon: "📱" },
        { name: "Débito", icon: "💳" },
        { name: "Crédito", icon: "💳" },
        { name: "VA/VR", icon: "🍽️" },
      ];

      expect(methods.every((m) => m.icon)).toBe(true);
    });
  });

  describe("Order Payment Recording", () => {
    it("should record payment method in order", () => {
      const order = {
        id: 1,
        payment_method: "Dinheiro",
      };

      expect(order.payment_method).toBe("Dinheiro");
    });

    it("should update order payment method", () => {
      let order = {
        id: 1,
        payment_method: "Dinheiro",
      };

      order.payment_method = "Pix";

      expect(order.payment_method).toBe("Pix");
    });

    it("should track payment method history", () => {
      const paymentHistory = [
        { orderId: 1, method: "Dinheiro", timestamp: new Date() },
        { orderId: 2, method: "Pix", timestamp: new Date() },
        { orderId: 3, method: "Crédito", timestamp: new Date() },
      ];

      expect(paymentHistory.length).toBe(3);
      expect(paymentHistory[0].method).toBe("Dinheiro");
    });
  });

  describe("Payment Delivery Information", () => {
    it("should indicate payment on delivery", () => {
      const paymentInfo = {
        type: "on_delivery",
        description: "Pagamento realizado na entrega",
      };

      expect(paymentInfo.type).toBe("on_delivery");
    });

    it("should list accepted payment methods", () => {
      const acceptedMethods = [
        "Dinheiro",
        "Pix",
        "Débito",
        "Crédito",
        "VA/VR",
      ];

      expect(acceptedMethods.length).toBe(5);
    });
  });
});


--- ARQUIVO: payment.ts ---
// ARQUIVO: server/payment.ts (Completo e Corrigido)

import { eq, and, desc, asc } from "drizzle-orm";
import { getDb } from "./db";
// ✅ CORREÇÃO: Usa 'paymentMethods' e 'foodCardBrands' (camelCase)
import { paymentMethods, foodCardBrands, orders } from "../drizzle/schema"; 
import { z } from "zod";

// Tipos base
export type PaymentMethod = typeof paymentMethods.$inferSelect;
export type FoodCardBrand = typeof foodCardBrands.$inferSelect;

// =========================================================================
// 1. MÉTODOS DE PAGAMENTO (Frontend/Geral)
// =========================================================================

/**
 * Lista todos os métodos de pagamento ativos.
 */
export async function listActivePaymentMethods(): Promise<PaymentMethod[]> {
    const db = await getDb();
    if (!db) throw new Error("Database not available");

    return db
        .select()
        .from(paymentMethods)
        .where(eq(paymentMethods.isActive, true))
        .orderBy(asc(paymentMethods.displayOrder));
}

/**
 * Retorna os detalhes de um método de pagamento específico.
 */
export async function getPaymentMethodById(id: number): Promise<PaymentMethod | null> {
    const db = await getDb();
    if (!db) throw new Error("Database not available");

    const [method] = await db.select().from(paymentMethods).where(eq(paymentMethods.id, id)).limit(1);
    
    return method || null;
}

// =========================================================================
// 2. VALIDAÇÃO DE CARTÃO-REFEIÇÃO (Frontend)
// =========================================================================

/**
 * Lista todas as marcas de cartão-refeição.
 */
export async function listFoodCardBrands(): Promise<FoodCardBrand[]> {
    const db = await getDb();
    if (!db) throw new Error("Database not available");

    return db
        .select()
        .from(foodCardBrands)
        .where(eq(foodCardBrands.isActive, true))
        .orderBy(asc(foodCardBrands.name));
}

/**
 * Valida se a marca de cartão-refeição é aceita.
 */
export async function validateFoodCardBrand(brandName: string): Promise<{ isValid: boolean; message: string }> {
    const brands = await listFoodCardBrands();
    const accepted = brands.some(brand => brand.name.toLowerCase() === brandName.toLowerCase());

    if (accepted) {
        return { isValid: true, message: "Marca de cartão aceita." };
    }
    
    return { isValid: false, message: "Marca de cartão não aceita." };
}

// =========================================================================
// 3. ADMIN (CRUD simplificado para métodos de pagamento)
// =========================================================================

/**
 * Lista todos os métodos de pagamento (incluindo inativos) para o admin.
 */
export async function listAllPaymentMethods(): Promise<PaymentMethod[]> {
    const db = await getDb();
    if (!db) throw new Error("Database not available");

    return db.select().from(paymentMethods).orderBy(asc(paymentMethods.name));
}

--- ARQUIVO: paymentMethods.ts ---
// server/paymentMethods.ts

import { getDb } from "./db.js";
import { paymentMethods, foodCardBrands } from "../drizzle/schema.js"; 
import { eq, asc } from "drizzle-orm";

// Tipos inferidos do Drizzle (camelCase)
export type PaymentMethod = typeof paymentMethods.$inferSelect;

// --- LEITURA ---

export async function getAllPaymentMethods() {
    const db = await getDb();
    if (!db) throw new Error("Database not available"); 
    
    const result = await db.select()
        .from(paymentMethods)
        .orderBy(asc(paymentMethods.displayOrder), asc(paymentMethods.name));

    // ✅ TRATAMENTO: Converte Decimal para Number para o tRPC/Frontend
    return result.map(m => ({
        ...m,
        id: Number(m.id),
        discountPercentage: Number(m.discountPercentage || 0),
        isActive: Boolean(m.isActive)
    }));
}

export async function getActivePaymentMethods() {
    const db = await getDb();
    if (!db) throw new Error("Database not available"); 
    
    const result = await db.select()
        .from(paymentMethods)
        .where(eq(paymentMethods.isActive, true)) 
        .orderBy(asc(paymentMethods.displayOrder));

    return result.map(m => ({
        ...m,
        id: Number(m.id),
        discountPercentage: Number(m.discountPercentage || 0),
        isActive: true
    }));
}

export async function getPaymentMethodById(id: number) {
    const db = await getDb();
    if (!db) throw new Error("Database not available"); 
    
    const result = await db.select()
        .from(paymentMethods)
        .where(eq(paymentMethods.id, id));
        
    if (!result[0]) return null;

    return {
        ...result[0],
        id: Number(result[0].id),
        discountPercentage: Number(result[0].discountPercentage || 0),
        isActive: Boolean(result[0].isActive)
    };
}

// --- ESCRITA ---

export async function createPaymentMethod(data: any) {
    const db = await getDb();
    if (!db) throw new Error("Database not available"); 

    // ✅ MYSQL: Usamos insertId do resultado em vez de .returning()
    const [result] = await db.insert(paymentMethods).values({
        name: data.name,
        isActive: data.isActive ?? true, 
        discountPercentage: data.discountPercentage ? String(data.discountPercentage) : "0.00",
        displayOrder: data.displayOrder ?? 0,
        description: data.description || null,
        icon: data.icon || null,
        brandName: data.brandName || null,
        brandLogoUrl: data.brandLogoUrl || null,
        // Caso seu schema use 'type', mantenha, senão remova:
        // type: data.type || "cash" 
    } as any); 
    
    return { success: true, id: result.insertId };
}

export async function updatePaymentMethod(id: number, data: any) {
    const db = await getDb();
    if (!db) throw new Error("Database not available"); 

    const updateData: any = {};
    
    if (data.name !== undefined) updateData.name = data.name;
    if (data.isActive !== undefined) updateData.isActive = data.isActive;
    if (data.discountPercentage !== undefined) updateData.discountPercentage = String(data.discountPercentage);
    if (data.displayOrder !== undefined) updateData.displayOrder = data.displayOrder;
    if (data.description !== undefined) updateData.description = data.description;
    if (data.icon !== undefined) updateData.icon = data.icon;
    if (data.brandName !== undefined) updateData.brandName = data.brandName;
    if (data.brandLogoUrl !== undefined) updateData.brandLogoUrl = data.brandLogoUrl;

    await db.update(paymentMethods)
        .set({
            ...updateData,
            updated_at: new Date()
        })
        .where(eq(paymentMethods.id, id));
        
    return { success: true };
}

export async function deletePaymentMethod(id: number) {
    const db = await getDb();
    if (!db) throw new Error("Database not available"); 
    
    try {
        await db.delete(paymentMethods).where(eq(paymentMethods.id, id));
        return { success: true };
    } catch (e) {
        throw new Error("Não é possível excluir. Este método pode estar vinculado a pedidos. Tente desativar.");
    }
}

export async function listFoodCardBrands() {
    const db = await getDb();
    if (!db) throw new Error("Database not available"); 
    
    return await db.select().from(foodCardBrands).orderBy(asc(foodCardBrands.name));
}

--- ARQUIVO: routers\addresses.ts ---
// server/routers/addresses.ts
import { z } from "zod";
import { router, protectedProcedure, adminProcedure, publicProcedure } from "../_core/trpc.js";
import * as CustomerAddresses from "../customer-addresses.js";
import { decrypt } from "../encryption.js";
import axios from "axios";

// --- SCHEMAS DE VALIDAÇÃO ---
const AddressInput = z.object({
  label: z.string().optional().nullable(),
  street: z.string().min(1, "Rua é obrigatória"),
  number: z.string().optional().nullable(),
  complement: z.string().optional().nullable(),
  neighborhood: z.string().optional().nullable(),
  city: z.string().optional().nullable(),
  state: z.string().optional().nullable(),
  zipCode: z.string().min(1, "CEP é obrigatório"),
  phone: z.string().optional().nullable(),
  isDefault: z.boolean().optional(),
});

// --- HELPERS DE LIMPEZA E CRIPTOGRAFIA ---
function safeDecrypt(val: any) {
  if (!val) return val;
  try {
    // Verifica se o valor tem o formato de criptografia (contém ':')
    if (typeof val === 'string' && val.includes(':')) {
      const decrypted = decrypt(val);
      return decrypted || val;
    }
    return val;
  } catch {
    return val;
  }
}

function toFront(addr: any) {
  if (!addr) return addr;
  
  const cleanStreet = safeDecrypt(addr.address || addr.street);
  
  return {
    ...addr,
    // ✅ CORREÇÃO: Agora o label passa pela descriptografia
    label: safeDecrypt(addr.label), 
    
    street: cleanStreet,
    address: cleanStreet,
    number: safeDecrypt(addr.number),
    complement: safeDecrypt(addr.complement),
    neighborhood: safeDecrypt(addr.neighborhood),
    city: safeDecrypt(addr.city),
    state: safeDecrypt(addr.state),
    zipCode: safeDecrypt(addr.zipCode),
    phone: safeDecrypt(addr.phone),
  };
}

function toDb(input: any, userId: number) {
  return {
    userId,
    label: input.label ?? "Endereço",
    address: input.street, 
    number: input.number ?? "",
    complement: input.complement ?? "",
    neighborhood: input.neighborhood ?? "",
    city: input.city ?? "",
    state: input.state ?? "",
    zipCode: input.zipCode,
    phone: input.phone ?? "",
    isDefault: input.isDefault ?? false,
  };
}

// --- ROUTER ---
export const addressesRouter = router({
  getCep: publicProcedure
    .input(z.object({ cep: z.string() }))
    .query(async ({ input }) => {
      const cleanCep = input.cep.replace(/\D/g, "");
      if (cleanCep.length !== 8) return null;
      try {
        const { data } = await axios.get(`https://viacep.com.br/ws/${cleanCep}/json/`);
        if (data.erro) return null;
        return { 
          street: data.logradouro, 
          neighborhood: data.bairro, 
          city: data.localidade, 
          state: data.uf 
        };
      } catch { return null; }
    }),

  list: protectedProcedure.query(async ({ ctx }) => {
    const list = await CustomerAddresses.listAddressesByUserId(ctx.user.id);
    return list.map(toFront);
  }),

  getDefault: protectedProcedure.query(async ({ ctx }) => {
    const addr = await CustomerAddresses.getDefaultAddress(ctx.user.id);
    return addr ? toFront(addr) : null;
  }),

  create: protectedProcedure
    .input(AddressInput)
    .mutation(async ({ ctx, input }) => {
      const res = await CustomerAddresses.createAddress(toDb(input, ctx.user.id));
      return toFront(res);
    }),

  update: protectedProcedure
    .input(z.object({ id: z.coerce.number(), data: AddressInput.partial() }))
    .mutation(async ({ ctx, input }) => {
      const patch = { ...input.data } as any;
      if (input.data.street) patch.address = input.data.street;
      
      const res = await CustomerAddresses.updateAddress(input.id, ctx.user.id, patch);
      return toFront(res);
    }),

  setDefault: protectedProcedure
    .input(z.object({ id: z.coerce.number() }))
    .mutation(async ({ ctx, input }) => {
      return await CustomerAddresses.setDefaultAddress(ctx.user.id, input.id);
    }),

  delete: protectedProcedure
    .input(z.object({ id: z.coerce.number() }))
    .mutation(async ({ ctx, input }) => {
      return await CustomerAddresses.deleteAddress(input.id, ctx.user.id);
    }),

  // Administração
  admin: router({
    list: adminProcedure
      .input(z.object({ userId: z.number() }))
      .query(async ({ input }) => {
        const list = await CustomerAddresses.listAddressesByUserId(input.userId);
        return list.map(toFront);
      }),

    create: adminProcedure
      .input(z.object({ userId: z.number(), data: AddressInput }))
      .mutation(async ({ input }) => {
        const res = await CustomerAddresses.createAddress(toDb(input.data, input.userId));
        return toFront(res);
      }),

    update: adminProcedure
      .input(z.object({ userId: z.number(), id: z.number(), data: AddressInput.partial() }))
      .mutation(async ({ input }) => {
        const patch = { ...input.data } as any;
        if (input.data.street) patch.address = input.data.street;
        
        const res = await CustomerAddresses.updateAddress(input.id, input.userId, patch);
        return toFront(res);
      }),

    delete: adminProcedure
      .input(z.object({ userId: z.number(), id: z.number() }))
      .mutation(async ({ input }) => {
        return await CustomerAddresses.deleteAddress(input.id, input.userId);
      }),
  })
});

--- ARQUIVO: routers\admin\coupons.ts ---
// server/routers/admin/coupons.ts (Versão Definitiva para MySQL/Drizzle)

import { z } from "zod";
import { router, adminProcedure } from "../../_core/trpc";
import { getDb } from "../../db"; 
import { coupons } from "../../../drizzle/schema"; 
import { eq, desc, InferSelectModel } from "drizzle-orm"; 


// =========================================================
// ESQUEMAS
// =========================================================

type Coupon = InferSelectModel<typeof coupons>;

// 1. Schema de Entrada para CRIAÇÃO/EDIÇÃO (Payload vindo do Frontend)
const couponInputSchema = z.object({
    code: z.string().min(3).max(50),
    discountType: z.enum(["percentage", "fixed"]),
    discount_value: z.number().positive(), // Espera Number

    // ✅ CORRIGIDO: Usamos .nullish() para aceitar number, null ou undefined
    minOrderValue: z.number().nullish(),
    maxDiscount: z.number().nullish(),
    
    // ✅ CORRIGIDO: Usamos .nullish() para aceitar number, null ou undefined
    usageLimit: z.number().int().nullish(),
    
    // ✅ CORRIGIDO: Aceita string (datetime-local), null ou undefined
    validFrom: z.string().nullish(),
    validUntil: z.string().nullish(),
    
    description: z.string().nullish(),
    isActive: z.boolean().default(true),
});


// =========================================================
// UTILS INTERNOS
// =========================================================

// Função para limpar e converter string de data/hora para objeto Date
const cleanDate = (val: string | null | undefined): Date | null => {
    return (val && val.trim() !== '') ? new Date(val) : null;
};


// =========================================================
// ROTAS DO ROTEADOR
// =========================================================

export const adminCouponsRouter = router({

    // 1. LISTAGEM DE CUPONS
    list: adminProcedure.query(async () => {
        const db = await getDb();
        if (!db) throw new Error("Database connection is unavailable.");
        const couponsList = await db.select().from(coupons).orderBy(desc(coupons.createdAt));
        return couponsList;
    }),

    // 2. CRIAÇÃO DE CUPOM
    create: adminProcedure
        .input(couponInputSchema)
        .mutation(async ({ input }) => {
            const db = await getDb();
            if (!db) throw new Error("Database connection is unavailable.");

            // 1. Verifica duplicidade de código
            const existingCoupon = await db.select({ id: coupons.id }).from(coupons).where(eq(coupons.code, input.code));
            if (existingCoupon.length > 0) {
                throw new Error("O código do cupom já existe.");
            }

            // 2. Converte e prepara dados para o Drizzle (tratando undefined/nullish)
            const dataToInsert = {
                code: input.code,
                description: input.description || null,
                discountType: input.discountType,
                
                // Converte number para string decimal
                discount_value: input.discount_value.toFixed(2), 
                
                // Conversão segura para valores opcionais (usa ? para verificar se é Number)
                minOrderValue: input.minOrderValue ? input.minOrderValue.toFixed(2) : null,
                maxDiscount: input.maxDiscount ? input.maxDiscount.toFixed(2) : null,
                
                usageLimit: input.usageLimit || null,
                isActive: input.isActive,
                
                // Conversão segura para datas
                validFrom: cleanDate(input.validFrom),
                validUntil: cleanDate(input.validUntil),
            };

            try {
                // ✅ CORREÇÃO MYSQL: Não usamos .returning()
                await db.insert(coupons).values(dataToInsert); 
                return { success: true };
            } catch (error) {
                console.error("Erro ao inserir cupom:", error);
                throw new Error("Falha interna ao criar cupom. Verifique logs do servidor.");
            }
        }),

    // 3. EDIÇÃO DE CUPOM (Usado para o toggleActive no Frontend)
    update: adminProcedure
        .input(couponInputSchema.extend({ id: z.number() })) 
        .mutation(async ({ input }) => {
            const db = await getDb();
            if (!db) throw new Error("Database connection is unavailable.");

            const existingCoupon = await db.select({ id: coupons.id }).from(coupons).where(eq(coupons.code, input.code));
            if (existingCoupon.length > 0 && existingCoupon[0].id !== input.id) {
                throw new Error("O código do cupom já existe em outro registro.");
            }

            const dataToUpdate = {
                code: input.code,
                description: input.description || null,
                discountType: input.discountType,
                discount_value: input.discount_value.toFixed(2), 
                
                minOrderValue: input.minOrderValue ? input.minOrderValue.toFixed(2) : null,
                maxDiscount: input.maxDiscount ? input.maxDiscount.toFixed(2) : null,
                
                usageLimit: input.usageLimit || null,
                isActive: input.isActive,
                
                validFrom: cleanDate(input.validFrom),
                validUntil: cleanDate(input.validUntil),
            };
            
            try {
                await db.update(coupons).set(dataToUpdate).where(eq(coupons.id, input.id));
                return { success: true };
            } catch (error) {
                console.error("Erro ao atualizar cupom:", error);
                throw new Error("Falha interna ao atualizar cupom.");
            }
        }),

    // 4. DELEÇÃO DE CUPOM
    delete: adminProcedure
        .input(z.object({ id: z.number() }))
        .mutation(async ({ input }) => {
            const db = await getDb();
            if (!db) throw new Error("Database connection is unavailable.");

            try {
                await db.delete(coupons).where(eq(coupons.id, input.id));
                return { success: true };
            } catch (error) {
                console.error("Erro ao deletar cupom:", error);
                throw new Error("Falha interna ao deletar cupom.");
            }
        }),
});

--- ARQUIVO: routers\admin\discountRules.ts ---
// server/routers/admin/discountRules.ts

import { z } from "zod";
import { router, adminProcedure } from "../../_core/trpc.js";
import { 
    createDiscountRuleInput, 
    listDiscountRules,
    createDiscountRule,
    updateDiscountRule,
    deleteDiscountRule
} from "../../discountRules.js"; 

export const adminDiscountRulesRouter = router({
  // 1) Listar todas as regras
  list: adminProcedure.query(async () => {
    return await listDiscountRules();
  }),

  // 2) Criar nova regra
  create: adminProcedure
    .input(createDiscountRuleInput)
    .mutation(async ({ input }) => {
      return await createDiscountRule(input);
    }),

  // 3) Atualizar regra existente
  // ✅ MELHORIA: Usando partial() para permitir atualizações parciais com segurança
  update: adminProcedure
    .input(
      createDiscountRuleInput.partial().extend({ 
        id: z.number() 
      })
    )
    .mutation(async ({ input }) => {
      const { id, ...data } = input;
      // O data aqui conterá apenas os campos enviados (name, discount_value, etc.)
      return await updateDiscountRule(id, data);
    }),

  // 4) Deletar regra
  delete: adminProcedure
    .input(z.object({ id: z.number() }))
    .mutation(async ({ input }) => {
      return await deleteDiscountRule(input.id);
    }),
});

import { z } from "zod";
import { router, adminProcedure } from "../../_core/trpc.js"; 
import * as AdminDishes from "../../admin-dishes.js"; 
import * as AdminSizes from "../../admin-sizes-accompaniments.js"; 

// --- SCHEMAS DE VALIDAÇÃO ---

const DishUpdateSchema = z.object({
  id: z.number(),
  name: z.string().optional(),
  description: z.string().optional(),
  price: z.number().optional(), 
  imageUrl: z.string().optional().nullable(),
  isActive: z.boolean().optional(),
  categoryId: z.number().optional(),
  displayOrder: z.number().optional(),
  isFeatured: z.boolean().optional(),
  nutritionalInfo: z.any().optional().nullable(), 
});

const DishCreateSchema = DishUpdateSchema.omit({ id: true });

export const adminDishesRouter = router({
  // --- GESTÃO DE PRATOS ---

  list: adminProcedure
    .input(z.object({ 
      page: z.number().default(1), 
      perPage: z.number().default(8), 
      search: z.string().nullish(), 
      categoryId: z.number().nullish(), 
      isActive: z.boolean().nullish() 
    }))
    .query(async ({ input }) => {
      return await AdminDishes.getPaginatedDishes({ 
        page: input.page, 
        limit: input.perPage, 
        search: input.search ?? undefined, 
        categoryId: input.categoryId ?? undefined, 
        isActive: input.isActive ?? undefined 
      });
    }),

  getById: adminProcedure
    .input(z.object({ id: z.number() }))
    .query(async ({ input }) => {
      return (await AdminDishes.getDishById(input.id)) as any;
    }),

  create: adminProcedure
    .input(
      DishCreateSchema.required({ 
        name: true, 
        price: true 
      })
    )
    .mutation(async ({ input }) => {
      return await AdminDishes.createDish(input);
    }),

  update: adminProcedure
    .input(DishUpdateSchema)
    .mutation(async ({ input }) => {
      const { id, ...data } = input;
      return await AdminDishes.updateDish(id, data);
    }),

  delete: adminProcedure
    .input(z.object({ id: z.number() }))
    .mutation(async ({ input }) => {
      return await AdminDishes.deleteDish(input.id);
    }),

  // ✅ CORREÇÃO AQUI: Adicionado o prefixo 'AdminDishes.'
  toggleActive: adminProcedure
    .input(z.object({ id: z.number(), isActive: z.boolean() }))
    .mutation(async ({ input }) => {
      // Chamando a função a partir do namespace importado
      return await AdminDishes.toggleDishStatus(input.id, input.isActive);
    }),

  updateImage: adminProcedure
    .input(z.object({ 
      id: z.number(), 
      imageUrl: z.string().nullable() 
    }))
    .mutation(async ({ input }) => {
      return await AdminDishes.updateDish(input.id, { imageUrl: input.imageUrl });
    }),

  // --- GESTÃO DE CATEGORIAS ---

  listCategories: adminProcedure
    .query(async () => {
      return await AdminDishes.getLocalCategories();
    }),

  createCategory: adminProcedure
    .input(z.object({ name: z.string() }))
    .mutation(async ({ input }) => {
      // Certifique-se que essa função existe no seu admin-dishes.js
      return await AdminDishes.createLocalCategory(input.name);
    }),
});

    removeAccompanimentGroup: adminProcedure.input(z.object({ sizeId: z.number(), groupId: z.number() })).mutation(async ({ input }) => await AdminSizes.unlinkAccompanimentFromSize(input.sizeId, input.groupId)),

export const adminCouponsRouter = router({
    list: adminProcedure.query(async () => await Coupon.listCoupons()),
    
    // ROTA CREATE CORRIGIDA
    create: adminProcedure
        .input(z.object({ 
            code: z.string(), 
            // ✅ CORRIGIDO: Usar .nullish() para aceitar string, null, ou undefined
            description: z.string().nullish(), 
            discountType: z.enum(["percentage", "fixed"]), 
            discount_value: z.number(), 
            
            // ✅ CORRIGIDO: Usar .nullish() para aceitar number, null, ou undefined
            minOrderValue: z.number().nullish(), 
            maxDiscount: z.number().nullish(), 
            usageLimit: z.number().int().nullish(), 
            
            // ✅ CORRIGIDO: Usar z.string().nullish() para datas (Frontend envia string | null)
            validFrom: z.string().nullish(), 
            validUntil: z.string().nullish(),
            
            // ✅ CORRIGIDO: Adicionado isActive ao schema de criação (Frontend estava enviando)
            isActive: z.boolean().optional().default(true),
        }))
        .mutation(async ({ input }) => await Coupon.createCoupon(input)),
    
    // ROTA UPDATE CORRIGIDA
    update: adminProcedure
        .input(z.object({ 
            id: z.number(), 
            code: z.string().optional(),
            
            // ✅ CORRIGIDO: Usar .nullish()
            description: z.string().nullish(), 
            discountType: z.enum(["percentage", "fixed"]).optional(), 
            discount_value: z.number().optional(), 
            
            // ✅ CORRIGIDO: Usar .nullish()
            minOrderValue: z.number().nullish(), 
            maxDiscount: z.number().nullish(), 
            usageLimit: z.number().int().nullish(), 
            
            // ✅ CORRIGIDO: Usar z.string().nullish() para datas
            validFrom: z.string().nullish(), 
            validUntil: z.string().nullish(), 
            
            // ✅ CORRIGIDO: is active já aceita optional
            isActive: z.boolean().optional() 
        }))
        .mutation(async ({ input }) => { 
            const { id, ...data } = input; 
            return await Coupon.updateCoupon(id, data); 
        }),
    
    delete: adminProcedure
