--- ARQUIVO: routers\admin\media.ts ---
import { z } from "zod";
import { adminProcedure, router } from "../../_core/trpc"; 
import { getDb } from "../../db"; 
import { media } from "../../db/media"; 
import { desc, eq } from "drizzle-orm";
import fs from "fs/promises";
import path from "path";

const UPLOADS_DIR = path.join(process.cwd(), "client", "public", "uploads");

export const mediaRouter = router({
  // --- LISTAGEM ---
  list: adminProcedure.query(async () => {
    try {
      // ✅ COM AWAIT
      const db = await getDb(); 
      return await db.select().from(media).orderBy(desc(media.id));
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("ERRO AO LISTAR MÍDIA:", error);
      throw new Error("Erro de banco de dados ao listar mídia.");
    }
  }),

  // --- UPLOAD ---
  upload: adminProcedure
    .input(z.object({ 
      filename: z.string(), 
      mimeType: z.string(), 
      base64Data: z.string() 
    }))
    .mutation(async ({ input }) => {
      try {
        // Garante que a pasta existe
        try { await fs.access(UPLOADS_DIR); } 
        catch { await fs.mkdir(UPLOADS_DIR, { recursive: true }); }

        const fileExt = path.extname(input.filename);
        const uniqueName = `${Date.now()}-${Math.round(Math.random() * 1e9)}${fileExt}`;
        const filePath = path.join(UPLOADS_DIR, uniqueName);
        
        await fs.writeFile(filePath, Buffer.from(input.base64Data, "base64"));
        
        const fileUrl = `/uploads/${uniqueName}`;
        
        // ✅ COM AWAIT (O erro estava aqui)
        const db = await getDb(); 

        const [result]: any = await db.insert(media).values({
          url: fileUrl,
          originalFilename: input.filename,
          mimeType: input.mimeType,
          filePath: filePath,
        });

        return { success: true, id: result.insertId, url: fileUrl };
      } catch (error) {
        console.error("ERRO NO UPLOAD:", error);
        throw new Error("Falha ao processar upload.");
      }
    }),

  // --- DELETE ---
  delete: adminProcedure
    .input(z.object({ id: z.number() }))
    .mutation(async ({ input }) => {
      // ✅ COM AWAIT
      const db = await getDb(); 
      
      const [item] = await db.select().from(media).where(eq(media.id, input.id));
      
      if (item) {
        try { await fs.unlink(item.filePath); } catch {}
        await db.delete(media).where(eq(media.id, input.id));
      }
      return { success: true };
    }),
});

--- ARQUIVO: routers\admin\packages.ts ---
// server/routers/admin/packages.ts
import { z } from "zod";
import { router, adminProcedure } from "../../_core/trpc.js";
import { getDb } from "../../db.js";
import { eq, desc } from "drizzle-orm";
import * as PackagesLogic from "../../packages.js"; 

import {
  packages,
  packageOptions,
  packageOptionDishes,
  packageOptionGroups,
  dishes,
  accompanimentGroups,
} from "../../../drizzle/schema.js";

export const adminPackagesRouter = router({
  // 1) Listar pacotes
  list: adminProcedure.query(async () => {
    const db = await getDb();
    const result = await db.select().from(packages).orderBy(desc(packages.createdAt));
    
    // ✅ Mapeia 'price' (banco) para 'base_price' (frontend)
    return result.map(pkg => ({
      ...pkg,
      base_price: pkg.price 
    }));
  }),

  // 2) Obter detalhes de um pacote específico
  get: adminProcedure
    .input(z.object({ id: z.number() }))
    .query(async ({ input }) => {
      const db = await getDb();
      const pkgRows = await db.select().from(packages).where(eq(packages.id, input.id)).limit(1);
      const pkg = pkgRows[0];
      if (!pkg) return null;

      // Busca as opções vinculadas ao pacote
      const options = await db.select().from(packageOptions)
        .where(eq(packageOptions.packageId, input.id))
        .orderBy(packageOptions.optionOrder);

      // Busca os detalhes (pratos e grupos) de cada opção
      const optionsWithDetails = await Promise.all(
        options.map(async (opt) => {
          const optDishes = await db.select({ id: dishes.id, name: dishes.name })
            .from(packageOptionDishes)
            .innerJoin(dishes, eq(packageOptionDishes.dishId, dishes.id))
            .where(eq(packageOptionDishes.optionId, opt.id));

          const optGroups = await db.select({ id: accompanimentGroups.id, name: accompanimentGroups.name })
            .from(packageOptionGroups)
            .innerJoin(accompanimentGroups, eq(packageOptionGroups.groupId, accompanimentGroups.id))
            .where(eq(packageOptionGroups.optionId, opt.id));

          return { ...opt, dishes: optDishes, accompanimentGroups: optGroups };
        })
      );

      return { 
        ...pkg, 
        base_price: pkg.price, // ✅ Mapeia para o formulário
        options: optionsWithDetails 
      };
    }),
    
  // 3) Criar novo pacote
  create: adminProcedure
    .input(z.object({
      name: z.string().min(1),
      slug: z.string().min(1),
      description: z.string().optional().nullable(),
      image_url: z.string().optional().nullable(),
      base_price: z.string().min(1), 
      number_of_options: z.number().int().min(0),
      month: z.string().optional().nullable(),
      isActive: z.boolean().optional(),
    }))
    .mutation(async ({ input }) => {
      const db = await getDb();
      const now = new Date();
      
      const res = await db.insert(packages).values({
        name: input.name,
        slug: input.slug,
        description: input.description,
        imageUrl: input.image_url,
        price: input.base_price, // ✅ Mapeia base_price -> price (schema)
        numberOfOptions: input.number_of_options,
        month: input.month,
        isActive: input.isActive ?? true,
        createdAt: now,
        updated_at: now,
      } as any);

      const insertId = (res as any).insertId ?? (res as any)[0]?.insertId;
      return { success: true, id: insertId };
    }),

  // 4) Atualizar pacote existente
  update: adminProcedure
    .input(z.object({
      id: z.number(),
      name: z.string().min(1),
      slug: z.string().min(1),
      description: z.string().optional().nullable(),
      image_url: z.string().optional().nullable(),
      base_price: z.string().min(1),
      number_of_options: z.number().int().min(0),
      month: z.string().optional().nullable(),
      isActive: z.boolean().optional(),
    }))
    .mutation(async ({ input }) => {
      const db = await getDb();
      const { id, ...data } = input;

      await db.update(packages).set({
        name: data.name,
        slug: data.slug,
        description: data.description,
        imageUrl: data.image_url,
        price: data.base_price, // ✅ Mapeia base_price -> price (schema)
        numberOfOptions: data.number_of_options,
        month: data.month,
        isActive: data.isActive,
        updated_at: new Date(),
      } as any).where(eq(packages.id, id));

      return { success: true };
    }),

  // 5) Deletar pacote
  delete: adminProcedure
    .input(z.object({ id: z.number() }))
    .mutation(async ({ input }) => {
      return await PackagesLogic.deletePackage(input.id);
    }),

  // --- GERENCIAMENTO DE OPÇÕES ---

  createOption: adminProcedure
    .input(z.object({ packageId: z.number(), name: z.string().min(1), optionOrder: z.number().optional() }))
    .mutation(async ({ input }) => {
      const db = await getDb();
      await db.insert(packageOptions).values(input);
      return { success: true };
    }),

  removeOption: adminProcedure
    .input(z.object({ optionId: z.number() }))
    .mutation(async ({ input }) => {
      return await PackagesLogic.deletePackageOption(input.optionId);
    }),

  addDishesToOption: adminProcedure
    .input(z.object({ optionId: z.number(), dishIds: z.array(z.number()) }))
    .mutation(async ({ input }) => {
      return await PackagesLogic.addDishesToOption(input.optionId, input.dishIds);
    }),

  addAccompanimentsToOption: adminProcedure
    .input(z.object({ optionId: z.number(), groupIds: z.array(z.number()) }))
    .mutation(async ({ input }) => {
      const db = await getDb();
      await db.delete(packageOptionGroups).where(eq(packageOptionGroups.optionId, input.optionId));
      
      if (input.groupIds.length > 0) {
        for (const gId of input.groupIds) {
          await db.insert(packageOptionGroups).values({
            optionId: input.optionId,
            groupId: gId
          } as any);
        }
      }
      return { success: true };
    }),

  getDishes: adminProcedure.query(async () => {
    const db = await getDb();
    return await db.select().from(dishes).orderBy(dishes.name);
  }),

  getAccompanimentGroups: adminProcedure.query(async () => {
    const db = await getDb();
    return await db.select().from(accompanimentGroups).orderBy(accompanimentGroups.name);
  }),
});

--- ARQUIVO: routers\admin\users.ts ---
import { z } from "zod";
import { eq, desc, sql, sum, like, or } from 'drizzle-orm'; 

import { router, adminProcedure } from "../../_core/trpc"; 
import { getDb } from "../../db"; 
// ✅ Importação das funções de criptografia
import { decrypt } from "../../encryption"; 

import { 
    users, 
    user_profiles,
    customerAddresses as customer_addresses, 
    loyaltyHistory, 
    orders 
} from "../../../drizzle/schema"; 

// =========================================================
// UTILITIES: HELPER DE DESCRIPTOGRAFIA SEGURO
// =========================================================

function safeDecrypt(val: any): string | null {
    if (!val || typeof val !== 'string') return val || null;
    
    // Se não contiver o separador da criptografia, assume que já é texto puro
    if (!val.includes(':')) return val;

    try {
        const res = decrypt(val);
        return res || val;
    } catch (err) {
        console.error("[DECRYPT ERROR] Falha ao processar valor.");
        return val; 
    }
}

function cleanAddress(addr: any) {
    if (!addr) return addr;
    
    const rawStreet = addr.street || addr.address;
    const cleanStreet = safeDecrypt(rawStreet);

    return {
        ...addr,
        label: safeDecrypt(addr.label),
        street: cleanStreet,
        address: cleanStreet,
        number: safeDecrypt(addr.number),
        neighborhood: safeDecrypt(addr.neighborhood),
        city: safeDecrypt(addr.city),
        state: safeDecrypt(addr.state),
        zipCode: safeDecrypt(addr.zipCode),
        complement: safeDecrypt(addr.complement),
        phone: safeDecrypt(addr.phone),
        receiverName: safeDecrypt(addr.receiverName),
    };
}

// =========================================================
// ESQUEMAS E TIPAGENS (AJUSTADOS PARA EVITAR ERRO 500)
// =========================================================

const listInputSchema = z.object({
    page: z.number().optional().default(1), 
    limit: z.number().optional().default(50), 
    search: z.string().optional(),
}).optional();

const orderSchema = z.object({
    id: z.number(),
    status: z.string(),
    total: z.string(),
    createdAt: z.any().nullable(), // Usando any para evitar conflito de formato de data
});

const detailsResponseSchema = z.object({
    user: z.object({
        id: z.number(),
        email: z.string(),
        name: z.string().nullable(),
        role: z.string(), 
        customerDocument: z.string().nullable(), 
        lastSignedIn: z.any().nullable(),
        createdAt: z.any().nullable(),
    }),
    profile: z.object({
        phone: z.string().nullable(),
        zipCode: z.string().nullable(),
        totalSpent: z.string().nullable(),
        loyaltyPoints: z.number().nullable(),
    }).nullable(),
    addresses: z.array(z.any()), // ✅ Obrigatório para o Modal carregar a aba de endereços
    recentOrders: z.array(orderSchema), 
});

// =========================================================
// ROTAS DO ROTEADOR
// =========================================================

export const adminUsersRouter = router({

    // 1. LISTAGEM DE USUÁRIOS
    list: adminProcedure
        .input(listInputSchema)
        .query(async ({ input }) => {
            const page = input?.page || 1;
            const limit = input?.limit || 50;
            const offset = (page - 1) * limit;

            const db = await getDb();
            if (!db) throw new Error("Database connection unavailable.");

            let searchCondition: any = undefined;
            if (input?.search && input.search.length > 2) {
                const term = `%${input.search}%`;
                searchCondition = or(
                    like(users.name, term),
                    like(users.email, term)
                );
            }

            try {
                const totalCountResult = await db.select({ count: sql<string>`count(*)` })
                    .from(users)
                    .where(searchCondition);
                const totalCount = parseInt(totalCountResult[0].count);

                const userList = await db.select({
                    id: users.id, 
                    email: users.email,
                    name: users.name,
                    role: users.role,
                    lastSignedIn: users.lastSignedIn,
                    createdAt: users.createdAt,
                    customerDocument: users.customerDocument, 
                })
                .from(users)
                .where(searchCondition)
                .orderBy(desc(users.createdAt))
                .limit(limit)
                .offset(offset);

                const decryptedList = userList.map(u => ({
                    ...u,
                    customerDocument: safeDecrypt(u.customerDocument),
                }));

                return { data: decryptedList, totalCount, page, limit };
            } catch (err) {
                console.error("Erro no list:", err); 
                throw new Error("Falha ao carregar lista.");
            }
        }),

    // 2. OBTER DETALHES (CORRIGIDO PARA EVITAR ERRO 500)
    getDetails: adminProcedure
        .input(z.object({ id: z.number() }))
        .output(detailsResponseSchema)
        .query(async ({ input }) => {
            const db = await getDb();
            if (!db) throw new Error("Database connection unavailable.");

            const userId = input.id;

            const [result] = await db.select({
                user: {
                    id: users.id,
                    email: users.email,
                    name: users.name,
                    role: users.role,
                    customerDocument: users.customerDocument, 
                    lastSignedIn: users.lastSignedIn,
                    createdAt: users.createdAt,
                },
                profile: {
                    phone: user_profiles.phone,
                    zipCode: user_profiles.zipCode,
                },
            })
            .from(users)
            .leftJoin(user_profiles, eq(users.id, user_profiles.userId)) 
            .where(eq(users.id, userId));

            if (!result) throw new Error("Usuário não encontrado.");

            // Busca e Limpeza de Endereços
            const rawAddresses = await db.select()
                .from(customer_addresses)
                .where(eq(customer_addresses.userId, userId));
            const cleanedAddresses = rawAddresses.map(cleanAddress);

            // Cálculos
            const loyaltySumResult = await db.select({ totalPoints: sum(loyaltyHistory.pointsChange) })
                .from(loyaltyHistory)
                .where(eq(loyaltyHistory.userId, userId));
            const totalPoints = loyaltySumResult[0]?.totalPoints ?? 0;

            const spentSumResult = await db.select({ totalSpent: sum(orders.total) })
                .from(orders)
                .where(eq(orders.userId, userId));
            const totalSpent = spentSumResult[0]?.totalSpent ? String(spentSumResult[0].totalSpent) : "0.00";

            const recentOrders = await db.select({
                id: orders.id,
                status: orders.status,
                total: orders.total,
                createdAt: orders.createdAt,
            })
            .from(orders)
            .where(eq(orders.userId, userId))
            .orderBy(desc(orders.createdAt))
            .limit(50);

            // Resposta higienizada para o Zod
            return {
                user: {
                    ...result.user,
                    customerDocument: safeDecrypt(result.user.customerDocument) || null,
                },
                profile: {
                    zipCode: safeDecrypt(result.profile?.zipCode) || null,
                    phone: safeDecrypt(result.profile?.phone || (cleanedAddresses[0]?.phone)) || null,
                    totalSpent,
                    loyaltyPoints: Number(totalPoints),
                },
                addresses: cleanedAddresses, // ✅ Agora incluído corretamente
                recentOrders: recentOrders.map(o => ({ ...o, total: String(o.total) })),
            };
        }),

    // 3. LISTA ESPECÍFICA DE ENDEREÇOS
    listAddresses: adminProcedure
        .input(z.object({ userId: z.number() }))
        .query(async ({ input }) => {
            const db = await getDb();
            const rawAddresses = await db.select()
                .from(customer_addresses)
                .where(eq(customer_addresses.userId, input.userId));

            return rawAddresses.map(cleanAddress);
        }),

    // 4. DELETAR USUÁRIO
    delete: adminProcedure
        .input(z.object({ id: z.number() }))
        .mutation(async ({ input }) => {
            const db = await getDb();
            const userId = input.id;
            try {
                await db.delete(loyaltyHistory).where(eq(loyaltyHistory.userId, userId));
                await db.delete(customer_addresses).where(eq(customer_addresses.userId, userId));
                await db.delete(user_profiles).where(eq(user_profiles.userId, userId));
                await db.delete(users).where(eq(users.id, userId));
                return { success: true };
            } catch (error) {
                console.error(`ERRO ao deletar usuário ${userId}:`, error);
                throw new Error("Falha ao deletar o usuário.");
            }
        }),

    // Stubs para evitar quebras no frontend
    updateRole: adminProcedure.input(z.any()).mutation(() => ({ success: true })),
    updateProfile: adminProcedure.input(z.any()).mutation(() => ({ success: true })),
    setPassword: adminProcedure.input(z.any()).mutation(() => ({ success: true })),
    create: adminProcedure.input(z.any()).mutation(() => ({ success: true })),
});

--- ARQUIVO: routers\admin-shipping.ts ---
// server/routers/admin-shipping.ts
import { router, publicProcedure, adminProcedure } from "../_core/trpc.js"; 
import { z } from "zod";
import { getDb } from "../db.js";
import { shippingRules, shippingSettings } from "../../drizzle/schema.js"; 
import { eq, asc, and, gte, lte } from "drizzle-orm";

export const adminShippingRouter = router({
  
  // --- CONFIGURAÇÕES GERAIS (Retirada no Local) ---
  getSettings: adminProcedure.query(async () => {
    const db = await getDb();
    if (!db) throw new Error("Database connection failed");
    
    const settings = await db.select().from(shippingSettings).limit(1);
    
    if (settings.length === 0) {
      // Cria registro inicial se não existir
      await db.insert(shippingSettings).values({ 
        pickupEnabled: 0, // Iniciamos desligado por segurança
        pickupLabel: "Retirada no Local", 
        pickupInstruction: "" 
      });
      return { pickupEnabled: false, pickupLabel: "Retirada no Local", pickupInstruction: "" };
    }

    // ✅ CORREÇÃO CRÍTICA: MariaDB retorna 0 ou 1. 
    // Forçamos a conversão para boolean real para o Switch do React não se perder.
    return {
      ...settings[0],
      pickupEnabled: settings[0].pickupEnabled === 1 || settings[0].pickupEnabled === true
    };
  }),

  updateSettings: adminProcedure
  .input(z.object({
    pickupEnabled: z.boolean(),
    pickupLabel: z.string().optional(),
    pickupInstruction: z.string().optional(),
  }))
  .mutation(async ({ input }) => {
    const db = await getDb();
    
    // 1. Converter Boolean para 0 ou 1 (Padrão MariaDB)
    const pickupValue = input.pickupEnabled ? 1 : 0;

    // 2. Tentar atualizar o registro ID 1
    const result = await db.update(shippingSettings)
      .set({
        pickupEnabled: pickupValue,
        pickupLabel: input.pickupLabel,
        pickupInstruction: input.pickupInstruction
      })
      .where(eq(shippingSettings.id, 1));

    // 3. SE nada foi atualizado (tabela vazia), criar o registro
    if (result[0].affectedRows === 0) {
      await db.insert(shippingSettings).values({
        id: 1,
        pickupEnabled: pickupValue,
        pickupLabel: input.pickupLabel || "Retirada",
        pickupInstruction: input.pickupInstruction || ""
      });
    }

    return { success: true };
  }),

  // --- REGRAS DE CEP ---
  getRules: adminProcedure.query(async () => {
    const db = await getDb();
    const rules = await db.select().from(shippingRules).orderBy(asc(shippingRules.cepStart)); 
    
    // ✅ Garantimos que o preço venha como número para o frontend
    return rules.map(rule => ({
      ...rule,
      price: parseFloat(String(rule.price || "0"))
    }));
  }),

  createRule: adminProcedure 
    .input(z.object({
      name: z.string(), 
      cepStart: z.string(), 
      cepEnd: z.string(),
      price: z.number(),
      active: z.boolean().default(true)
    }))
    .mutation(async ({ input }) => {
      const db = await getDb();
      
      await db.insert(shippingRules).values({
        name: input.name,
        cepStart: input.cepStart.replace(/\D/g, ''), 
        cepEnd: input.cepEnd.replace(/\D/g, ''),
        price: input.price.toFixed(2), // Salva como string decimal
        active: input.active ? 1 : 0
      });
      return { success: true };
    }),

  deleteRule: adminProcedure
    .input(z.object({ id: z.number() }))
    .mutation(async ({ input }) => {
      const db = await getDb();
      await db.delete(shippingRules).where(eq(shippingRules.id, input.id));
      return { success: true };
    }),

  // --- CÁLCULO DE FRETE (Público) ---
  calculate: publicProcedure
    .input(z.object({ cep: z.string() }))
    .query(async ({ input }) => {
      const db = await getDb();
      const cepClean = input.cep.replace(/\D/g, '');

      const [settings] = await db.select().from(shippingSettings).limit(1);
      
      const matchedRules = await db.select().from(shippingRules).where(
        and(
            eq(shippingRules.active, 1),
            lte(shippingRules.cepStart, cepClean),
            gte(shippingRules.cepEnd, cepClean)
        )
      );

      return {
        pickup: settings ? {
          ...settings,
          pickupEnabled: !!settings.pickupEnabled
        } : null,
        delivery: matchedRules.length > 0 ? {
            price: parseFloat(matchedRules[0].price || "0"),
            name: matchedRules[0].name
        } : null 
      };
    }),
});

--- ARQUIVO: routers\auth copy.ts ---
// server/routers/auth.ts
import { z } from "zod";
import { router, publicProcedure, protectedProcedure } from "./../_core/trpc.js";
import { getSessionCookieOptions } from "./../_core/cookies.js";
import { COOKIE_NAME, ONE_YEAR_MS } from "@shared/const";
import { sdk } from "./../_core/sdk.js";
import * as AuthPassword from "../auth-password.js";
import { decrypt } from "../encryption.js";

/**
 * Detecta se uma string parece estar no formato do nosso AES-256-GCM:
 * ivHex:authTagHex:cipherHex
 */
function looksEncryptedGcm(val: unknown): val is string {
  if (typeof val !== "string") return false;
  const s = val.trim();
  if (!s) return false;

  const parts = s.split(":");
  if (parts.length !== 3) return false;

  const [iv, tag, cipher] = parts;

  // IV = 16 bytes => 32 hex chars
  // TAG = 16 bytes => 32 hex chars
  if (!/^[0-9a-fA-F]{32}$/.test(iv)) return false;
  if (!/^[0-9a-fA-F]{32}$/.test(tag)) return false;

  // cipher precisa ser hex com tamanho par (pelo menos 2 chars)
  if (!/^[0-9a-fA-F]+$/.test(cipher)) return false;
  if (cipher.length < 2 || cipher.length % 2 !== 0) return false;

  return true;
}

/**
 * Retorna usuário seguro para o frontend:
 * - Normaliza cpf/customerDocument
 * - Se estiver criptografado, descriptografa
 */
function cleanUser(user: any) {
  if (!user) return user;

  const rawDoc = user.customerDocument ?? user.cpf ?? null;

  let doc: string | null = null;
  if (typeof rawDoc === "string" && rawDoc.trim()) {
    if (looksEncryptedGcm(rawDoc)) {
      // decrypt() já trata erro e retorna null em falha
      doc = decrypt(rawDoc) ?? rawDoc;
    } else {
      doc = rawDoc;
    }
  }

  // padroniza os dois nomes (compat com código antigo e novo)
  return {
    ...user,
    cpf: doc,
    customerDocument: doc,
  };
}

export const authRouter = router({
  /**
   * O frontend usa para verificar sessão e pegar "quem sou eu"
   */
  me: protectedProcedure.query(({ ctx }) => cleanUser(ctx.user)),

  /**
   * Mantido por compatibilidade (alguns componentes chamam getProfile)
   * OBS: seu "perfil completo" (phone, birthDate, etc) deve vir do auth.getProfile
   * do router que você criou com join em user_profiles, não daqui.
   */
  getProfile: protectedProcedure.query(({ ctx }) => cleanUser(ctx.user)),

  login: publicProcedure
    .input(z.object({ email: z.string().email(), password: z.string() }))
    .mutation(async ({ input, ctx }) => {
      const user = await AuthPassword.validateLogin(input.email, input.password);

      const sessionToken = await sdk.createSessionToken(user.openId, {
        name: String(user.name || ""),
        expiresInMs: ONE_YEAR_MS,
      });

      const cookieOptions = getSessionCookieOptions(ctx.req);
      ctx.res.cookie(COOKIE_NAME, sessionToken, {
        ...cookieOptions,
        maxAge: ONE_YEAR_MS,
      });

      return cleanUser(user);
    }),

  register: publicProcedure
    .input(
      z.object({
        email: z.string().email(),
        password: z.string(),
        name: z.string().optional(),
      })
    )
    .mutation(async ({ input, ctx }) => {
      const user = await AuthPassword.createUserWithPassword(
        input.email,
        input.password,
        input.name
      );

      const sessionToken = await sdk.createSessionToken(user.openId, {
        name: String(user.name || ""),
        expiresInMs: ONE_YEAR_MS,
      });

      const cookieOptions = getSessionCookieOptions(ctx.req);
      ctx.res.cookie(COOKIE_NAME, sessionToken, {
        ...cookieOptions,
        maxAge: ONE_YEAR_MS,
      });

      return cleanUser(user);
    }),

  logout: protectedProcedure.mutation(({ ctx }) => {
    const cookieOptions = getSessionCookieOptions(ctx.req);
    ctx.res.clearCookie(COOKIE_NAME, { ...cookieOptions, maxAge: -1 });
    return { success: true };
  }),
});


--- ARQUIVO: routers\auth.ts ---
// server/routers/auth.ts
import { router, publicProcedure, protectedProcedure } from "../_core/trpc.js";
import { z } from "zod";
import { lucia } from "./auth.js";
import { Argon2id } from "oslo/password"; // Recomendado (ou use bcrypt)
import { eq } from "drizzle-orm";
import { users } from "../drizzle/schema/users";
import { getDb } from "../db.js";
import { TRPCError } from "@trpc/server";

const argon2 = new Argon2id();

export const authRouter = router({
  login: publicProcedure
    .input(z.object({ email: z.string().email(), password: z.string() }))
    .mutation(async ({ input, ctx }) => {
      const db = await getDb();
      const user = await db.query.users.findFirst({ 
        where: eq(users.email, input.email) 
      });
      
      if (!user || !user.password) {
        throw new TRPCError({ code: "UNAUTHORIZED", message: "Credenciais inválidas" });
      }

      const validPassword = await argon2.verify(user.password, input.password);
      if (!validPassword) {
        throw new TRPCError({ code: "UNAUTHORIZED", message: "Credenciais inválidas" });
      }

      // 1. Cria a sessão na tabela 'sessions'
      const session = await lucia.createSession(user.id, {});
      
      // 2. Cria o cookie e envia para o navegador
      const cookie = lucia.createSessionCookie(session.id);
      if (ctx.res) {
        ctx.res.appendHeader("Set-Cookie", cookie.serialize());
      }

      return { success: true };
    }),

  logout: protectedProcedure.mutation(async ({ ctx }) => {
    // Apaga a sessão do banco de dados
    await lucia.invalidateSession(ctx.session.id);
    
    // Limpa o cookie do navegador
    const cookie = lucia.createBlankSessionCookie();
    ctx.res.appendHeader("Set-Cookie", cookie.serialize());
    
    return { success: true };
  }),
});

--- ARQUIVO: routers\cart.ts ---
import { z } from "zod";
import { TRPCError } from "@trpc/server";
import { router, protectedProcedure, publicProcedure } from "../_core/trpc.js";
import { getDb } from "../db.js";
import { sql } from "drizzle-orm";

// --- HELPERS DE TRATAMENTO ---

const numberOptionalCoerce = z.preprocess((v) => {
  if (v === null || v === "" || v === undefined) return undefined;
  if (typeof v === "string" && v.trim() !== "" && !Number.isNaN(Number(v))) return Number(v);
  return v;
}, z.number().optional());

function parseJsonSafe<T>(val: any, fallback: T): T {
  if (val == null || val === "") return fallback;
  if (typeof val !== "string") return val as T;
  try {
    return JSON.parse(val) as T;
  } catch {
    return fallback;
  }
}

function extractInsertId(res: any): number | null {
  if (!res) return null;
  if (Array.isArray(res) && res[0] && typeof res[0].insertId === "number") return res[0].insertId;
  if (typeof res.insertId === "number") return res.insertId;
  return null;
}

// --- LOGICA DE CARRINHO ATIVO ---

async function ensureActiveCart(db: any, userId: number) {
  const [rows]: any = await db.execute(sql`
    SELECT id, discount_value, coupon_code, shipping_value
    FROM carts
    WHERE user_id = ${userId} AND status = 'active'
    LIMIT 1
  `);

  if (rows?.length) return rows[0];

  const res: any = await db.execute(sql`
    INSERT INTO carts (user_id, status, discount_value, shipping_value)
    VALUES (${userId}, 'active', 0.00, 0.00)
  `);

  const insertId = extractInsertId(res);
  if (!insertId) throw new Error("Falha ao criar carrinho ativo.");

  return { id: insertId, discount_value: "0.00", coupon_code: null, shipping_value: "0.00" };
}

// --- ROTEADOR ---

export const cartRouter = router({
  /**
   * getActive: Lê o carrinho e retorna para o Frontend com metadados de Cupom
   */
  getActive: publicProcedure.query(async ({ ctx }) => {
    if (!ctx.user?.id) return { items: [], subtotal: 0, total: 0, discount: 0 };

    const db = await getDb();
    const userId = Number(ctx.user.id);

    try {
      const cart = await ensureActiveCart(db, userId);

      const [itemsRaw]: any = await db.execute(sql`
        SELECT 
          ci.*, 
          d.name as dish_name, d.image_url as dish_image,
          p.name as pkg_name, p.image_url as pkg_image,
          ds.name as size_name
        FROM cart_items ci
        LEFT JOIN dishes d ON d.id = ci.dish_id
        LEFT JOIN packages p ON p.id = ci.package_id
        LEFT JOIN dish_sizes ds ON ds.id = ci.size_id
        WHERE ci.cart_id = ${Number(cart.id)}
        ORDER BY ci.created_at DESC
      `);

      const items = (itemsRaw ?? []).map((r: any) => ({
        id: r.id,
        productId: r.dish_id || r.package_id,
        dishId: r.dish_id,
        packageId: r.package_id,
        sizeId: r.size_id,
        sizeName: r.size_name,
        name: r.dish_name || r.pkg_name || "Produto",
        imageUrl: r.dish_image || r.pkg_image,
        quantity: Number(r.quantity),
        unitPrice: Number(r.unit_price),
        options: parseJsonSafe(r.accompaniments, []),
        notes: r.notes,
        lineTotal: Number((Number(r.unit_price) * r.quantity).toFixed(2))
      }));

      const subtotal = Number(items.reduce((acc, it) => acc + it.lineTotal, 0).toFixed(2));
      const discount = Number(cart.discount_value || 0);
      const couponCode = cart.coupon_code;

      return {
        id: cart.id,
        items,
        subtotal,
        discount,
        // ✅ Campos essenciais para o layout do cupom aparecer:
        couponDescription: couponCode ? `Cupom ${couponCode} aplicado` : null,
        autoDiscount: 0, 
        autoDiscountName: null,
        
        minOrderAmount: 50.00,
        minOrderMessage: subtotal < 50.00 
          ? `Faltam R$ ${(50 - subtotal).toFixed(2)} para o pedido mínimo` 
          : null,
        total: Math.max(0, subtotal - discount)
      };
    } catch (e: any) {
      console.error("🔴 [getActive] Error:", e);
      throw new TRPCError({ code: "INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR", message: "Erro ao carregar carrinho" });
    }
  }),

  /**
   * addItem: Adiciona itens com logs de depuração
   */
  addItem: protectedProcedure
    .input(z.object({
      productId: numberOptionalCoerce,
      dishId: numberOptionalCoerce,
      packageId: numberOptionalCoerce,
      sizeId: numberOptionalCoerce,
      quantity: z.number().min(1).default(1),
      price: numberOptionalCoerce,
      unitPrice: numberOptionalCoerce,
      options: z.any().optional(),
      notes: z.string().optional(),
      metadata: z.any().optional()
    }))
    .mutation(async ({ ctx, input }) => {
      console.log("📥 [DEBUG BACK 1] Input recebido no tRPC:", JSON.stringify(input, null, 2));

      const db = await getDb();
      const userId = Number(ctx.user.id);
      const cart = await ensureActiveCart(db, userId);

      const dishId = input.dishId ?? input.productId ?? null;
      const packageId = input.packageId ?? null;
      const sizeId = input.sizeId ?? null;
      const finalPrice = input.unitPrice ?? input.price ?? 0;

      console.log(`💰 [DEBUG BACK 2] User: ${userId} | Cart: ${cart.id} | Price: ${finalPrice}`);

      const optionsStr = input.options ? JSON.stringify(input.options) : "";
      const notes = input.notes || "";

      const [existing]: any = await db.execute(sql`
        SELECT id, quantity FROM cart_items 
        WHERE cart_id = ${cart.id} 
          AND dish_id <=> ${dishId} 
          AND package_id <=> ${packageId} 
          AND size_id <=> ${sizeId}
          AND COALESCE(accompaniments, '') = ${optionsStr}
          AND COALESCE(notes, '') = ${notes}
        LIMIT 1
      `);

      if (existing?.length) {
        console.log("♻️ [DEBUG BACK 3] Atualizando quantidade do item existente.");
        const newQty = existing[0].quantity + input.quantity;
        await db.execute(sql`
          UPDATE cart_items 
          SET quantity = ${newQty}, unit_price = ${finalPrice} 
          WHERE id = ${existing[0].id}
        `);
        return { success: true, updated: true };
      }

      console.log("🆕 [DEBUG BACK 3] Inserindo novo item no banco.");
      await db.execute(sql`
        INSERT INTO cart_items 
        (cart_id, dish_id, package_id, size_id, quantity, unit_price, accompaniments, notes, metadata)
        VALUES 
        (
          ${cart.id}, ${dishId}, ${packageId}, ${sizeId}, 
          ${input.quantity}, ${finalPrice}, ${optionsStr || null}, 
          ${notes || null}, ${input.metadata ? JSON.stringify(input.metadata) : null}
        )
      `);

      return { success: true };
    }),

  updateItem: protectedProcedure
    .input(z.object({ id: z.number(), quantity: z.number().min(0) }))
    .mutation(async ({ ctx, input }) => {
      const db = await getDb();
      if (input.quantity === 0) {
        await db.execute(sql`DELETE FROM cart_items WHERE id = ${input.id}`);
      } else {
        await db.execute(sql`UPDATE cart_items SET quantity = ${input.quantity} WHERE id = ${input.id}`);
      }
      return { success: true };
    }),

  removeItem: protectedProcedure
    .input(z.object({ id: z.number() }))
    .mutation(async ({ ctx, input }) => {
      const db = await getDb();
      await db.execute(sql`DELETE FROM cart_items WHERE id = ${input.id}`);
      return { success: true };
    }),

  clear: protectedProcedure.mutation(async ({ ctx }) => {
    const db = await getDb();
    const userId = Number(ctx.user.id);
    const cart = await ensureActiveCart(db, userId);
    await db.execute(sql`DELETE FROM cart_items WHERE cart_id = ${cart.id}`);
    // Ao limpar o carrinho, limpamos também o cupom
    await db.execute(sql`UPDATE carts SET coupon_code = NULL, discount_value = 0.00 WHERE id = ${cart.id}`);
    return { success: true };
  })
});

--- ARQUIVO: routers\coupons.ts ---
    // server/routers/coupons.ts
    import { z } from "zod";
    import { TRPCError } from "@trpc/server";
    import { router, protectedProcedure } from "../_core/trpc.js";
    import { getDb } from "../db.js";
    import { coupons, carts } from "../../drizzle/schema/index.js"; 
    import { eq, sql } from "drizzle-orm";

    export const couponsRouter = router({
    validateCoupon: protectedProcedure
        .input(z.object({
        code: z.string(),
        subtotal: z.number()
        }))
        .mutation(async ({ ctx, input }) => {
        const db = await getDb();
        const now = new Date();

        // 1. Busca o cupom no banco
        const [coupon] = await db.select()
            .from(coupons)
            .where(eq(coupons.code, input.code))
            .limit(1);

        // 2. Validações básicas
        if (!coupon) throw new TRPCError({ code: "NOT_FOUND", message: "Cupom não encontrado." });
        if (!coupon.isActive) throw new TRPCError({ code: "BAD_REQUEST", message: "Este cupom não está mais ativo." });

        // 3. Valida Datas
        if (coupon.validFrom && now < new Date(coupon.validFrom)) 
            throw new TRPCError({ code: "BAD_REQUEST", message: "Este cupom ainda não é válido." });
        if (coupon.validUntil && now > new Date(coupon.validUntil)) 
            throw new TRPCError({ code: "BAD_REQUEST", message: "Este cupom expirou." });

        // 4. Valida Valor Mínimo
        if (coupon.minOrderValue && input.subtotal < Number(coupon.minOrderValue)) {
            throw new TRPCError({ 
            code: "BAD_REQUEST", 
            message: `Valor mínimo para este cupom é R$ ${Number(coupon.minOrderValue).toFixed(2)}` 
            });
        }

        // 5. Calcula o desconto que será gravado
        let discountAmount = 0;
        if (coupon.discountType === 'percentage') {
            discountAmount = input.subtotal * (Number(coupon.discount_value) / 100);
            // Aplica o teto de desconto se existir
            if (coupon.maxDiscount) {
            discountAmount = Math.min(discountAmount, Number(coupon.maxDiscount));
            }
        } else {
            discountAmount = Number(coupon.discount_value);
        }

        // 6. APLICA NO CARRINHO (Grava no banco)
        await db.execute(sql`
            UPDATE carts 
            SET coupon_code = ${coupon.code}, 
                discount_value = ${discountAmount.toFixed(2)}
            WHERE user_id = ${ctx.user.id} AND status = 'active'
        `);

        return { 
            isValid: true, 
            discount: discountAmount,
            description: coupon.description || `Cupom ${coupon.code} aplicado`
        };
        }),

    // Rota para remover o cupom
    removeCoupon: protectedProcedure.mutation(async ({ ctx }) => {
        const db = await getDb();
        await db.execute(sql`
        UPDATE carts 
        SET coupon_code = NULL, discount_value = 0.00 
        WHERE user_id = ${ctx.user.id} AND status = 'active'
        `);
        return { success: true };
    })
    });

// server/routers/index.ts

/**
 * 🛠️ CORREÇÃO DE CAMINHO:
 * O erro ERR_MODULE_NOT_FOUND acontecia porque o caminho estava "./src/_core/".
 * Agora aponta corretamente para fora de routers e entra em _core.
 */
import { router, publicProcedure, mergeRouters } from "../_core/trpc.js";

// === CLIENTE (ROTAS) ===
import { authRouter } from "./auth.js";
import { cartRouter } from "./cart.js";
import { addressesRouter } from "./addresses.js";
import { loyaltyRouter } from "./loyalty.js";
import { packagesRouter } from "./packages.js";
import { paymentMethodsRouter } from "./paymentMethods.js";
import { ordersRouter } from "./orders.js";
import { productsRouter } from "./products.js";
import { couponsRouter } from "./coupons.js";
import { profileRouter } from "./profile.js";

// === ADMIN (ROTAS) ===
import * as AdminDishesRouters from "./admin/dishes.js";
import { adminPackagesRouter } from "./admin/packages.js";
import { adminUsersRouter } from "./admin/users.js";
import { adminShippingRouter } from "./admin-shipping.js";
import { adminCouponsRouter } from "./admin/finance.js";
import { adminDiscountRulesRouter } from "./admin/discountRules.js";
import { adminLoyaltyRouter } from "./admin/loyalty.js";
import { adminSettingsRouter } from "./admin/settings.js";
import { mediaRouter } from "./admin/media.js";

// === LÓGICA DE TEMA ===

export const appRouter = router({
  // === GERAIS ===
  theme: router({
    get: publicProcedure.query(() => ThemeLogic.getTheme()),
  }),

  // === ROTAS DE LOJA (CLIENTE) ===
  cart: cartRouter,
  products: productsRouter,
  packages: packagesRouter,
  addresses: addressesRouter,
  loyalty: loyaltyRouter,
  paymentMethods: paymentMethodsRouter,
  coupons: couponsRouter,
  orders: ordersRouter,

  // === AUTH & SESSÃO ===
  // Aqui fundimos a lógica de autenticação (Lucia/JWT) com sub-rotas
  auth: mergeRouters(
    authRouter,             // Contém: login, register, me, logout
    router({
      cart: cartRouter,     // Permite acessar auth.cart.getActive
    })
  ),

  // === PERFIL ===
  profile: profileRouter,

  // === PÚBLICO ===
  public: router({
    dishes: router({ 
      getById: productsRouter.getById 
    }),
    packages: packagesRouter,
  }),

    dishes: AdminDishesRouters.adminDishesRouter,
    sizes: AdminDishesRouters.adminSizesRouter,

    packages: adminPackagesRouter,

    shipping: adminShippingRouter,
    coupons: adminCouponsRouter,
    discountRules: adminDiscountRulesRouter,
    paymentMethods: paymentMethodsRouter,
    loyaltySettings: adminLoyaltyRouter,
    storeSettings: adminSettingsRouter,
    orders: ordersRouter,
    media: mediaRouter,
  }),
});

export type AppRouter = typeof appRouter;

import { z } from "zod";

export const ordersRouter = router({
  // --- ROTAS DO CLIENTE (trpc.auth.orders.x) ---
  
  // Resolve o 404 do auth.orders.listMy
  listMy: protectedProcedure.query(async ({ ctx }) => {
    return await AdminOrders.listOrders({ 
      userId: ctx.user.id, 
      page: 1, 
      limit: 50 
    });
  }),

  getMyOrderDetails: protectedProcedure
    .input(z.object({ id: z.coerce.number() }))
    .query(async ({ input, ctx }) => {
      const order = await AdminOrders.getOrderById(input.id);
      if (order.order.userId !== ctx.user.id) {
        throw new TRPCError({ code: 'UNAUTHORIZED', message: "Não tens permissão para ver este pedido." });
      }
      return order;
    }),

  create: protectedProcedure.input(z.any()).mutation(async ({ input, ctx }) => {
    return await OrderLogic.createOrder(input, ctx.user);
  }),

  // --- ROTAS DE ADMIN (trpc.admin.orders.x) ---

    return await AdminOrders.listOrders(input);
  }),

  updateStatus: adminProcedure
    .input(z.object({ id: z.coerce.number(), status: z.string() }))
    .mutation(async ({ input }) => {
      return await AdminOrders.updateOrderStatus(input.id, input.status);

  getById: adminProcedure

    .query(async ({ input }) => {

    }),
});


--- ARQUIVO: routers\packages.ts ---
// server/routers/packages.ts
import { z } from "zod";
import { TRPCError } from "@trpc/server";
import { router, publicProcedure } from "../_core/trpc.js"; 
import { getDb } from "../db.js"; 
import { eq, desc } from 'drizzle-orm'; 

import { 
    packages, 
    packageOptions, 
    packageOptionDishes, 
    packageOptionGroups, // <--- A tabela pivô
    dishes, 
    accompanimentGroups,
    accompanimentOptions 
} from "../../drizzle/schema.js"; 

export const packagesRouter = router({
    list: publicProcedure
        .input(z.object({
            page: z.number().optional(),
            perPage: z.number().optional(),
        }).optional())
        .query(async () => {
            const db = await getDb();
            if (!db) return []; 
            
            try {
                return await db.select({
                    id: packages.id,
                    name: packages.name,
                    slug: packages.slug,
                    description: packages.description,
                    imageUrl: packages.imageUrl,
                    basePrice: packages.price,
                    numberOfOptions: packages.numberOfOptions,
                    month: packages.month,
                    isActive: packages.isActive,
                    createdAt: packages.createdAt,
                    updated_at: packages.updated_at,
                })
                .from(packages)
                .where(eq(packages.isActive, true)) 
                .orderBy(desc(packages.createdAt)); 
            } catch (err) {
                console.error("[DB ERROR - packages.list]:", err); 
                return [];
            }
        }),

    getById: publicProcedure
        .input(z.object({ id: z.coerce.number() }))
        .query(async ({ input }) => {
            const db = await getDb();
            if (!db) throw new TRPCError({ code: 'INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR', message: "DB indisponível" });

            try {
                // 1. Busca o Pacote
                const pkgRows = await db.select().from(packages).where(eq(packages.id, input.id)).limit(1);
                const pkg = pkgRows[0];
                
                if (!pkg || !pkg.isActive) {
                    throw new TRPCError({ code: 'NOT_FOUND', message: "Pacote não encontrado" });
                }

                // 2. Busca as Opções (ex: Proteína, Guarnição)
                const options = await db.select().from(packageOptions) 
                    .where(eq(packageOptions.packageId, input.id)) 
                    .orderBy(packageOptions.optionOrder); 

                // 3. Monta a árvore de detalhes
                const optionsWithDetails = await Promise.all(options.map(async (opt) => {
                    
                    // 3a. Pratos
                    const optDishes = await db.select({
                        id: dishes.id,
                        name: dishes.name,
                        image: dishes.imageUrl
                    })
                    .from(packageOptionDishes) 
                    .innerJoin(dishes, eq(packageOptionDishes.dishId, dishes.id))
                    .where(eq(packageOptionDishes.optionId, opt.id)); 

                    // 3b. Grupos de Acompanhamento
                    // 🚨 CORREÇÃO RADICAL: Removemos as colunas 'isRequired' e 'maxSelections' do SELECT.
                    // Se elas não existirem no schema.js, elas são 'undefined' e quebram o Drizzle.
                    const optGroupsBase = await db.select({
                        id: accompanimentGroups.id,
                        name: accompanimentGroups.name,
                        // Removido: isRequired: packageOptionGroups.isRequired,
                        // Removido: maxSelections: packageOptionGroups.maxSelections
                    })
                    .from(packageOptionGroups) 
                    .innerJoin(accompanimentGroups, eq(packageOptionGroups.groupId, accompanimentGroups.id)) 
                    .where(eq(packageOptionGroups.optionId, opt.id)); 
                    
                    const optGroups = await Promise.all(optGroupsBase.map(async (groupRow) => {
                        // 3c. Itens do grupo
                        const groupOptions = await db.select()
                            .from(accompanimentOptions)
                            .where(eq(accompanimentOptions.groupId, groupRow.id));
                            // .orderBy(...) removido por segurança

                        return {
                            id: groupRow.id,
                            name: groupRow.name,
                            options: groupOptions, 
                            // ⚠️ USANDO VALORES PADRÃO PROVISÓRIOS
                            // Isso garante que o site carregue. Depois você ajusta o schema.
                            isRequired: false, 
                            maxSelections: 1, 
                        };
                    }));

                    return { 
                        ...opt, 
                        dishes: optDishes, 
                        accompanimentGroups: optGroups 
                    };
                }));

                return { 
                    ...pkg, 
                    basePrice: pkg.price,
                    options: optionsWithDetails 
                };

            } catch (err) {
                console.error("[TRPC Error - packages.getById]:", err);
                if (err instanceof TRPCError) throw err;
                throw new TRPCError({ 
                    code: 'INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR', 
                    message: "Erro interno ao carregar pacote" 
                });
            }
        }),
});

// server/routers/paymentMethods.ts
import { router, publicProcedure, adminProcedure } from "../_core/trpc.js";
import * as PaymentMethodsLogic from "../paymentMethods.js"; 
import { z } from "zod";

// ✅ Schema unificado: Coerce garante que '20' vire 20 (número)
const paymentMethodSchema = z.object({
  name: z.string().min(1, "O nome é obrigatório"),
  isActive: z.boolean().optional().default(true),
  discountPercentage: z.coerce.number().min(0).max(100).optional().default(0),
  displayOrder: z.coerce.number().int().optional().default(0),
  description: z.string().optional().nullable(),
  icon: z.string().optional().nullable(),
  brandName: z.string().optional().nullable(),
  brandLogoUrl: z.string().optional().nullable(),
  type: z.string().optional().default("cash"),
});

export const paymentMethodsRouter = router({
  // 1) Listar ativos (Usado no Checkout)
  list: publicProcedure.query(async () => {
    return await PaymentMethodsLogic.getActivePaymentMethods();
  }),

  // 2) Listar todos (Usado na tabela do Admin)
  // Caminho final: admin.paymentMethods.listAll
  listAll: adminProcedure.query(async () => {
    return await PaymentMethodsLogic.getAllPaymentMethods();
  }),
  
  // 3) Buscar por ID
  get: publicProcedure
    .input(z.object({ id: z.coerce.number() })) // Adicionado coerce por segurança
    .query(async ({ input }) => {
      return await PaymentMethodsLogic.getPaymentMethodById(input.id);
    }),

  // --- CRUD Admin ---

  create: adminProcedure
    .input(paymentMethodSchema)
    .mutation(async ({ input }) => {
      return await PaymentMethodsLogic.createPaymentMethod(input);
    }),

  update: adminProcedure
    .input(paymentMethodSchema.partial().extend({ id: z.coerce.number() }))
    .mutation(async ({ input }) => {
      const { id, ...data } = input;
      return await PaymentMethodsLogic.updatePaymentMethod(id, data);
    }),

  delete: adminProcedure
    .input(z.object({ id: z.coerce.number() }))
    .mutation(async ({ input }) => {
      return await PaymentMethodsLogic.deletePaymentMethod(input.id);
    }),
});

// server/routers/products.ts

import * as AdminDishes from "../admin-dishes.js";

  list: publicProcedure
    .input(z.object({ 
      page: z.number().default(1), 
      perPage: z.number().default(12), 
      search: z.string().nullish(), 
      category: z.union([z.number(), z.string()]).nullish() 
    }))
    .query(async (opts) => {
      return await AdminDishes.getPaginatedDishes({ 
        page: opts.input.page, 
        limit: opts.input.perPage, 
        search: opts.input.search ?? undefined, 
        categoryId: opts.input.category ? Number(opts.input.category) : undefined, 
        isActive: true 
      });
    }),

  // 2. CATEGORIAS (Para o menu de filtros)
  categories: publicProcedure.query(async () => {
    return await AdminDishes.getLocalCategories();
  }),

  // 3. BUSCA POR ID (Aqui ele traz TUDO: macros, calorias, tags)
  getById: publicProcedure
    .input(z.object({ id: z.coerce.number() }))
    .query(async ({ input }) => {
      const dish = await AdminDishes.getDishById(input.id);
      if (!dish) throw new TRPCError({ code: 'NOT_FOUND', message: "Prato não encontrado" });
      return dish;
    }),

--- ARQUIVO: routers\profile.ts ---
// server/routers/profile.ts
import { z } from "zod";
import { eq } from "drizzle-orm";
import { TRPCError } from "@trpc/server";
import { router, protectedProcedure } from "../_core/trpc.js";
import { users, user_profiles } from "../../drizzle/schema/index.js";
import { encryptFields, decryptFields } from "../encryption.js";

// Campos sensíveis reais do user_profiles (sem customerDocument agora)
const PROFILE_PII_FIELDS = ["phone", "birthDate"] as const;

export const profileRouter = router({
  // ✅ GET perfil completo
  get: protectedProcedure.query(async ({ ctx }) => {
    const db = ctx.db;

    const rows = await db
      .select({
        id: users.id,
        email: users.email,
        name: users.name,
        customerDocument: users.customerDocument, // CPF (criptografado ou não, depende do que você salvar)
        profile: {
          phone: user_profiles.phone,
          birthDate: user_profiles.birthDate,
        },
      })
      .from(users)
      .leftJoin(user_profiles, eq(users.id, user_profiles.userId))
      .where(eq(users.id, ctx.user.id))
      .limit(1);

    if (!rows.length) {
      throw new TRPCError({ code: "NOT_FOUND", message: "Usuário não encontrado" });
    }

    const row = rows[0];

    const decryptedProfile = row.profile
      ? decryptFields(row.profile as any, PROFILE_PII_FIELDS as any)
      : { phone: null, birthDate: null };

    // CPF fica em users.customerDocument (se você criptografar ele, descreve aqui)
    // Observação: decryptFields trabalha com objeto; aqui é string simples.
    // Se você estiver criptografando o CPF como string, é melhor fazer:
    // const cpf = decrypt(row.customerDocument) ?? row.customerDocument;
    const cpf = row.customerDocument ?? null;

    return {
      id: row.id,
      email: row.email,
      name: row.name ?? "",
      cpf,
      phone: decryptedProfile.phone ?? null,
      birthDate: decryptedProfile.birthDate ?? null,
    };
  }),

  // ✅ UPDATE perfil completo
  update: protectedProcedure
    .input(
      z.object({
        name: z.string().min(2).optional(),
        cpf: z.string().optional().nullable(), // apenas números (validação no frontend ou aqui depois)
        phone: z.string().optional().nullable(),
        birthDate: z.string().optional().nullable(), // YYYY-MM-DD
      })
    )
    .mutation(async ({ ctx, input }) => {
      const db = ctx.db;

      // 1) Atualiza USERS (nome + cpf)
      if (input.name !== undefined || input.cpf !== undefined) {
        await db
          .update(users)
          .set({
            ...(input.name !== undefined ? { name: input.name } : {}),
            ...(input.cpf !== undefined ? { customerDocument: input.cpf } : {}),
            updated_at: new Date(),
          })
          .where(eq(users.id, ctx.user.id));
      }

      // 2) Atualiza USER_PROFILES (PII criptografada)
      const encryptedProfile = encryptFields(
        {
          phone: input.phone ?? null,
          birthDate: input.birthDate ?? null,
        },
        PROFILE_PII_FIELDS as any
      );

      await db
        .insert(user_profiles)
        .values({
          userId: ctx.user.id,
          ...encryptedProfile,
        })
        .onDuplicateKeyUpdate({
          set: {
            ...encryptedProfile,
            updated_at: new Date(),
          },
        });

      return { success: true };
    }),
});

--- ARQUIVO: routers\sizes.ts ---
// server/routers/sizes.ts
import { z } from "zod";
import { router, adminProcedure, publicProcedure } from "../_core/trpc.js";
import { getDb } from "../db.js";
import { sql } from "drizzle-orm";
// ✅ Importação com extensão .js obrigatória para ESM
import * as AdminSizes from "../admin-sizes-accompaniments.js";

export const sizesRouter = router({
  // 1. Listagem para Admin e Vitrine
  list: publicProcedure.query(async () => {
    return await AdminSizes.getAllDishSizes();
  }),

  // 2. Rota de Vínculos: Essencial para o mapeamento no useAdminSizes.ts
  getAccompanimentGroups: adminProcedure.query(async () => {
    const db = await getDb();
    if (!db) return [];

    // ✅ MariaDB/MySQL retorna um array onde o primeiro elemento [rows] contém os dados
    // O alias 'sizeId' e 'groupId' deve bater com o useEffect do useAdminSizes.ts
    const [rows]: any = await db.execute(sql`
      SELECT 
        size_id as sizeId, 
        accompaniment_group_id as groupId 
      FROM size_accompaniment_groups
    `);

    return Array.isArray(rows) ? rows : [];
  }),

  // 3. Ações de Vínculo (Toggle no Frontend)
  addAccompanimentGroup: adminProcedure
    .input(z.object({ 
      sizeId: z.coerce.number(), 
      groupId: z.coerce.number() 
    }))
    .mutation(async ({ input }) => {
      // ✅ Chama a lógica para inserir o vínculo na tabela de junção
      return await AdminSizes.linkAccompanimentToSize({
        sizeId: input.sizeId,
        groupId: input.groupId,
        isRequired: false // Valor padrão
      });
    }),

  removeAccompanimentGroup: adminProcedure
    .input(z.object({ 
      sizeId: z.coerce.number(), 
      groupId: z.coerce.number() 
    }))
    .mutation(async ({ input }) => {
      // ✅ Chama a lógica para remover o vínculo
      return await AdminSizes.unlinkAccompanimentFromSize(input.sizeId, input.groupId);
    }),

  // 4. CRUD de Tamanhos
  getById: adminProcedure
    .input(z.object({ id: z.coerce.number() }))
    .query(async ({ input }) => {
      return await AdminSizes.getSizeById(input.id);
    }),

  create: adminProcedure
    .input(z.object({
      name: z.string().min(1, "Nome é obrigatório"),
      priceModifier: z.coerce.number().default(0),
      weight: z.string().optional().nullable(),
    }))
    .mutation(async ({ input }) => {
      return await AdminSizes.createDishSize(input);
    }),

  update: adminProcedure
    .input(z.object({ 
      id: z.coerce.number(),
      name: z.string().optional(),
      priceModifier: z.coerce.number().optional(),
      weight: z.string().optional().nullable(),
      isActive: z.boolean().optional(),
    }).passthrough())
    .mutation(async ({ input }) => {
      const { id, ...data } = input;
      return await AdminSizes.updateDishSize(id, data);
    }),

  delete: adminProcedure
    .input(z.object({ id: z.coerce.number() }))
    .mutation(async ({ input }) => {
      return await AdminSizes.deleteDishSize(input.id);
    }),
});

// server/routers.ts

import { COOKIE_NAME, ONE_YEAR_MS } from "@shared/const";
import { getSessionCookieOptions } from "./_core/cookies";
import {
  publicProcedure,
  protectedProcedure,
  router,
  adminProcedure,
} from "./_core/trpc";
import { z } from "zod";

// --- IMPORTS DE BANCO DE DADOS ---
import { getDb } from "./db";
import { customerAddresses } from "../drizzle/schema";
import { eq } from "drizzle-orm";

// --- IMPORTS ADMIN USERS ---
import {
  listUsers,
  getUserDetails,
  updateUserProfile,
  updateUserRole,
  createUserWithProfile,
} from "./admin-users";

// --- IMPORTS DE MÓDULOS ---
import * as Coupon from "./coupon";

// 🟢 IMPORT DO NOVO ROUTER DE PACOTES

// -------------------------------------------------------------
// ROUTER DE ENDEREÇOS
// -------------------------------------------------------------

const addressesRouter = router({
  list: adminProcedure
    .input(z.object({ userId: z.number() }))
    .query(async ({ input }) => {
      const db = await getDb();
      if (!db) throw new Error("Database not available");
      return await db
        .select()
        .from(customerAddresses)
        .where(eq(customerAddresses.userId, input.userId));
    }),
});

// -------------------------------------------------------------
// SCHEMAS DE VALIDAÇÃO
// -------------------------------------------------------------

const DishUpdateSchema = z.object({
  id: z.number(),
  name: z.string().optional(),
  description: z.string().optional(),
  price: z.number().optional(), 
  imageUrl: z.string().optional().nullable(),
  isActive: z.boolean().optional(),
  categoryId: z.number().optional(),
  displayOrder: z.number().optional(),
  isFeatured: z.boolean().optional(),
});

const DishCreateSchema = DishUpdateSchema.omit({ id: true });

// -------------------------------------------------------------
// ROTAS TRPC
// -------------------------------------------------------------

export const appRouter = router({

  // 1. ROTAS DE COMPATIBILIDADE (FRONTEND CLIENTE)
  products: router({
    list: publicProcedure
      .input(z.object({
          page: z.number().default(1),
          perPage: z.number().default(12),
          search: z.string().nullish(),
          category: z.any().nullish(), 
        }))
      .query(async ({ input }) => {
        const categoryId = input.category ? Number(input.category) : undefined;
        return await AdminDishes.getPaginatedDishes({
          page: input.page,
          limit: input.perPage,
          search: input.search ?? undefined,
          categoryId: isNaN(categoryId!) ? undefined : categoryId,
          isActive: true, 
        });
      }),

    categories: publicProcedure.query(async () => {
      return await AdminDishes.getLocalCategories();
    }),
  }),

  // 2. ROTAS PÚBLICAS
  public: router({
    dishes: router({
      list: publicProcedure 
        .input(z.object({
            page: z.number().default(1),
            perPage: z.number().default(10),
            search: z.string().nullish(),
            categoryId: z.number().nullish(),
            isActive: z.boolean().nullish(),
          }))
        .query(({ input }) =>
          AdminDishes.getPaginatedDishes({
            page: input.page,
            limit: input.perPage,
            search: input.search ?? undefined,
            categoryId: input.categoryId ?? undefined,
            isActive: input.isActive ?? undefined,
          }),
        ),

      getById: publicProcedure
        .input(z.object({ id: z.number() }))
        .query(async ({ input }) => await AdminDishes.getDishById(input.id) as any),

      getSizes: publicProcedure
        .input(z.object({ dishId: z.number() }))
        .query(async ({ input }) => await AdminSizes.getSizesByDishId(input.dishId)),
      
      getSizeAccompaniments: publicProcedure
        .input(z.object({ sizeId: z.number() }))
        .query(async ({ input }) => await AdminSizes.getAccompanimentGroupsBySizeId(input.sizeId)),

      getAccompanimentOptions: publicProcedure
        .input(z.object({ groupId: z.number() }))
        .query(async ({ input }) => await AdminSizes.getAccompanimentOptionsByGroup(input.groupId)),

      categories: router({
        list: publicProcedure.query(async () => await AdminDishes.listCategories()),
      }),
      shipping: router({
        calculate: publicProcedure
          .input(z.object({ zipCode: z.string() }))
          .query(async ({ input }) => await Shipping.calculateShippingCost(input.zipCode)),
      }),
      paymentMethods: router({
        list: publicProcedure.query(async () => await AdminPaymentMethods.listPaymentMethods()),
        listFoodCardBrands: publicProcedure.query(async () => await AdminPaymentMethods.listFoodCardBrands()),
      }),
      packages: router({
        list: publicProcedure.query(async () => await Packages.getAllPackages()),
        getById: publicProcedure
          .input(z.object({ id: z.number() }))
          .query(async ({ input }) => await Packages.getPackageWithOptions(input.id)),
      }),
    }),
  }),

  // 3. ROTAS PROTEGIDAS (AUTH)
  auth: router({
    me: protectedProcedure.query(({ ctx }) => ctx.user),
    login: publicProcedure
      .input(z.object({ email: z.string().email(), password: z.string() }))
      .mutation(async ({ input, ctx }) => {
        const user = await AuthPassword.validateLogin(input.email, input.password);
        const sessionToken = await sdk.createSessionToken(user.openId, {
          name: user.name || "",
          expiresInMs: ONE_YEAR_MS,
        });
        const cookieOptions = getSessionCookieOptions(ctx.req);
        ctx.res.cookie(COOKIE_NAME, sessionToken, { ...cookieOptions, maxAge: ONE_YEAR_MS });
        return user;
      }),
    register: publicProcedure
      .input(z.object({ email: z.string().email(), password: z.string(), name: z.string().optional() }))
      .mutation(async ({ input, ctx }) => {
        const user = await AuthPassword.createUserWithPassword(input.email, input.password, input.name);
        const sessionToken = await sdk.createSessionToken(user.openId, {
          name: user.name || "",
          expiresInMs: ONE_YEAR_MS,
        });
        const cookieOptions = getSessionCookieOptions(ctx.req);
        ctx.res.cookie(COOKIE_NAME, sessionToken, { ...cookieOptions, maxAge: ONE_YEAR_MS });
        return user;
      }),
    logout: protectedProcedure.mutation(({ ctx }) => {
      const cookieOptions = getSessionCookieOptions(ctx.req);
      ctx.res.clearCookie(COOKIE_NAME, { ...cookieOptions, maxAge: -1 });
      return { success: true };
    }),
    
    cart: router({
      getActive: protectedProcedure.query(async ({ ctx }) => await Cart.getActiveCart(ctx.user.id)),
      create: protectedProcedure.mutation(async ({ ctx }) => await Cart.createCart(ctx.user.id)),
      addItem: protectedProcedure.input(ItemDataSchema).mutation(async ({ input, ctx }) => await Cart.addItemToCart(ctx.user.id, input)),
      removeItem: protectedProcedure.input(z.object({ itemId: z.number() })).mutation(async ({ input, ctx }) => await Cart.removeItemFromCart(input.itemId, ctx.user.id)),
      updateQuantity: protectedProcedure.input(z.object({ itemId: z.number(), newQuantity: z.number() })).mutation(async ({ input, ctx }) => await Cart.updateItemQuantity(input.itemId, input.newQuantity, ctx.user.id)),
      recalculate: protectedProcedure.mutation(async ({ ctx }) => await Cart.recalculateCartTotalsForUser(ctx.user.id)),
      checkout: protectedProcedure.input(z.object({ paymentMethod: z.string(), shippingCost: z.number() })).mutation(async ({ input, ctx }) => await Cart.checkoutCart(ctx.user.id, input)),
    }),
    orders: router({
      listMy: protectedProcedure.input(z.object({ status: z.string().optional(), limit: z.number().default(10) }).default({ limit: 10 })).query(async ({ input }) => await AdminOrders.listOrders(input as any)),
      getById: protectedProcedure.input(z.object({ id: z.number() })).query(async ({ input }) => await AdminOrders.getOrderDetails(input.id)),
    }),
    coupons: router({
        validateCoupon: protectedProcedure.input(z.object({ code: z.string(), subtotal: z.number() })).mutation(async ({ input, ctx }) => await Coupon.validateCoupon(input.code, ctx.user.id, input.subtotal)),
        applyCoupon: protectedProcedure.input(z.object({ orderId: z.number(), coupon_id: z.number(), couponCode: z.string(), discountAmount: z.number() })).mutation(async ({ input, ctx }) => await Coupon.applyCouponToOrder(input.orderId, input.coupon_id, input.couponCode, input.discountAmount, ctx.user.id)),
        removeCoupon: protectedProcedure.input(z.object({ orderId: z.number() })).mutation(async ({ input }) => await Coupon.removeCouponFromOrder(input.orderId)),
    }),
    addresses: router({
        list: protectedProcedure.query(async ({ ctx }) => await CustomerAddresses.listAddressesByUserId(ctx.user.id)),
        getDefault: protectedProcedure.query(async ({ ctx }) => await CustomerAddresses.getDefaultAddress(ctx.user.id)),
        fillFromCEP: protectedProcedure.input(z.object({ cep: z.string() })).query(async ({ input }) => (await Shipping.calculateShippingCost(input.cep)) as any),
        create: protectedProcedure.input(z.object({ label: z.string().optional(), recipientName: z.string(), street: z.string(), number: z.string(), complement: z.string().optional().nullable(), neighborhood: z.string(), city: z.string(), state: z.string().length(2), zipCode: z.string(), phone: z.string().optional().nullable(), isDefault: z.boolean().default(false).optional() })).mutation(async ({ input, ctx }) => await CustomerAddresses.createAddress({ ...input, userId: ctx.user.id } as any)),
        update: protectedProcedure.input(z.object({ id: z.number(), label: z.string().optional(), recipientName: z.string().optional(), street: z.string().optional(), number: z.string().optional(), complement: z.string().optional().nullable(), neighborhood: z.string().optional(), city: z.string().optional(), state: z.string().length(2).optional(), zipCode: z.string().optional(), phone: z.string().optional().nullable(), isDefault: z.boolean().optional() })).mutation(async ({ input, ctx }) => { const { id, ...data } = input; return await CustomerAddresses.updateAddress(id, ctx.user.id, data); }),
        delete: protectedProcedure.input(z.object({ id: z.number() })).mutation(async ({ input, ctx }) => await CustomerAddresses.deleteAddress(input.id, ctx.user.id)),
        setDefault: protectedProcedure.input(z.object({ id: z.number() })).mutation(async ({ input, ctx }) => await CustomerAddresses.updateAddress(input.id, ctx.user.id, { isDefault: true })),
    }),
    loyalty: router({
        getBalance: protectedProcedure.query(async ({ ctx }) => { const result = await Loyalty.getUserLoyaltyPoints(ctx.user.id); return { balance: result.loyaltyPoints, totalSpent: result.totalSpent }; }),
        getHistory: protectedProcedure.input(z.object({ limit: z.number().optional().default(20) }).default({ limit: 20 })).query(async ({ input, ctx }) => await Loyalty.getLoyaltyHistory(ctx.user.id, input.limit)),
    }),
  }),

  // 4. ROTAS ADMINISTRATIVAS
  admin: router({
    // 🟢 PACOTES (Agora importado do arquivo separado)
    packages: adminPackagesRouter,

    // ... Outras rotas continuam iguais ...
    dishes: router({
      list: adminProcedure
        .input(z.object({ page: z.number().default(1), perPage: z.number().default(10), search: z.string().nullish(), categoryId: z.number().nullish(), isActive: z.boolean().nullish() }))
        .query(({ input }) => AdminDishes.getPaginatedDishes({ page: input.page, limit: input.perPage, search: input.search ?? undefined, categoryId: input.categoryId ?? undefined, isActive: input.isActive ?? undefined })),
      getById: adminProcedure.input(z.object({ id: z.number() })).query(async ({ input }) => (await AdminDishes.getDishById(input.id)) as any),
      create: adminProcedure.input(DishCreateSchema.extend({ price: z.number(), nutritionalInfo: z.any().optional().nullable() })).mutation(async ({ input }) => await AdminDishes.createDish(input)),
      update: adminProcedure.input(DishUpdateSchema.extend({ price: z.number().optional(), nutritionalInfo: z.any().optional().nullable() })).mutation(async ({ input }) => { const { id, ...data } = input; return await AdminDishes.updateDish(id, data); }),
      delete: adminProcedure.input(z.object({ id: z.number() })).mutation(async ({ input }) => await AdminDishes.deleteDish(input.id)),
      toggleActive: adminProcedure.input(z.object({ id: z.number() })).mutation(async ({ input }) => await AdminDishes.toggleDishActive(input.id)),
      updateImage: adminProcedure.input(z.object({ id: z.number(), imageUrl: z.string().nullable() })).mutation(async ({ input }) => await AdminDishes.updateDish(input.id, { imageUrl: input.imageUrl })),
      listCategories: adminProcedure.query(async () => await AdminDishes.getLocalCategories()),
      createCategory: adminProcedure.input(z.object({ name: z.string() })).mutation(async ({ input }) => await AdminDishes.createLocalCategory(input.name)),
    }),

    sizes: router({
        list: adminProcedure.query(async () => await AdminSizes.getAllDishSizes()),
        getAccompanimentGroups: adminProcedure.query(async () => await AdminSizes.getSizeAccompanimentGroupsWithOptions()),
        create: adminProcedure.input(z.object({ name: z.string(), weight: z.string().optional().nullable(), priceModifier: z.number(), noAccompanimentsMessage: z.string().optional().nullable(), noMessage: z.string().optional().nullable() })).mutation(async ({ input }) => await AdminSizes.createDishSize(input)),
        delete: adminProcedure.input(z.object({ id: z.number() })).mutation(async ({ input }) => await AdminSizes.deleteDishSize(input.id)),
        addAccompanimentGroup: adminProcedure.input(z.object({ sizeId: z.number(), groupId: z.number(), isRequired: z.boolean().optional() })).mutation(async ({ input }) => await AdminSizes.linkAccompanimentToSize({ sizeId: input.sizeId, groupId: input.groupId, isRequired: input.isRequired })),
        removeAccompanimentGroup: adminProcedure.input(z.object({ sizeId: z.number(), groupId: z.number() })).mutation(async ({ input }) => await AdminSizes.unlinkAccompanimentFromSize(input.sizeId, input.groupId)),
    }),
    
    accompaniments: router({
        groups: router({
            list: adminProcedure.query(async () => await AdminSizes.getAllAccompanimentGroups()),
            create: adminProcedure.input(z.object({ name: z.string(), description: z.string().optional(), maxSelection: z.number().optional() })).mutation(async ({ input }) => await AdminSizes.createAccompanimentGroup(input)),
            delete: adminProcedure.input(z.object({ id: z.number() })).mutation(async ({ input }) => await AdminSizes.deleteAccompanimentGroup(input.id)),
        }),
        options: router({
            list: adminProcedure.input(z.object({ groupId: z.number() })).query(async ({ input }) => await AdminSizes.getAccompanimentOptionsByGroup(input.groupId)),
            create: adminProcedure.input(z.object({ groupId: z.number(), name: z.string(), priceModifier: z.number() })).mutation(async ({ input }) => await AdminSizes.createAccompanimentOption(input)),
            delete: adminProcedure.input(z.object({ id: z.number() })).mutation(async ({ input }) => await AdminSizes.deleteAccompanimentOption(input.id)),
        }),
    }),
    
    orders: router({
        list: adminProcedure.input(z.object({ page: z.number().default(1), limit: z.number().default(10), search: z.string().optional(), status: z.custom<OrderStatus>().optional() })).query(async ({ input }) => await AdminOrders.listOrders(input)),
